Ngesizini edlule baphelela endaweni yesi - 12 namaphuzu awu - 34 .
" Umdlalo wokugcina neStellenbosch ubunzima kakhulu .
Izitayela zethu zokudlala bezishayisana .
Thina besilibamba ibhola futhi sizama ukushaya amagoli kodwa bekusobala ukuthi bona bebezele iphuzu .
Bebezihlalele emuva bese bezama ukusizuma ngejubane , uma bethola ibhola , " kusho uNcikazi .
" Bekulukhuni ukudiliza udonga abalwakhe emuva .
Sizamile ukubahlasela ezinhlangothini , sazama nokudlala ibhola eliphezulu kodwa kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya .
Ngingasho kodwa ukuthi sidlale kahle yize noma sigcine sihlulekile ukuthola igoli .
Ngiyaziqhenya ngabadlali nangendlela abazinikele ngayo .
Besinabadlali abawu - 13 kuphela abebekulungele ukudlala , abanye sibafake belimele .
Ngingabala uMakhubela ( Ntsako ) , uSibisi ( Nkosinathi ) , uMtshali ( Lindokuhle ) noMathiane ( Matome ) .
" Uma unabadlali abenza konke okusemandleni ukuthi bangene enkundleni noma bengeluleme kahle , kukhombisa ukuthi iqembu linekusasa elihle .
Ngiyaziqhenya kakhulu ngala badlali .
Ngifisa ukuthi leli qembu liqhubeke lidlondlobale .
" Abafana Bes'thende bebedinga ukuthi bawunqobe umdlalo wokugcina ukuze bazibeke ethubeni elihle lokuqeda endaweni yesithathu , obekuzoholela ekutheni babeyingxenye yomqhudelwano weCaf Confederation Cup .
Ukudlala kwabo ngokulingana kwenze bahluleka ukudlula i - Orlando Pirates , egcine inamaphuzu awu - 50 .
Noma kunjalo uNcikazi uyaziqhenya ngokuthi bakwazile ukwephula irekhodi leqembu abalenza ngesizini ka - 2008 / 9 , beqeda endaweni yesihlanu namaphuzu awu - 46 , izintambo zisaphethwe nguManqoba Mngqithi .
Okunye okumhlaba umxhwele uNcikazi ukubona abadlali bakhe bephakanyiswa ohlwini lwabadlali abebesethubeni lokuwina izindondo kumaPSL Awards , nokubona abanye bebizelwa emaqenjini esizwe .
" Kuyangithokozisa ukuthi uSifiso ( Mlungwana ) usethubeni lokungena eqenjini lama - Olympics .

Maningi amarekhodi esiwaphulile kule sizini .
Kuningi kakhulu okuhle esikwenzile .

Ukuba kwakukhona owangibhulela kusaqala isizini , wangitshela ukuthi sizoqeda endaweni yesine ngangizojabula kabi .
Angifuni ukungeneliseki ngesikwenzile njengoba isiphelile isizini .

Sekuphenduka usiko ukuphuma kumuncu kwezintandokazi kwiMadrid
IQEMBU elikhulu kunawo wonke eSpain iReal Madrid lisaqhubeka nomlando walo wokuphetha kabi ubudlelwano nabadlali abayizintandokazi kubalandeli bayo .
Kuleli sonto zishaqise abaningi izindaba zokushiya kukakaputeni weminyaka kwiLos Blancos , uSergio Ramos , okuvele ukuthi ngeke ayithole inkontileka entsha kuleli qembu .
Izolo uRamos evalelisa eqenjini asehlale kulo iminyaka engu - 16 , uthe naye kumethusile uma etshelwa ukuthi inkontileka ebibekwe yiMadrid ukuthi ayisayine , ibiphelelwa yisikhathi .
" Into yokuqala engifisa ukuyisho ukuthi bengingafuni ukushiya .
Bengisafuna ukuhlala kwiMadrid .
Besinezingxoxo zokuthi kwelulwe inkontileka yami kodwa zaphazamiseka ngenxa yeCovid - 19 .
Bezilokhu zishintsha izinto ebesivumelana ngazo kodwa abakaze bangitshele ukuthi ngizophelelwa yisikhathi sokusayina inkontileka entsha , " kuchaza uRamos .
URamos ( 35 ) , uthe iMadrid imnikeze inkontileka yonyaka owodwa ehambisana nokuncishiselwa umholo .
Uthe ubenganankinga nokuncipha komholo kodwa ubefisa kube yinkontileka yeminyaka emibili ukuze ezokhululeka benomndeni wakhe .
Iphephandaba laseMadrid , iMarca libika ukuthi leli qembu lihoxise inkontileka uRamos esevumile ukuyisayina .
URamos unqobe izindebe eziwu - 22 eminyakeni ayidlalele iMadrid .
Kulezo zindebe kubalwa ama - UEFA Champions League amane , izicoco zeLa Liga ezinhlanu , amaClub World Cup amane kanye nezinkomishi ezimbili zeCopa Del Rey .
Ushiya leli qembu nje , seliqala ukuzakhela umlando ngokuphetha kabi ubudlelwano balo nabadlali abayizintandokazi kubalandeli beqembu .
Ngo - 2018 kushiye cishe umdlali omkhulu kunabo bonke emlandweni waleli qembu , uChristiano Ronaldo , okwathusa abaningi ukuhamba kwakhe kwazise uhambe esayidabula inethi .
URonaldo uhambe kwiMadrid eshaye amagoli awu - 451 emdlalweni ewu - 438 .
Ufike kwiSeria A washaya amagoli awu - 21 kwisizini yakhe yokuqala kanti nakule sizini ephelelile ushaye into ecokeme elibasela izikhawu eziwu - 29 ibhola enethini .
IMadrid ibiwadinga amagoli akhe kule sizini kwazise isishwebe kancane isicoco seligi kanti nakwiChampions League , kwacacela ngisho ingane incane ukuthi leli qembu ebeliphekwa wuZinadine Zidane , lishoda ngamagoli phambili .
Sisakhuluma ngamagoli , omunye umdlali olaxazwe yiMadrid kule sizini nguGareth Bale ( 31 ) , ovutha engabaselwe emdlalweni yeEuro eqhubekayo njengamanje .
Lo mdlali ube nobudlelwano obubi noZidane owamfaka ohlwini lwabadlali afisa ukubadayisa , ukuze athole imali yokuthenga abadlali abasha .
IMadrid yavimba isifiso sikaBale sokuyodlala eqenjini laseChina iJiangsu Suning ngo - 2019 , yajike yambolekisa kwiTottenham Hotspur kule sizini ephelile kulandela isikhathi ekhuhla ibhentshi .
Ngasemaphethelweni e - English Premier League , uBale ubengomunye wabadlali abayingozi phambi kwepali , okuyifomu aqhubeke phezu kwayo kwi - Euro .
Umqeqeshi okhuza ibuya kwiReal Madrid uCarlo Ancelotti , usheshe waphumela obala wathi uzomdinga uBale ngesizini ezayo , usezinhlelweni zakhe .
Ngenxa yobudlelwano obungebuhle phakathi kwabaphathi beqembu noBale akukacaci ukuthi lo mdlali uzimisele ngani ngesizini entsha .
Omunye umdlali ohambe kamuncu kuleli qembu nguMesut Ozil .
Lo mdlali kwethusa abaningi ukuvela kwezindaba zokuthi usejoyina i - Arsenal .
U - Ozil wajoyina Ezimhlophe ngo - 2010 esuka kwiWerder Bremen .
Ngesikhathi eshiya ngo - 2013 , uRonaldo wazwakalisa ukungenami ngokudayiswa kwakhe : " Ungenze ngaba wumdlali ongcono .
Uma udlala nabadlali abaseqopheleni eliphezulu nawe liyakhuphuka izinga lakhoU - Ozil uhambe kwi - Madrid enama - assist awu - 61 kuyo yonke imidlalo ayidlalile kumasizini amathathu nokumenze wahamba esebizwa ngenkosi yama - assist .
IMadrid ibukhombisile ubunya nakonozinti .
Icishe ibe ngcono indlela okwahamba ngayo owayengukapteni u - Iker Cassilas kwazise wayesenamaphutha epalini futhi emmise kabi uDiego Lopes ngaphambi kokuthi leli qembu lisayinise uKeylor Navas .
UNavas washaya ingcwenga eminyakeni ayichithe kwiMadrid edla izicoco ezintathu ze - Eufa Champions League nesicoco esidowa seLa Liga kodwa naye washaywa ngesithende kalula sekufike unozinti omusha .
UNavas usedlalela iPSG eFrance .
Ekhuluma ngoMashi ngokudayiswa kwakhe wathi : " kunezinto ezenzeka engingazi zadalwa yini kodwa zenzeka .
Ngiyaye ngizame ukucabanga ngokuhle kuphela .
Ngikhumbula okuhle kuphela ngesikhathi sami noZidane , owayengilwela isikhathi esiningi futhi ngiyambonga ngokungethemba .
" IDiski Yomhlaba
Umqeqeshi weBucs usevivela eyamaqoqo yeCaf
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUKUBUYA kwabadlali ekulimaleni kususe ingcindezi kumqeqeshi we - Orlando Pirates , uJosef Zinnbauer obhekene nomthwalo wokwenza kahle emiqhudelwaneni emithathu .
EZimnyama ezibhaxabule iChippa United ngo - 3 - 0 koweligi ngempelasonto eNelson Mandela Bay Stadium , eGqeberha , ngoLwesithathu , zizodlala owukuqala wamaqoqo eCaf Confederation Cup ne - ES Setif yase - Algeria ngo - 9 ebusuku , e - Ohene Djan Sports Stadium , eGhana .
KuGroup A , kukhona ne - Al - Ahly Benghazi yaseLibya ne - Enyimba yaseNigeria .
NgoLwesithathu kuMashi 17 , zizokwamukela i - Enyimba , e - Orlando Stadium .
Ngemuva kwalo mdlalo , zizobhekana neKaizer Chiefs koweDStv Premiership .
Leli qembu libuye lazibekisela indawo kuma - quarterfinal eNedbank Cup .
Ebuzwa uZinnbauer ukuthi kakumethusi yini ukudlala emiqhudelwaneni emithathu , uthe : " Kuzoba nzima kodwa okungijabulisayo wukubuya kwabadlali ekulimaleni .
Emasontweni edlule , bekungiphathisa ngekhanda ukushoda kwesikwati sami .
Benza kahle kakhulu oTshegofatso Mabasa , Gabadinho Mhango , Sam ( Bongani ) nabanye .
Nokho kumele sibanike isikhathi .
Kuhlale kuyinto ethokozisayo ukubona abadlali bebanga ijezi .
Ukuphelela kwesikwati sami kungenza ngikwazi ukulungiselela kahle yomithathu le miqhudelwano .
Ukudlala kule miqhudelwano kuzogqugquzela nabadlali bami .
" Lo mqeqeshi ukubeke kwacaca ukuthi ukudlala kahle noma kabi kwezimbangi zakhe , iSundowns neChiefs kwiCaf Champions League akumfaki ngcindezi .
" Angibheki amanye amaqembu ukuthi adlala kanjani , okubalulekile kimina yiqembu lami .
Kuyajabulisa ukubona iqembu lakuleli linqoba emidlalweni yase - Afrika .
Ukwenza kahle e - Afrika , kwenza izwe lizethembe .
Abadlali bathole amava azosiza nakwiligi yakuleli , " kusho uZinnbauer .
Emdlalweni wangempelasonto , eZimnyama bezinqoba okwesithathu kulandelana .
Zinyukele endaweni yesibili kwi - log ngamaphuzu awu - 35 , emuva kwemidlalo ewu - 20 .
Sezisele ngephuzu elilodwa kwiSundowns enemidlalo ewu - 16 .
Mayelana nomdlalo weChippa , uZinnbauer uncome iqembu lakhe ngokudlala kahle .
" Kuyangijabulisa ukunqoba okwesithathu kulandelana nokuthola amaphuzu aphelele .
Udonga lwami lwasemuva lwenze kahle kakhulu .
UMakaringe ( Fortune ) noHotto ( Deon ) baphinde babhakuzisa inethi .
Kungijabulisile nokuthola kukaBen Motshwari igoli .
" Ngiyambongela ngokubizwa kwiBafana Bafana , kumfanele ukudlala eqenjini lesizwe .
Kula masonto edlule udlale kahle kakhulu .
Kuyajabulisa ukushaya kwakhe igoli kungakapheli sikhathi esingakanani ebizwe kwelesizwe .
" UDan " Dance " Malesela ocija amaChilli Boys , uthe : " Uma sizoqhubeka namaphutha anjena , impilo yethu izoba nzima .
Ukuba siye ekhefini sibambene ngeqanda nePirates bewungeke umdlalo uphele ngalo mphumela .
Kuningi okungahambanga kahle kulo mdlalo , kunabadlali abebecashile , bengawenzi umsebenzi wabo . "
UMngqithi uphume nesifundo i - Al Ahly ibawashisa ijezi
UKUKHISHWA kwiCAF Champions League kumshiye nesifundo esibuhlungu umqeqeshi weMamelodi Sundowns , uManqoba Mngqithi , okungenzeka ashintshe indlela abawuhlelela ngayo lo mqhudelwano ngesizini ezayo .
ISundowns idlale ngokulingana ngo - 1 - 1 ne - Al Ahly yase - Egypt emlenzeni wesibili kuma - quarterfinal ePitoli ngoMgqibelo ntambama .
Nokho ihlulwe ngo - 3 - 1 uma sekuhlanganiswa imiphumela yemilenze yomibili .
Kowokuqala e - Egypt , AmaBrazilians aguqiswe ngezikaPitso Mosimane ngo - 2 - 0 .
Sekungokwesithathu iminyaka ilandelana iSundowns iphuma kuma - quarterfinal eChampions League .
UMngqithi uthe isifundo abaphume naso ngesokuthi ukudlala ekuhambeni kuqala , okutholakala ngokuqeda phezulu eqoqweni , akusebenzi .
I - Sundowns ihlala ilwela ukuqeda eqhulwini ukuze izogwema ezinye izinkunzi kuma - quarterfinal kwazise awaqhathwa wodwa amaqembu aqede phezulu emaqoqweni .
" Mhlawumbe ukuqeda endaweni yesibili yikhona okulungile ngoba uma udlala owomlenze wokuqala ekhaya , kuba nzima ekuhambeni .
Uma ukhumbula sidlala ne - Ahly sayihlula emdlalweni wokuqala lapha , sashaya amagoli ayisihlanu .
Kodwa sesidlala ngakubo sathwala kanzima ukubehlula .
Kule midlalo elandelanayo kubukeka sengathi unethuba lokudlulela phambili uma uqala ekhaya .
Uma ubheka siqede phezulu eqoqweni kodwa siphumile , " kusho uMngqithi " Mhlawumbe kuthumela umyalezo wokuthi le mpi yokuqeda phezulu eqoqweni ukuze uzodlala ekuhambeni kuqala , ayinazithelo .
Mhlawumbe kufanele ulwele ukudlala ekhaya kuqala lapho kungekho zinto eziningi okufanele uzibheke ezingenzeka .
Ulwela ukuwina umdlalo ophambi kwakho .
Kolandelayo usulwela ukungaphunyukwa onakho .
ISimba ishaye amagoli amathathu , izamile .
Kodwa ngebhadi ngoba iChiefs yenza kahle ekhaya , iphumelele ukudlulela phambili .
Yinto okufanele siyifunde ngoba silokhu sibhekane nenkinga efanayo , " kusho yena .
Ukuwashiswa ijezi kuma - quarterfinal kweSundowns kusho ukuthi isiyoze ibuyele kwiChampions League ngesizini ezayo kwazise akubukeki kukhona iqembu elizoyiphazamisa ekutheni iwine iligi yeDStv Premiership .
Mayelana nendlela abaphume ngayo , uMngqithi uthe : " Besazi ukuthi ngeke kube lula .
Kodwa sizenzele thina ubunzima ngokungenelwa yigoli kade kuyikhona .
Sizame kanzima ukubacindezela kodwa bebehlezi emuva .
Angibasoli abadlali , ngicabanga ukuthi bakwenze konke okusemandleni kodwa osukwini sihlulekile ukuthola imiphumela ebesiyifuna .
Injalo iChampions League , ungenza konke kodwa kwesinye isikhathi kube nzima ukugqobhoza iqembu elihlezi emuva . "
UMngqithi ufuna bazibhalele owabo umlando kowe - Al Ahly
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEITHIMBA labaqeqeshi leMamelodi Sundowns lizimisele ngokuqopha owalo umlando uma selibhekene ne - Al Ahly kowomlenze wesibili wama - quarterfinal eCaf Champions League kusasa eLucas Moripe Stadium ngo - 3 ntambama .
Lokhu kuvezwe oliholayo , uManqoba Mngqithi , kwabezindaba izolo ekuseni .
UMngqithi uthe abafuni ukubambelela ekutheni iSundowns yabhudluza i - Al Ahly ngo - 5 - 0 ePitoli kumasizini adlule .
Uthe konke lokho sekuwumlando .
Ngaleso sikhathi uMngqithi wayeyiphini likaPitso Mosimane kumaBrazilians .
Manje uMosimane usewumqeqeshi we - Al Ahly .
AmaBrazillians abhekene nomqansa wokwehlula amaRed Devils ase - Egypt ngo - 3 - 0 ukuze ezodlulela kowandulela owamanqamu kulo mqhudelwano .
Ngempelasonto edlule emlenzeni wokuqala , eCairo , ashaywa ngo - 2 - 0 .
" Umlando wokushaya i - Al Ahly ngamagoli amahlanu ngeke usisize ngalutho .
Kuningi osekwashintsha kuwona womabili amaqembu , kusukela kubadlali kuya kubaqeqeshi .
I - Sundowns inabadlali nethimba labaqeqeshi abasezingeni eliphezulu , abafuna ukuzakhela owabo umlando .
" Sigqugquzelwa yimpumelelo esiyithole sindawonye , efana nesibalo samagoli esiwashaye kwiChampions League nemidlalo esiyinqobile .
Siyiqembu elinentshisekelo yokunqoba , elinikana ibhola ngobuchule , elikwazi ukuhlasela nelingongcweti ekuphazamiseni izinhlelo zezitha zokuhlasela .
Ubufakazi balokhu yisibalo esincane samagoli asingenele .
Sihlale sikhonya enkundleni .
Umdlalo weCape Town City kuphela esahluleka ukwenza lokhu kuwo .
" Nginesiqiniseko sokuthi iSundowns kuphela engakwazi ukubuya , ishaye i - Al Ahly , sesike sakwenza lokho .
Ngeke kuthi ngoba nakhu sesidlala ne - Al Ahly siqale singabaze ikhono labadlali nempumelelo yethu .
Yebo , kuzoba nzima kodwa maningi amathuba okunqoba , " kusho uMngqithi .
Uqhube wathi kumele bagweme amaphutha abaqhatha nenduku emdlalweni odlule .
" Owawubona umlenze wokuqala uzokutshela ukuthi ubani owakha amathuba amaningi phakathi kwiSundowns ne - Al Ahly .
Njengoba ngike ngasho phambilini , sashaywa amaphutha ethu , kwaba yishwa nje ukuthi kasishayanga negoli elilodwa .
Ngabe kukhulunywa okunye ukube ibhola likaMotupa ( Aubrey ) kalishayanga ipali .
Kukhona amanye amabili esawayeka ngekhanda kuhlanganisa nilekaMosa ( Lebusa ) .
Kunamanye esasibazumile kuwo esawayeka .
" E - Egypt bamangala sihlasela ngaleya ndlela , babezitshela ukuthi sizohlala emuva silinde bona .
Asazi , mhlawumbe kulokhu bazohlala emuva .
Ibhola liyinkinga , singalishaya khona kunjalo igoli .
Nathi uma sizokhipha konke , singaqapheli singazifaka enkingeni .
" Izindaba ezizokwehla kamtoti kubalandeli bamaBrazillians ngezokubuya ekulimaleni kukaThemba " Mshishi " Zwane .
" Ngokombiko wodokotela , isimo sakhe sihle kakhulu .
Sekuphele isikhashana eziqeqesha nathi , nayizolo ejimini ( ngoLwesithathu ) wenze kahle kakhulu .
Uhlale ekhonya ngaso sonke isikhathi , " kusho uMngqithi .
UBaloyi ukhala esonozinti eMzansi
ZAKHELE XABAU - BRIAN " Spiderman " Baloyi , owayengunozinti weBafana Bafana , ubona ukuthathwa konozinti bangaphandle kungayixazulula inkinga yepali eqenjini lesizwe .
UBaloyi , ongomunye wonozinti abebengaconsi phansi kubalandeli baseMzansi eminyakeni edlule , ubekhuluma ngesikhathi kwethulwa ngokusemthethweni umqhudelwano , iHollywood Bets U / 15 Siyakhula Cup eMhlanga , eThekwini , ngeledlule .
Kulo mqhudelwano kuzodlala amaqembu angu - 16 aseThekwini ngoJulayi 3 - 4 ezinkundleni ezingaphandle kwaseMoses Mabhida Stadium , iHollywood Bets ibambisene naMaZulu Community Trust neLa Liga .
UBaloyi uthe ukuvimbisa onozinti bangaphandle kwamaqembu eDStv Premiership yikhona okudala inkinga uma sekufanele kuqokwe ozovimbela iBafana .
Le nkinga ikhalise nomqeqeshi , uMolefi Ntseki , esaqeqesha iBafana , wagcina encenga uCyril Chibwe waseZambia ogcine eqoke iChipolopolo .
Okwamanje kwiBafana kuvimba uRonwen Williams weSuperSport United .
" Lena yinkinga esesibe nayo iminyaka eminingi .
Kodwa njengenjwayelo , eMzansi silinda inkinga ikhule .
Inkinga ebesihlala sinayo bekuhlala kungeyabagadli ngenxa yokuthi abaphezulu kade bevela eZambia , Zimbabwe naseNigeria .
Manje amaqembu amakhulu , ngisho amancane nadlala kwiGladAfrica Championship , adlalisa abagadli bangaphandle okungeyona into embi , " kusho uBaloyi .
" Eminyakeni embalwa edlule sekushintshile konozinti .
Amaqembu angaphezu kwesigamu kwiPremiership avimbisa onozinti bangaphandle .
I - Sundowns eminyakeni emine kuya kweyisihlanu kade ishaya ngonozinti abathathu noma abane bangaphandle .
Ngakho uma unamaqembu amathathu amakhulu evimbisa onozinti bangaphandle , kudlulele kwiMaritzburg United neChippa namanye , uzoba nenkinga .
" Ukuncintelwa ijezi konozinti , okudala ukwehla kwezinga kwabaseqenjini lesizwe , akuyona inkinga yaseMzansi kuphela .
I - Egypt iwubuyisile umthetho ovimbela onozinti bangaphandle ukuthi badlale kumaligi akhona .
" E - Egypt abanawo lo mthetho mahhala .
Kwesinye isikhathi kufanele sizibeke phambili siyizwe noma siyiligi .
Kufanele siwushaye nathi lo mthetho ?
Mhlawumbe cha .
Okufanele sikwenze wukukhulisa abethu onozinti .
Kufanele sisheshe kakhulu ngoba isizukulwane sika - Itu ( Itumeleng Khune ) sesiyashabalala .
Kufanele siyinake indaba yonozinti .
Ngebhadi isikhathi sesihambile .
Esingakuqala manje kungalunga emuva kweminyaka eyisihlanu kuya kwengu - 10 , " kusho uBaloyi .
" Ngicabanga ukuthi kufanele siyicabange eyokuthatha onozinti bangaphandle , abangakaze bawavimbele amazwe abo kodwa abaqeqeshwe bakhuliswa kahle bekhula .
Lokhu kungaba yisixazululo sesikhashana kodwa sibe nalo uhlelo lokukhulisa abethu .
Lena yinkinga ongekho umuntu ofuna ukukhuluma ngayo emaqenjini nakwelesizwe .
Amaqembu avele anqamulele ngokulanda unozinti wangaphandle , " kuphetha uBaloyi .
Inzukazikeyi ngesicoco seGladAfrica
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEIPREMIER Soccer League ( PSL ) seyithole izinsongo zokusatshiswa ngokuthi luzofakwa enkantolo udaba lombango wesicoco seGladAfrica Championship .
Kuyiwe emidlalweni yokugcina kulesi sigaba kukhulunywa kakhulu .
Amaqembu abethinteka kulokhu kukhuluma iRoyal AM , izolo ebambane ngo - 1 - 1 neCape Town All Stars neSekhukhune edlule ngehubo lika - 3 - 1 kwiJDR .
ISekhukhune sifake isikhalo kwiPSL Resolution Chamber ( DRC ) , sikhononda ngokungadlalisi kwePolokwane City abadlali abahlanu abangaphansi kweminyaka engu - 23 .
IDRC ibe seyiphuca iPolokwane City amaphuzu amathathu .
Nokho iSekhukhune idlulisele lesi sinqumo kumehluleli , obe esesinika amaphuzu amathathu .
Izolo iPSL ikhiphe isitatimende ivezela abezindaba ukuthi alikho iqembu elizonikezwa indebe .
Ngaphandle kwendebe okubangwayo wukuthi iqembu elizoqeda phezulu lizokhuphukela kwiDStv Premiership .
" Kuyijoka leligi ukwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi iyayalwa futhi ikhipha isinqumo ngokushesha esizokwanelisa izinhlangothi zonke .
Njengoba lolu daba lusasezithebeni , kuwumbono ophusile ukuthi kubambezeleke ukunikezelwa kwenkomishi .
IPSL iyazibophezela ngokuthi lolu daba izoluxazulula ngokushesha , " sifundeka kanjena lesi sitatimende .
Ngokwe - log yeGladAfrika , iRoyal isonge iphezulu ngamaphuzu awu - 51 , emidlalweni ewu - 30 .
ISekhukhune siqede sikweyesibili ngamaphuzu awu - 50 .
Emdlalweni , obuseChatsworth Stadium , eThekwini , i - All Stars , iyona ebone imbobo yepali ngegoli elishaywe uWaseem Isaacs ngomzuzu ka - 79 .
EleRoyal lishaywe uSamuel Manganyi seliyozilahla kunina .
Kube iphenathi kade kudlaliswe kabi uWandile Mabuza .
Iqembu elizogcina liqeda endaweni yesibili lizodlala kweyokuhlunga nalelo elisendaweni yesithathu .
Okwamanje indawo yesithathu ibanjwe iRichards Bay FC ngamaphuzu awu - 49 .
La maqembu azobhekana nelizoqeda endaweni ka - 15 kwiDStv Premiership , kubangwa khona ukukhuphukela esigabeni esiphezulu .

IChiefs izoshintsha isikimu koweDiski Challenge
STHEMBISO NGOBESEUZOSHINTSHA ukwenza umqeqeshi weKaizer Chiefs kwiDStv Diski Challenge , u - Arthur Zwane , uma sebebhekene neTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ngempelasonto .
Umdlalo ungeSonto ngo - 9 .
30 ekuseni eLucas Moripe Stadium , ePitoli .
UZwane uveze ukuthi kulo mdlalo uzoshaya ngabadlali abangajwayele ukuthola isikimu .
Ukhuluma kanjena nje , ngempelasonto iqembu lakhe libe ngelokuqala ukuzibekisela indawo emidlalweni eyandulela owamanqamu kwiDiski Challenge Rewired .
Lokhu abafana beChiefs bakwenze ngemuva kokuxebula ngo 3 - 1 iSwallows FC .
KwiGroup B , iChiefs ihlezi esicongweni se - log yeDiski ngamaphuzu angu - 15 emidlalweni eyisithupha .
Amaqembu asebanga indawo yesibili yi - Orlando Pirates neMamelodi Sundwons nabo abazobhekana ngeSonto ngo - 12:00 PM , khona eLucas Moripe .
UZwane uthe ujabule kakhulu ngokuthi iqembu lakhe likwazile ukuzibekisela indawo emidlalweni eyandulela owamanqamu .
" Abadlali bami kubafanele lokhu .
Basebenze ngokukhulu ukuzikhandla ukuze babe kule ndawo abakuyo njengamanje .
Bathembisa ukuthi bafuna ukufinyelela emdlalweni wamanqamu , ukuze banqobele iqembu , nabo uqobo lwabo ngokunjalo nabalandeli .
" Manje ngeke sisabheka emuva .
Sihamba ngomgudu ofanele futhi sesiwutholile nomgqigqo wethu .
Nokuzethemba kukhulu kakhulu manje , " usho kanje uZwane , obuye abe ngumsizi kaGavin Hunt eqenjini elikhulu lamaKhosi .
Le nkakha yeChiefs , iphawule ngomdlalo wabo wokugcina wamaqoqo , abazowudlala neTshakuma .
Ithe : " Kulo mdlalo wethu wokugcina neTTM sizonikeza abafana abancane ithuba lokuthi badlale , okuyinto ezobasiza ekutheni bathole isipiliyoni .
Lokhu kuyingxenye yethu yokulungisela isizini ezayo .
" Kodwa - ke uma sesidlala emdlalweni owandulela owamanqamu bazobuya bonke abadlali abajwayele ukudlala .
Sizoba neqembu eliqinile uma sesibhekene nanoma ngubani kowandulela owamanqamu .
" Imidlalo yeDStv Diski Challenge yangempelasonto : NgoMgqibelo - Ngo - 10:00 AM : AmaZulu FC v Cape Town City ( King Zwelithini Stadium ) ; Maritzburg United v TS Galaxy ( Harry Gwala Stadium ) ; Stellenbosch FC v Chippa United ( Idas Valley ) ; Lamontville Golden Arrows v Supersport United ( Sugar Ray Xulu Stadium ) ; Bloemfontein Celtic v Baroka FC ( Dr Petrus Molemela Stadium ) ;
Swallows FC v Black Leopards ( Dobsonville Stadium ) .
NgeSonto - Ngo - 9 : 30am : Tshakuma Tsha Madzivhandila v Kaizer Chiefs ( Lucas Moripe Stadium ) .
Ngo - 12:00 PM : Mamelodi Sundowns v Orlando Pirates ( Lucas Moripe Stadium ) .
Isikhulu sicasukile ngabashiywe ngaphandle kwiBafana
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUDINWE uyaveva umnikazi weCape Town City , uJohn Comitis , ngokushiywa ngaphandle eqenjini lesizwe kwezinsika zeqembu lakhe , uThabo Nodada noMduduzi Mdantsane .
Ngesonto eledlule , umqeqeshi weBafana Bafana , uMolefi Ntseki , umemezele iqembu labadlali abawu - 26 elizobhekana neGhana neSudan kweyokuhlungela i - Africa Cup of Nations ( Afcon ) ezoba eCameroon ngonyaka ozayo .
OweGhana uzoba ngoMashi 25 eFNB Stadium , kuthi oweSudan ube ngoMashi 28 ekuhambeni , e - El Hilal Stadium .
Kulesi sikwati bashiywe ngaphandle uNodada noMdatsane phezu kokuba beyishukumisa kwiDStv Primiership .
UCraig Martin kuphela odlala kumaCitizens oqokelwe kuleli qembu .
UMdantsane ulele isithathu kwabahamba phambili ekushayeni amagoli kwiDStv Premiership .
Uvalele ayisishiyagalolunye , walekelela kwamane emidlalweni ewu - 17 ayidlalile .
Nakuba uNodada esashaye amathathu kuphela kodwa ulime indima enkulu kumagoli awu - 29 ashaywe amaCitizens .
Ugcine ukuqokelwa kwelesizwe ngonyaka odlule , elakuleli lidlala owobungani neNamibia .
Ukushiywa ngaphandle kwalaba badlali kususe okukhulu ukukhuluma ngendlela uNtseki aqoka ngayo iqembu lesizwe .
" Ngiphoxekile futhi ngidiniwe ngokushiywa kukaNodada noMdantsane .
Ngihambisana nalabo ababuza ukuthi bashiywe kanjani ngaphandle laba badlali ?
Bakwenze konke laba badlali .
UMdantsane ulele isithathu ngokushaya amagoli , enjalo nje udlala ingcwenga yebhola .
Angisayiphathi - ke ekaNodada , ngiye ngizibuze ukuthi wabadlelani abaqeqeshi beBafana .
Ungomunye wabadlali bezinga eliphezulu kuleli , engikholelwa ukuthi bangalenzela lukhulu iqembu lesizwe , " kubeka uComitis .
UComitis uthe ngala mazwi akaqondile ukudelela uNtseki noma umsebenzi wakhe .
Ube esebongela uMartin ngokuqokelwa kwelesizwe .
" Ngesingami abadlali beqembu elilodwa bangaqokelwa kwelesizwe badlule eshumini , inqobo nje uma bekufanele ukudlala kulo .
Ngimfisela inhlanhla uMartin , engathi naseqenjini lesizwe angenza kahle njengoba enza kithina .
Ungomunye wabadlali abanekusasa elihle .
Nathi kwiCity sisabheke lukhulu kuyena ukusisiza ekufezeni izifiso zathu zale sizini .
" Umqeqeshi weTS Galaxy , u - Owen Da Gama , ungomunye ocashunwe ebuza ukuthi ushiywe kanjani uMdantsane .
Uthe ukube ungumqeqeshi weBafana , lo mdlali oyibamba kuthule umoya esiswini , ubezoba endaweni yokuqala ohlwini lwabadlali abezobaqokela kwelesizwe .
Umqeqeshi waMaZulu FC , uBenni McCarthy , ubuziwe ngalokhu kwisithangami nabezindaba izolo lapho abemukela umklomelo womqeqeshi ovelele .
Uthe ubazi kahle ubuhlungu bokuzimisela bese ungaqokelwa kwelesizwe , kuvele kubizwe abantu abebengadlali .
Uthe ukholelwa ukuthi uThabo Nodada noMduduzi Mdantsane beCape Town City bebekufanele ukubizelwa kwiBafana Bafana .
UNurkovic nesixwayiso kozakwabo ngoweCAF
UMGADLI weKaizer Chiefs , uSamir Nurkovic , uxwayisa ngenjabulo eyadlulele ekubeni ungakapheli umsebenzi obamele kwiCAF Champions League .
U - Nurkovic ushaye igoli okube yilona lodwa lomdlalo ngesikhathi iChiefs ibhekene neWydad Casablanca kowomlenze wokuqala owandulela owamanqamu weCAF Champions League eMorocco , ngempelasonto .
Umdlalo womlenze wesibili uzoba seFNB Stadium , eNasrec , ngoMgqibelo ngo - 6 ebusuku .
Amakhosi adinga okungenani ukudlala ngokulingana ukuze ezodlulela kowamanqamu .
" Kube wumsebenzi omuhle weqembu lonke .
Ngijabule kakhulu ngokufaka isandla kulokhu kuwina kodwa asikwazi ukuqhubeka nokujabula ngoba kuseyisikhathi sekhefu .
Ngesonto elizayo sizodlala nabo ekhaya futhi .
Kufanele senze isiqiniseko sokuthi siyawuwina nalowo mdlalo , " kusho uNurkovic .
Ngokuwina , iChiefs izibeke ethubeni lokudlala owamanqamu weCAF Champions League nokungaba okokuqala emlandweni wayo phezu kokuba iyiqembu lokuqala eMzansi eladlala kulo mqhudelwano .
Umqeqeshi , u - Arthur Zwane , uthe iqhinga labo lokuhlala emuva libasebenzele .
" Kade sizosebenza lapha eMorocco , futhi senza lokho ngqo .
Siyakholwa wukuthi besingenza kangcono kodwa besidlala nelinye lamaqembu amakhulu ezwenikazi .
Basifake ingcindezi imizuzu engu - 90 yonke kodwa besihlelekile futhi besikulungele lokho ngoba besazi lapho bemandla ngakhona nangobuthaka babo .
" Sahlela ukuthi sizohlala emuva sivale izikhala , silinde isikhathi esifanele sithole ibhola , sizame ukubalimaza lapho esazi khona ukuthi babuthaka .
Siphumelele ukuthola igoli kodwa besihlele ukushaya amabili uma kwenzeka .
Kodwa siyajabula ngegoli esilishayile .
Manje sizobamukela ekhaya eJohannesburg .
Siyazi ukuthi akukapheli .
Sisanemizuzu engu - 90 okufanele siyidlale ezoba nzima ngoba bazoza ngakho konke .
Bazofuna ukushaya igoli noma amabili .
Kodwa sizobe sibalungele , " kusho uZwane .
Komunye umdlalo womlenze wokuqala owandulela owamanqamu weChampions League , i - Esperance yaseTunisia , ihlulwe ekhaya ngo - 1 - 0 yi - Al Ahly eqeqeshwa nguPitso Mosimane .
Owomlenze wesibili uzoba se - Egypt ngoMgqibelo ngo - 9 ebusuku .
UWilliams nenselelo kwabavale izikhala kwiBafana
UNOZINTI weBafana Bafana , uRonwen Williams , uphonsele inselelo abadlali okuchitshiyelwe ngabo wathi ababhukule basebenzele impumelelo yeqembu .
IBafana izokwamukela iGhana emdlalweni wokuhlungela i - Africa Cup of Nations ( Afcon ) ozoba seFNB Stadium , eNasrec , kusasa ngo - 6 ntambama .
Elakuleli libambene neGhana eqhulwini kuGroup C ngamaphuzu ayisishiyagalolunye emuva kwemidlalo emine .
Umdlalo wokugcina wokuhlunga iBafana izowudlala neSudan ekuhambeni ngeSonto .
Amalungiselelo eBafana aphazanyiswe ukungaphumeleli kwabanye abadlali abadlala phesheya kwezilwandle abanqatshelwe ukuza eMzansi ngamaqembu abo ngenxa yokudlanga kweCovid - 19 .
Laba badlali nguKeagan Dolly , Bongani Zungu , Dean Furman noThulani Serero .
Izindawo zabo zivalwe ngoVincent Pule , Thabang Monare , Lebo Maboe , Mothobi Mvala , Thabo Nodada noThabiso Kutumela .
Ukuthola amaphuzu amathathu kweBafana kungandisa amathuba okungena kwi - Afcon .
" Siphoxekile ngokuthi abanye abadlali abafikanga esiluqale nabo lolu hambo .
Kodwa abadlali abafakiwe kufanele babhukule ngempela .
Ngeke kube lula ngoba sincane isikhathi esinaso ngaphambi kosuku lomdlalo .
Kodwa kade aqala amalungiselelo omdlalo .
Ithimba labaqeqeshi kade laqala ukusithumelela ulwazi ngeGhana .
Ngakho siyalazi iqhinga esizolisebenzisa nokuthi iGhana idlala kanjani .
Kusezandleni zethu singabadlali ukuthi sisize abasha bazinze , bafunde indlela esihlele ukudlala ngayo , " kusho uWilliams .
" Siyakwazi ukubaluleka komdlalo .
Umqeqeshi ( Molefi Ntseki ) wasibuza ukuthi yini esifuna ukuyizuza , samtshela ukuthi sifuna ukuhlala phezulu eqoqweni .
Yileyo inselelo esiyibeke emahlombe ethu .
Okwamanje kubukeka kuthembisa .
Okunye esakusho wukuthi sifuna ukuwina yonke imidlalo yasekhaya .
Nalokho kusahamba kahle ngoba sisayiwine yomibili .
Sifuna ukuqhubeka nalowo mgqigqo .
" Emdlalweni wokuqala wamaqoqo iBafana yashaywa yiGhana ngo 2 - 0 ekuhambeni .
Ukunqatshelwa kwabadlali ngamaqembu aphesheya kuyithintile neGhana esizodlala ngaphandle kwezethenjwa okuyizelamani u - Andre noJordan Ayew ezidlala e - England .
Abanye abanqatsheliwe yinjini uThomas Partey owashaya igoli kowasekhaya neBafana , Nicholas Opoku no - Emmanuel Lomotey odlala eFrance .
Umqeqeshi uCharles Akonnoro usebamemezele abadlali azochibiyela ngabo .
" Sifuna lingaphuki irekhodi lethu lasekhaya .
Uma singathola lokho , sizobe sesingene ngonyawo kwi - Afcon .
Ngiphoxekile ngokuthi abanye abadlali abafikanga kodwa sizobanqobela .
Sinethemba lokuthi le Covid - 19 izodlula , sihlangane futhi siyiqembu , " kusho uWilliams .
Amaqembu amabili azoqeda elandelana phezulu eqoqweni azongena kwi - Afcon .
Eqoqweni leBafana uGroup C indawo yesithathu ibanjwe yiSudan ngamaphuzu ayisithupha .
Namuhla izodlala neSao Tome and Principe esemsileni njengoba ingakatholi maphuzu emidlalweni emine .
UMngqithi akayizwa eyokushaywa yiChiefs eqede ngomgqigqo wabo kwiligi
LUNGILE MAJOKAUMQEQESHI weMamelodi Sundowns usale engakwamukeli ukuthi bahlulwe yiKaizer Chiefs emdlalweni weDStv Premiership obungeSonto ntambama eLoftus Versfeld .
Kulo mdlalo iSundowns ebibheke ukuqhubeka nerekhodi layo lokungehlulwa kwiligi , iguqe ngo 2 - 1 .
AmaBrazilians abeye emdlalweni eseqhube imidlalo ewu - 21 engayazi induku kwiPremiership .
Abesephule irekhodi lemidlalo ewu - 19 alalibekwe Amakhosi kumasizini edlule .
Amagoli kulo mdlalo avalelwe phakathi enethini uGaston Sirino obeke phambili ompetha beligi .
Esiwombeni sesibili ibhola likaSamir Nurkovic lishaye kwisitobha seSundowns , uMosa Lebusa layongena enethini .
Kungakapheli imizuzu engakanani , uDumisani Zuma uze nelesibili leziMpofana .
UMngqithi ephawula ngemuva komdlalo kwiSuperSport uthe kufana nokuthi bazigwazi ngowabo .
Akukho okutheni okwenziwe yiChiefs ukuthi ibingaze iqede ngomgqigqo wabo .
" Ungasho ukuthi ( ibhola ) lithinte kumdlali kodwa ayikho inhlanhla ebholeni abakutholile kube wumphumela wokusebenza kanzima .
Kusukela lapho siphaphalazile .
Basihlasela , bathola uhlangothi lwethu lwesokudla luvulekile .
Ikhombise ukunganaki indlela esivale engayo emuva kwangathi akekho ombonayo uZuma ngaleso sikhathi .
" Kodwa ukukhuluma iqiniso , ngicabanga ukuthi leli akusilona iqembu obekumele lisithathele irekhodi lethu lokungehlulwa .
Angicabangi ukuthi balwe ngokwanele ukwenza izinto zibenzima kithina .
Kodwa ngikholwa wukuthi sizehlule thina , " kusho uMngqithi .
ISundowns isazihola phambili kwi - log ngaphuzu awu - 47 , ilandelwa AmaZulu FC ngamaphuzu awu - 44 .
Indawo yesithathu ibanjwe iLamontville Golden Arrows ngawu - 42 .
Ngokuwina kwi'Downs , iChiefs inyukele endaweni yesishiyagalombili ngamaphuzu awu - 28 .
Ukuqeda kwiTop 8 yikhona osekulwelwa iqembu likaGavin Hunt njengoba lingekho nhlobo embangweni wesicoco seligi .
UHunt uthe ubonga ukuthi ekugcineni nabo bathole lokhu obekubafanele emdlalweni .
Uqhube wathi ngokubona kwakhe bebengashaya amagoli kulo mdlalo ukube bawasebenzisile amathuba , ikakhulakazi abawathole esiwombeni sokuqala .
" Kodwa ke okusemqoka wukuthi ngemuva kokwehlulwa ( yiCape Town City ) ngale ndlela okwenzeke ngayo ngoLwesithathu , kulokhu sithole obekusifanele .
Kufanele ngabe senza okungcono kwiligi kodwa akunjalo .
Sizobhekana nomdlalo ngamunye .
Siyadlala futhi ngoLwesithathu .
Sizolokhu sibangcono , kumele , " kusho uHunt .
NgoLwesithathu iChiefs izokwamukela iChippa United eFNB Stadium ngo - 5 ntambama .
ISundowns yona izobe iqhuthana ne - Arrows ngesikhathi esifanayo eLoftus Versfeld .
AmaProteas azimisele ukunyathela ngolusha eWest Indies
XOLILE MPISANEASETHELEKILE esiqhingini saseSaint Lucia amaProteas ukuzoqala amalungiselelo emidlalo yochungechunge lwama - test azoyidlala neqembu laseWest Indies .
La maqembu agcina ukubhekana ngqo eWest Indies ngo - 2010 .
Ngo - 2016 ayeyingxenye yomqhudelwano owawufake neqembu lase - Australia .
Bazodlala imidlalo yama - test emibili ezoba seDarren Sammy Cricket Ground khona eSaint Lucia .
UDean Elgar , osanda kuqokwa ngokuphelele ukuba ngukaputeni weqembu lama - test kumaProteas , uthe kumele baqale uhambo olusha kule midlalo .
" Kuyasijabulisa siyiqembu ukuthi sizophinda simele izwe lethu .
Phezu kokuba sizobe sivalelekile ehhotela ngenxa ye - Covid 19 kodwa okubalulekile wukubuyela enkundleni , " kusho uElgar .
" Into esemqoka wukuthi sisheshe sijwayele isimo sezulu nendawo esizohlala kuyona , ukuze amalungiselelo ethu ahambe ngendlela .
Kumele sizimisele sisazilolonge ukuze le midlalo isithole sisesimeni esihle .
Lokho kusezandleni zethu .
" AmaProteas angena kulolu chungechunge nje asehlele endaweni yesikhombisa uma kukleliswa amaqembu ama - test emhlabeni , iWest Indies isendaweni yesithupha .
U - Elgar uthe kumele balisebenzise leli thuba ukuze basuke kule ndawo engabafanele .
" Kumele sishintshe indlela esicabanga ngayo , akulula kodwa ngoba sikhuluma ngabadlali abawu - 18 abangafani .
Inhloso wukuthi sonke sikholelwe kuleli qembu nezinhlelo esisebenzela phezu kwazo .
" Inselelo enkulu enginayo nginguaputeni omusha wukuthi ngenze bonke abadlali bangethembe futhi bahambisane nezinhlelo ezizoyisa leli qembu phambili .
" Kulo nyaka amaProteas asedlale kabili kuma - test , ahlule iSri Lanka ngo 2 - 0 ngoJanuwari ase ehlulwa yiPakistan ngo 2 - 0 ngoFebhuwari .
Ngaphambi kwalokho babegcine bedlale ne - England ekuqaleni kuka - 2020 , bakhala ngaphansi ngo 3 - 1 .
U - Elgar uthe kabalitholanga ithuba lokuthi badlale into ehlangene ngenxa yokuthi imidlalo ibihlukene kakhulu .
" Ubhubhane luphazamise okuningi .
Asikwazanga ukudlala isibalo semidlalo esanele , ngakho - ke kunzima ukusho ukuthi sikuliphi izinga siyiqembu .
Njengoba sesithole leli thuba lokuqala kabusha , sifisa ukudlala imidlalo eminingi futhi sidlale kangcono , " kuqhuba uElgar .
" Siyazi ukuthi kule midlalo yama - test esayidlala nePakistan kasidlalanga ngendlela esezingeni lamaProteas .
Kuningi esikufisayo kodwa asikho isidingo sokuthi sigagamele ngoba ukwakha iqembu kuthatha isikhathi . "
UMkhalele uyishaye emuva naphambili ngeseCosafa
UZWAKALE eyishaya emuva naphambili ngesikhathi esifanayo uHelman Mkhalele ebuzwa ngokubiza abadlali abasemgodleni weqembu eliya kuma - Olympic Games kodwa abanye ebebashiye ngaphandle .
UMkhalele , oyiphini likaHugo Broos kwiBafana Bafana nokunguye ozobe ekhuzela isikwati kwiCosafa Cup eGqeberha ngenyanga ezayo , esikwatini asethule izolo eSafa House akambalanga u - Evidence Makgopa , ogqame ngamagoli amabili behlula i - Uganda kamuva .
Ngesikhathi esifanayo , ubabizile ozakwabo esikwatini se - Under 23 okubalwa nesethenjwa sikanozinti weLamontville Golden Arrows , uSifiso Mlungwana , Bongani Sam we - Orlando Pirates , Sifiso Ngobeni weBloemfontein Celtic noSiyabonga Ngezana noHappy Mashiane beKaizer Chiefs .
Bonke laba badlali bebelokhu beyingxenye yesikwati sikaDavid Notoane nobekulindelwe ukuthi bangasali ebhanoyini eliya eTokyo eJapan lapho bevula khona nosokhaya ngomhlaka - 21 .
Nokho izolo ebethula uMkhalele kucacile ukuthi sebelikhombile eliya e - Asia , ikakhulu esebuzwa lo mqeqeshi waseNewcastle ukuthi umshiye kanjani uMakgopa , oqokwe njengomdlali ovelele kwiDStv Diski Challenge .
" Sibabizile abanye abadlali besikwati sika - Under 23 ngokuxhumana nenhlokomqeqeshi esikwatini sika - Under 23 , uDavid Notoane .
Usivumele ukuba sibabize , " kusho uMkhalele .
Kucacile kodwa ukuthi laba ababiziwe sebesefiwe esikwatini esiya eJapan , sekubuzwa ngoMakgopa .
" Angiqale ngokumbongela u - Evidence ngokuthi azethule ngokudlala kanjeya sibhekene ne - Uganda .
Lokho kwakhombisa ukuthi angadlala noma yisesigcawini esikhulu kanjani , " kusho uMkhalele , ozobe esizwa nguVeli Khumalo ocija isikwati sika - Under 17 .
" Asimbizanga ngoba usesikwatini esiya eJapan kuma - Olympics .
Lokho thina ( esikwatini seCosafa ) kusinika ithuba lokuqoka omunye umdlali .
" ICosafa iqala ngoJulayi 7 kuya kuJulayi 18 .
KwiGroup A , iBafana Bafana iboshelwe neLesotho , Eswatini neBotswana .
KwiGroup C kuboshelwe iZimbabwe , Namibia , Mozambique nezimenywa iSenegal yasentshonalanga ye - Afrika .
KwiGroup C kuboshelwe iZambia , Malawi , Madagascar neComoros .
Kula mazwe angu - 12 , mane azodlulela kumasemifinal ngoJulayi 16 .

Bancishwe ikhefu abadlali bePirates
SITHEMBISO MKHIZENGEKE balithole ikhefu abadlali be - Orlando Pirates abahlulwe izimbangi zaseSoweto , iKaizer Chiefs ngo 1 - 0 koweDStv Premiership , eFNB Stadium ngempelasonto edlule .
Ngokusho komqeqeshi wePirates , uJosef Zinnbauer , obedinwe egane unwabu , ubehlele ukuthi aphumuze abadlali bakhe njengoba kunekhefu leFifa .
Nokho ukungcwatshwa yigoli likaSamir Nukorvic kumshintshise umqondo .
" Ngeke ngikufihle ukuthi besisophe ukuthi uma sesinqobile nginike abadlali bami izinsuku ezimbili zokuphumula .
Kodwa manje lokho ngeke kusenzeka ngoba angeneme ngenxa yomphumela .
Asikho isidingo sokuphumula ngoba kumele kusetshenzwe .
Sinezinto eziningi okumele sizizuze kule sizini .
Sihlalelwe nawumsebenzi wokujabulisa abalandeli bethu , " kusho uZinnbauer .
Njengoba kuleli sonto abanye abadlali bePirates bezobe bejuluka ejimini ekomkhulu layo , eMayfair , uThulani " Tyson " Hlatshwayo , Innocent Maela , Ben Motshwari , Vincent Pule babizwe kwiBafana Bafana .
UDeon Hotto noGabadinho Mhango babizwe eNamibia naseMalawi ngokwehlukana .
Echaza mayelana nokusebenzisa uHotto njengomgadli wabeka uMhango noTshegofatso Mabasa ebhentshini , uthe : " Abanye abadlali bethu basanda kubuya ekulimaleni , ngaleyo ndlela abakakulungeli ukugijima umdlalo wonke . "
Ukwehlulwa kweBucs kuyibeke endaweni yesine ngemuva kwemidlalo engu - 21 namaphuzu awu - 35 .
Iyeke ithuba lokulala endaweni yesibili , beyizogudluza iLamontville Golden Arrows .
Isele ngemuva ngamaphuzu amahlanu kwiMamelodi Sundowns enemidlalo emithathu engakayidlali ngenxa yokuxinwa eyeCaf Champions League neyeNedbank Cup .
UZinnbauer akakufihlanga ukuthi imcasulile indlela iChiefs epake ngayo ibhasi ekubeni ibidlalela ekhaya .
" Sibonile ukuthi asibukhali phambili ingakho sizame ukuphusha u " Figo " ( uLinda Mntambo ) noNtsiki ( uNtsikelelo Nyauza ) , kanti noKabelo Dlamini noSiphesihle Ndlovu bazame konke okusemandleni .
Kumele sikhumbule ukuthi siyinqobile imidlalo emithathu eyedlule abalandeli bajabula kakhulu .
Uma ngalelo langa izinto zingahlangani isuke ingekho into ongayenza .
" Kolandelayo eZimnyama zizobhekana ne - Al Ahly Benghazi yaseLibya , ngo - Ephreli 2 , eMartyrs Of February Stadium koweCaf Confederation Cup .
Oweligi ziyoze ziwudlale ngo - Ephreli 7 , neMaritzburg United , e - Orlando Stadium .
I - Arrows ibuyele kwamhlaba ihlulwa elisemsileni
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEI - LAMONTVILLE Golden Arrows iwuqale kabi umzuliswano wesibili weDStv Premiership ishaywa iBlack Leopards ngo - 2 - 1 emdlalweni obusekhaya , eSugar Ray Xulu Stadium , eClermont , izolo ebusuku .
Kulo mdlalo amagoli eLidoda Duvha abhajiswe ezintanjeni u - Anas Mohammed ngomzuzu ka - 31 nasesikhathini sikanompempe esiwombeni sesibili .
Elokubika le - Arrows lishaywe ngesithende uMichael Gumede .
Bekuwumdlalo wesibili i - Arrows ithola umpetshisi kwiligi .
Ibifike emdlalweni indizela phezulu ngemuva kokuthi ngoMsombuluko iqophe umlando ngokuba ngeyokuqala KwaZulu - Natal ukunqoba i - Q Innovation .
Idle i - Q2 yeDStv Premiership .
Emidlalweni eyisikhombisa iqoqe amaphuzu awu - 16 .
Bese kuphele imidlalo emine yeligi Abafana Bes'thende beshaya kwasani oluphambi kwabo .
Baye kowayizolo bephuma ekubhaxabuleni iStellenbosch ngo - 3 - 1 .
Izolo esiwombeni sokuqala , konakale izinhlelo zomqeqeshi uMandla Ncikazi , zibulawa ukuphuma ngohlaka kwesiqongqwane , uNkosinathi Sibisi ongqubuzane kabi emoyeni nonozinti wakhe uSifiso Mlungwane .
Kungene uGladwin Shitolo ofike wangenza lutho .
Izinto zibhimbe kakhulu esiwombeni sesibili kuphuma ngekhadi elibomvu uPule Mmodi odlalise kabi uKenneth Mthatheni seliyozilahla kunina .
Kulo mdlalo , iLeopards ihlasele zisuka , i - Arrows ibilibele ukulahla amabhola kalula .
Esiwombeni sokuqala lilodwa ibhola eliyingozi elicishe lashaywa uVelemseni Ndwandwe ngoka - 27 .
Kusize unozinti weLeopards , uKing Ndlovu .
Ngoka - 31 , kuthele izithelo ukwenza kahle kweLidoda Duvha , u - Anas eliqedela ngekhanda kade kukhahlele uLifa Hlongwane .
UMumuni Abubakar noSibongiseni Mthethwa bebeyibulala yonke iminyakazo ye - Arrows esiswini .
Ukufika kukaKostadin Papic ukuzolekelelana noLehlohonolo Seema , kubukeka kuzoba nezithelo ezinhle kwiLeopards ababalekela izembe .
Esiwombeni sesibili , uNcikazi ufake uLindokohle Mtshali ofike wazama ukubamba isisu .
I - Arrows iqalile yahlasela kubhoke uKnox Mutizwa , Michael Gumede , noMmodi .
Ngemuva kokuphuma kukaMmodi , lehlile izinga layo , kwaqala phansi ukuhlasela kweLidoda Duvha .
ILeopards obese kuphele imidlalo emihlanu iwukudla kwenduku , inyukele endaweni ka - 15 , ngamaphuzu awu - 12 .
Ibhuleki selivalwe iMaritzburg United edonsa kanzima ngaphansi kuka - Ernst Middendorp .
Kule mpelasonto kunemidlalo yeNedbank Cup , i - Arrows engasekho kuyona njengoba yakhishwa AmaZulu FC .
ILeopards izobhekana naMaZulu kwiLast 16 yeNedbank Cup ngoMgqibelo .
UHunt unikwa ithemba ukungabibikho kwezihlwele emidlalweni yeCaf
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUMQEQESHI weKaizer Chiefs , uGavin Hunt , uqiniswa idolo ukungabibikho kwezihlwele ezijwayele ukuthwalisa kanzima amaqembu akuleli emidlalwani yeCaf Champions League azimisele ukuhamba ibanga elide kuyo .
Kuyinto eyaziwayo ukuthi uma amaqembu akuleli edlalela ekuhambeni kwiChampions League noma kwiCaf Confederation Cup , ubunzima aqala ukubuthwala ehla ngakho kodwa esikhumulweni sezindiza .
Kwesinye isikhathi kuvela imibiko yokuncishwa noma ukunikwa izinkundla zokuziqeqesha ezingekho ezingeni .
Kwesinye esikhathi imidlalo idlalelwe ezindaweni ezingenamahhotela asezingeni elifanele .
Asuke esalindwe nayiziwengu zezihlwele ezigcwala phama enkundleni .
Kulo nyaka ezikaHunt zingene okokuqala esigabeni samaqoqo eChampions League .
Njengoba ziphuma esigwebeni ebesizivimba ukusayinisa , zizogijima lo mqhudelwano ngeningi labadlali abasebancane , abangenaso naso isipiliyoni sokumelena nezinselelo zale midlalo .
Ebuzwa uHunt ukuthi akanavalo yini ngalokhu uthe : " Sibazi kahle ubunzima esizobhekana nabo .
Ngiyazama ukuthi ngiqinise imiqondo nemizimba yabadlali bami .
Iqiniso esingeke siliphike ukuthi iningi lamazwe asenhla nezwekazi i - Afrika asibona sintekenteke .
Ngeke uhambe ibanga elide kule midlalo uma abadlali bakho bengaqinile emqondweni nasemzimbeni .
Okunginika ithemba ukungabi bikho kwabalandeli .
Amaqembu anjengeWAC Casablanca esiqhathwe nayo ku - Group C anabalandeli abayinkinga , abangagcina befaka ingebhe kubadlali .
Ukungabibikho kwabo kuzosisebenzela kakhulu .
" Ngeledlule , abaningi bakuthathe njengokuqhubeka kokuhlukuyezwa kwamaqembu akuleli ukunqatshelwa kweMamelodi Sundowns ukungena e - Algeria ukuyodlala neCR Belouizdad nokuvinjwa kweChiefs ukudlala neCasablanca , eMorocco .
La mazwe abekhala ngokudla lubi kweCovid - 19 eNingizimu Afrika .
Lolu daba lugcine lungenwe iCaf ethathe isinqumo esithe iSundowns neBelouizdad sebezodlalela eTanzania kuthi Amakhosi neCasablanca badlalele eBurkina Faso .
Yomibili le midlalo isizokuba ngeSonto .
Phezu kwenkinga yesipiliyoni kwiChiefs , uHunt ongelona ivukana emidlalweni yase - Afrika , uthe bazimisele ukudlula esigabeni samaqoqo , baphume okungenani kwesomkhumulajezi .
" Ngeke ngithi nginengcindezi ngokwenza kahle kwiChampions League , okubalulekile ukuthi sidlale ngikuzigqaja , sibeke phambili isithunzi seqembu .
Kwamina uqobo ngingajabula ukuhamba ibanga elide kulokhu .
Kuzomele singaxhamazeli , sithathe umdlalo ngamunye .
Nakuba abadlali beshaywa isipiliyoni kodwa bajabule , bayakuqonda ukuthi kumele baziqophele owabo umlando , " kusho uHunt .
Izolo ebusuku Amakhosi adlale kowokuqala kowamaqoqo neHoroya yaseGuinea .
Usekhonjwe indlela uNtseki kwesokuqeqesha iBafana
LUNGILE MAJOKAUSEXOSHIWE uMolefi Ntseki esikhundleni sokuqeqesha iqembu lesizwe iBafana Bafana .
Lokhu kumenyezelwe isikhulu esiphezulu seSouth African Football Association ( Safa ) , uTebogo Motlanthe kwisithangami nabezindaba ngoLwesithathu eSafa House .
" Ngo - 10 ( ngoLwesithathu ) isigungu esiphezulu seSafa sithathe isinqumo sokwehlukana kuthi nomqeqeshi , " kusho uMotlanthe .
Uthe yena njengesikhulu esiphezulu ubesazohlangana noNtseki ukumazisangokusemthethweni ngesinqumo esithathiwe , badingide nodaba lwenkontileka ebingakapheli .
Okugqamile kulesi sithangami wukuthi umengameli weSafa uDanny Jordaan ubengabonwa kuso .
UMotlanthe ubehambisana nosihlalo wekomodi losomaqhinga , uJack Maluleka .
Uthe isigungu esiphezulu sithume bona ukuthi bazoxolisa esizweni ngokuthi iBafana ayiyi kwi - Africa Cup of Nations ( Afcon ) ezobanjelwa eCameroon ngonyaka ozayo .
UNtseki uxoshwe ngemuva kokuthi ehlulekile ukufaka iBafana kwi - Afcon .
INingizimu Afrika ihlulwe yiSudan ngo 2 - 0 ngempelasonto edlule emdlalweni wokugcina wokuhlunga kuGroup C .
Lokhu kwenze yaqeda eqoqweni isendaweni yesithathu ngamaphuzu awu - 10 .
UHunt usale engeneme bedlula sekuvalwe amehlo koweCaf
USALE enganeme ngabadlali bakhe umqeqeshi weKaizer Chiefs , uGavin Hunt , bephuma ngembobo yenaliti koweCAF Champions League ngoMgqibelo ntambama .
Amakhosi ahlulwe yiSimba SC yaseTanzania ngo 3 - 0 emdlalweni womlenze wesibili wama - quarterfinal eDar es Salaam ngempelasonto .
Ayekade enqobe ngo 4 - 0 kowokuqala kuleli .
IChiefs isizobhekana neWydad Casablanca yaseMorocco kowandulela owamanqamu oyimilenze emibili .
Owokuqala uzoba ngoJuni 18 eMorocco .
Owesibili uzoba seMzansi ngoJuni 25 .
Komunye owandulela owamanqamu , i - Esperance yaseTunisia izobhekana ne - Al Ahly yase - Egypt ekhiphe iMamelodi Sundowns .
Okushiye uHunt engagculisekile yindlela ezakhe ezidlale ngayo eTanzania .
" Sihlulekile ukudlala ngenxa yezizathu ezaziwayo .
Besilokhu siphisana ngebhola .
Kodwa okubalulekile wukuthi sidlulele phambili .
Yilokho okubalulekile emidlalweni yemilenze emibili .
Bekunzima kakhulu namuhla , " kusho uHunt .
Ngemuva komdlalo womlenze wokuqala eFNB Stadium , iningi belizitshela ukuthi iChiefs isiyogcina icala eTanzania .
ISimba , ekade yesekwa ngabalandeli bayo enkundleni , icishe yawona umcimbi kwazise umdlalo uphele sekubanjwe umoya .
" Ibingekho ingozi emizuzwini engu - 20 noma engu - 26 yokuqala .
Bathola ikhona , bashaya igoli okuyilona elisihlalise emuva .
Bashaya nelesibili ngaso isiwombe sokuqala elenze kwaba nzima .
Emuva kwalokho , simake kwaze kwaba sekugcineni .
Kade sazi ukuthi badlalela ekhaya , bazohlasela ngakho konke .
Badlale ngabadlali abane phambili , " kusho uHunt .
UHunt kufanele anganami ngendlela ezakhe ezinze ngayo emdlalweni weSimba .
Uma sizoqhubeka nokudlala ngendlela engagculisi zingagcina zingayinuki iTop 8 kwiDStv Premiership .
IChiefs ibambe indawo ka - 11 kwi - log ngamaphuzu awu - 30 .
Idinga ukuqoqa amaphuzu emidlalweni emithathu esele ukuze izibeke ethubeni lokunyukela emaqenjini ayisishiyagalombili aphezulu .
NgoLwesithathu , Amakhosi azovakashela iBlack Leopards koweligi eThohoyandou Stadium , eGiyani , ngo - 3 ntambama .
Izobe isidlala neLamontville Golden Arrows ( Juni 2 ) bese isonga iligi neTS Galaxy ngoJuni 5 .
Emuva kwemidlalo yeligi izolungiselela iWydad edlale nayo kabili esigabeni samaqoqo .
IWydad ihlule iChiefs ngo 4 - 0 kowokuqala ekuhambeni .
Amakhosi awine owesibili ngo 1 - 0 .
UTruter akaneme ngamagoli adedelwa yiZinyoni
STHEMBISO NGOBESEUZOLWA nokulungisa inkinga yodonga alubona lungaqinile umqeqeshi weSwallows FC , uBrandon Truter , njengoba ebona beqhubeka nokungenelwa ngamagoli angafanele emidlalweni yabo yakamuva .
UTruter ukusho lokhu ngemuva kokuba iZinyoni zaseDube ziphinde zalahla amaphuzu amqoka ngesikhathi zibanjwa ngo - 1 - 1 yiTshakuma Tsha Madzivhandila emdlalweni weDStv Premiership ngempelasonto , eDobsonville Stadium , eSoweto .
Kulo mdlalo igoli leSwallows lishaywe nguZaphania Mbokoma kwathi elokulinganisa leTTM ebithela emuva njengembumba , labekwa enethini nguBulelani Ndengane kade kuyiphenathi edalwe nguPetso Maphanga kungenasidingo .
Ukuhluleka kweSwallows ukuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele kuyenzele phansi njengoba isishoveleke endaweni yesihlanu kwi - log ngamaphuzu angu - 31 emidlalweni engu - 18 .
UTruter ukhale kakhulu ngohluleka kwezakhe ukunqoba lo mdlalo , athe bekumele bawunqobe noma yikanjani kwazise badlale kahle .
" Lona bekungumdlalo onzima kakhulu , emizuzwini engu - 85 ebisidlaliwe ubungasho ukuthi amaphuzu agcwele asesemgodleni kodwa futhi saphinde sawudedela kalula sekusele imizuzu emibili nje ekutheni uphele .
" Besekuwumdlalo wethu wesikhombisa siwudlala ngokulingana kule sizini , okuhle wukuthi siyakwazi ukushaya amagoli kodwa futhi aphinde asingenele ngendlela exakayo .
Kodwa - ke kuzomele siyilungise ngokushesha indaba yokuvuza kodonga lwethu lwasemuva .
Ngiyethemba ukuthi abadlali bami bazofunda lukhulu emaphutheni enzekile , kuzomele bakhule , " kusho uTruter obezwakala ukuthi isiqala ukumkhathaza indaba yokugqoza kokunqoba .
ISwallows izobuyela enkundleni uma isigadulisana neChippa United emdlalweni weligi ngoMashi 20 eNelson Mandela Bay Stadium , eGqeberha .
UMaluleka usabheke ezinye izicoco kwi'Downs
XOLILE MPISANEUMDLALI wasesiswini weMamelodi Sundowns , uGeorge Maluleka , uthi usalindele lukhulu emva kokuwina isicoco seDStv Premiership kwisizini yakhe yokuqala naleli qembu .
UMaluleka ( 32 ) usayine kumaBrazilians ngoJulayi ngonyaka odlule emva kokuphela kwenkontileka yakhe neKaizer Chiefs .
Noma edlale imidlalo ewu - 11 kuphela kwiligi kwisizini esanda kuphela , waqala emihlanu , uthe bekungelula ukuvele athole isikimu eqenjini elinabadlali abanjengo - Andile Jali , Rivaldo Coetzee , Hlompho Kekana nabanye .
" Ngijabule kakhulu , ukuwina izicoco kuyohlezi kujabulisa .
Bekuyisizini yami yokuqala neqembu kodwa ngikwazile ukuphakamisa indebe yeligi futhi , " kusho uMaluleka .
" Kule midlalo engiyidlalile ngicabanga ukuthi ngenze kahle .
Umdlalo engingathokozanga ngawo esawudlala neBloemfontein Celtic kodwa ngigculisekile ngeminye .
" Konke kwenzeke ngendlela ebengiyilindele .
ISundowns inenqwaba yabadlali abasezingeni eliphezulu .
Sisivikele isicoco seligi , okusho ukuthi siyabuyela kwi - CAF Champions League ngesizini ezayo .
Kwasiphatha kabi ukukhishwa yi - Al Ahly .
" Noma kunjalo siyaziqhenya .
Ngiyazama ukungazifaki ngaphansi kwengcindezi ngoba bekuyisizini yokuqala .
Abantu abaningi babethi ngeke ngidlale kodwa ngidlalile .
Nami ngiphonsile esivivaneni , ngijabule kakhulu .
" UMaluleka wayiwina kabili iligi neSuperSport United , wayinqoba kanye neChiefs njengoba esephinde wayithatha neSundowns .
Uthe usalambele ezinye izicoco futhi unethemba lokuthi ziyeza uma ebheka adlala nabo nomsebenzi owenziwa ngabaqeqeshi uManqoba Mngqithi , Steve Komphela noRhulani Mokwena .
" Angisabheki emuva , ngisalindele okukhulu kunalokhu .
Ngiyethemba ukuthi kuningi esisazokuzuza naleli qembu , " kuqhuba uMaluleka .
" Nabaqeqeshi bashaye into ecokeme ngokuthatha iligi ngesizini yabo yokuqala , kuyakhombisa ukuthi basezingeni eliphezulu .
USteve uthanda kwenziwe izinto ngendlela eqondile , uManqoba udlala indima yokuba ubaba noRhulani naye ukhona .
Bayahlangana bakhe amasu esizowasebenzisa enkundleni .
Bonke baletha okuthile okuhlukile okuphathelene nebhola noma impilo nje .
Ngibona ukuthi yilokho okwenze siphumelele . "
UMngqithi udalula imfihlo yabo kwiDowns
UKWENGEZWA kukaSteve Komphela ethimbeni labaqeqeshi beMamelodi Sundowns ekuqaleni kwesizini , kudale ukungabaza ukuthi bazokwazi ukusebenza bebathathu ngokubambisana ngaphandle kokuxokizelana .
UKomphela wethulwe waba ngumqeqeshi omdala ( senior coach ) ejoyina uManqoba Mngqithi noRulani Mokwena abethulwe kwathiwa bangabaqeqeshi abalinganayo ekuholeni iqembu .
Yinto ebingakaze ibonakale kunobhutshuzwayo waseNingizimu Afrika ukuthi iqembu libe nezinhloko zabaqeqeshi ezintathu .
Kodwa bagile izimanga behlanganisa imidlalo engu - 20 yeligi bengayazi induku , kangangoba banqobe isicoco seligi besahlulwe wumdlalo owodwa kwengu - 27 yeDStv Premiership .
Baphume kuma - semifinal eNedbank Cup nakuma - quarterfinal eCaf Champions League .
Engxoxweni ekhethekile neSolezwe ngeSonto , uMngqithi uveze imfihlo ebenze baphumelela ukubambisana bobathathu .
" Into esivumelane ngayo kuqala isizini wukuthi kufanele sisebenzele ukugeza igama lomuntu omnyama .
Siyindlu emnyama sidume ngokuthi kasikwazi ukubambisana .
Sidume ngokuthi sivele sibange amandla sibuye sikhwabanise uma sibekwe ezikhundleni zokuhola .
Bekufanele sibe yisibonelo sokuthi indlu emnyama yingakwenza okuhlukile , ingaklwebhani kodwa ibambisane , " kusho uMngqithi .
Lo mqeqeshi waseMvubukazi , eMzimkhulu sikhuluma nje , ubalwe nazo izinsizwa asebenza nazo , uMokwena noKomphela bamele iSundowns embangweni womklomelo womqeqeshi ovelele kule sizini .
Isicoco esinqotshwe yiSundowns ngesika - 11 emlandweni weligi yePremier Soccer League .
Yibisisinqoba okwesine amasizini elandelana .
Nyakenye uMngqithi wubekhona besinqoba okwesithathu kulandelana eyiphini likaPitso Mosimane osekwi - Al Ahly .
Empeleni kusekhona ukuhlukana phakathi kubathandi bakanobhutshuzwayo .
Abanye basamile ekutheni yima kuzocaca ngesizini ezayo ukuthi ngabe ngempela siyasebenza yini isixaxa mbiji , sikaMngqithi nozakwabo noma bebesashaya ngoshuni oshiywe nguMosimane .
" Ngeke ngiqambe amanga ngithi uPitso akasishiyanga isisekelo lapha eqenjini .
Nami bengikhona lapho .
Yimi owazi kahle ukuthi ushiye senzeni .
Nokho umuntu oqonda ibhola ubonile ukuthi sithe ukuhluka isitayela sokudlala .
Ngaphezu kwalokho , kunenqwaba yabadlali abafike kule sizini esehambile .
Lokho kwenze sashintsha izindawo zabanye abaningi abakade bekhona .
Lokho kufanele kusheshe kutolike ukushintsha kwendlela yokudlala , " " kusho uMngqithi .
IChiefs iphunyule sekuvalwe amehlo
SIBUSISO MDLALOSE noNHLANHLA SITHOLEKUQOPHEKE umlando eNaturena emuva kokuthi iKaizer Chiefs ingene esigabeni esandulela esamanqamu eCaf Champions League okokuqala emlandweni wayo , yize ishaywe yiSimba SC ngo 3 - 0 emdlalweni obudlalelwa eTanzania izolo ntambama .
Amakhosi abeye kulo mdlalo ehamba phambili ngo 4 - 0 emuva kokuthi emlenzeni wokuqala obuseFNB Stadium , eGoli .
Lapha bekudingeka ukuba iSimba ishaye amagoli amahlanu , bese kuthi iChiefs ingabi nayo impendulo .
Ephawula ngalo mdlalo umqeqeshi waMakhosi uGavin Hunt uthe konke kuhambe njengoba bebefisa , ukudlulela esigabeni esandulela esamanqamu .
" Bekungelula neze kulo mdlalo .
Kubengconywana esikhathini esingangemizuzu ewu - 26 yokuqala .
Emuva kwalo bathole igoli lokuqala nokwenze sadlala ngaphansi kwengcindezi , " kuchaza uHunt .
Ngalo mphumela uthe : " Empeleni lomphumela akusiwona owami ngedwa kodwa oweqembu lonke leChiefs .
Yize sinqobile kodwa kumele silungiselele imidlalo emithathu esele yeligi .
Mayelana nomdlalo wesigaba esandulela esamanqamu kubukeka izophazamisa izinhlelo zokuqala amalungiselelo esizini entsha , kodwa akusenani sizibona .
" Komunye umdlalo i - Al Ahly iqhubeke lapho igcine khona iwashisa ijezi iMamelodi Sundowns ibambana nayo ngo 1 - 1 emlenzeni sesibili wama - quarterfinal eCaf Champions League obuseLucas Moripe Stadium , izolo ntambama .
I - Al Ahly ibivele ize kulo mdlalo ihamba phambili ngamagoli njengoba emlenzeni wokuqala kuyiyona ebinqobe ngo 2 - 0 eCairo , e - Egypt , ngoMgqibelo odlule .
Nokho ezikaPitso Mosimane zikhombise zisuka nje ukuthi azizile ukuzosinisa amahleza kulo mdlalo ngenkathi uYassir Ibrahim engqomfela phakathi ngekhanda ibhola ebeliyikhona ebigotshwe u - Amr Sulaya ngomzuzu ka - 11 .
Okuqaphelekile kulo mdlalo ukubuya kwesiklwibhishi nesethenjwa seDowns , uThemba " Mshishi " Zwane nenjini yasesiswini u - Andile Jali abangadlalanga emlenzeni wokuqala e - Egypt , abadlake kangcono kakhulu kulo mdlalo .
UMosa Lebosa uyena otholele iDowns igoli lokulinganisa ngomzuzu ka - 29 engqomfela phakathi ngekhanda ibhola ebeligotshwe u - Aubrey Modiba kade kuyikhona .
Nakuba ziye ekhefini zibambene ngo 1 - 1 kodwa kodwa iDowns yiyona ebiphethe umdlalo ngesiwombe sokuqala , nakwesesibili bekuyesifanayo kodwa kwala khona ukwenza .
IDowns bekudingeka inqobe lo mdlalo ngo 3 - 0 ingangenelwa goli kulo mdlalo ukuze izibekisele indawo kowandulela owamanqamu , nokho okugcine kungenzekanga njengoba ezikaMosimane zibukeke " zipake ibhasi " kulo mdlalo .
Ngemuva komdlalo uPitso Mosimane ocija amaRed Devils uphume enkundleni eqhasha ngaphandle kokuxhawula kubalingani bakhe beSundowns .
Ekhuluma nabezindaba emuva komdlalo uthe uphoxeke kabi ngemibiko ebibhalwe ezingqwembeni endleleni eya enkundleni .
" Ngiyazibuza ukuthi kumele ngilenzeleni engcono leli qembu njengoba abalandeli balo bengithuka ngale ndlela .
Okungizwisa ubuhlungu kakhulu ukungithuka ngomama .
Ngiyamazi umuntu obephehla lokhu , kodwa kulungile , " kukhala uMosimane .
Isikhulu asizilungele izinselelo eziza nokunqoba iNedbank
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUNGENA ezintangeni umnikazi weRichards Bay , uSifiso " Jomo " Biyela uma ebuzwa ukuthi ngabe uzilungele izinselelo zokunqoba iNedbank Cup .
INatal Rich Boyzs idlulele kuma - quarterfinal eNedbank Cup ngemuva kokuqumba phansi iTS Sporting ngo 2 - 1 emdlalweni weLast 16 .
Emdlalweni wokuqala leli qembu eliphekwa uSimo Dladla lawashisa ijezi iKaizer Chiefs .
Kuma - qaurterfinal ezikaBiyela ziqhathwe neChippa United edlule kwiCape Town City ngo - 2 - 1 .
Umdlalo ungoMgqibelo ngo - 3 .
30pm eSisa Dukashe Stadium , eMdantsane .
Amanye amaqembu adlala kwiGladAfrica Championship akuma - quarter final , iCape Town All Stars ezodlala nontanga bayo iPretoria Callies .
INedbank Cup idume ngokuba nofishi abancane abadla abakhulu , ngo - 2019 , iTS Galaxy eyayidlala kwiGladAfrica , yamangaza izwe ishaya iKaizer Chiefs kowamanqamu ale nkomishi .
Yaba yiqembu lokuqala elidlala kulesi sigaba ukunqoba lo mqhudelwano , nokudlala kwiCaf Confederation Cup okubikwa ukuthi inezindleko ezimba eqolo .
Ebuzwa uBiyela ukuthi njengoba abafana bakhe beshisa ngalolu hlobo , ngabe uzivivele yini izindleko zokunqoba iNedbank Cup , uthe : " Eish , iqhinga liyozakha uma kwenzeka ngibhekana naleso simo .
Ukukhuluma iqiniso , bengingakulindele ukufika kulesi sigaba esesikuso .
Ubhekana nezinselelo ezifana nalezi uma unabadlali abanethelante , abalithandayo iqembu labo .
" Uqhube wathi : " INedbank Cup kayikho ezinhlelweni zami , ekhanda kuduma isicoco seligi .
Sisembhidlangweni wokuqoqa amaphuzu awu - 65 .
Ngizokwenza konke okusemandleni ukujabulisa abadlali bami ukuze lifezeke leli phupho .
Ngingamane ngikhiphe amabhonasi uma kungiphoqa .
AmaNatal Rich Boys ngiwafuna kwiDStv Premiership ngesizini ezayo .
" UDan " Dance " Malesela owanqobisa iGalaxy , iNedbank ngo - 2019 , uthe ukunqoba kweBay kwiKaizer akusho ukuthi kumele bayisabe .
" Ngiwumuntu ongenandaba nokuthi amaqembu aqhathwe kanjani , nokuthi iqembu elithile lizodlala nobani .
Okubalulekile ukuthi sizodlala kanjani emdlalweni ozayo , kusiphoqa ukwenyusa izinga .
Kunamaqembu asatshwa kungafanele , uthole ukuthi uma sesidlala nawo awanasimanga , " kubeka uMalesela ngemuva kokuqhathwa kwabo .
Nasemidlalweni yeligi iBay kuyihambela kahle .
Iqhwakele ngamaphuzu awu - 28 emuva kwemidlalo ewu - 16 .
Kuyibhedele ekugcineni iSwallows ibanjwa koweligi
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEIPHINDE yahluleka iSwallows ukuzibuyisela embangweni wesicoco seligi , ibambana ngo - 1 - 1 neTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ( TTM ) emdlalweni obuyizolo , eDobsonville Stadium .
Igoli leSwallows libhakuziswe enethini uZaphania Mbokoma ngomzuzu ka - 31 ngemuva komnyakazo omuhle kaKamohelo Mahlatsi noRuzaigh Gamildien .
Ele TTM kube iphenathi evalelwe phakathi uBulelani Ndengane esikhathini sikanompempe .
IZinyoni zibulawe uPetso Maphanga ongene esiwombeni sesibili owise uNdengane ebhokisini singekho isidingo .
Usawoti esilondeni seSwallows uphinde wathelwa ukunqoba kweLamontville Golden Arrows eshaye iBlack Leopards ngo - 3 - 1 .
I - Arrows inyukele kweyesine ngamaphuzu awu - 32 , Izinyoni zehlela kweyesihlanu ngawu - 31 .
Izolo bekuwumdlalo weshumi Izinyoni zidlala ngokulingana .
Zagcina ukunqoba ngoJanuwari zishaya iBaroka .
Njengoba beziphuma ekushayweni okokuqala zidlala neTS Galaxy koweNedbank Cup , bekwethenjwa ukuthi zizokwazi ukuvala igebe lamaphuzu phakathi kwazo namaqembu angaphezulu .
Esiwombeni sokuqala okugqame kuso unozinti weSwallows , uVirgil Vries obevimba izinguzunga zamashodi kaRhulani Manzini noFarai Madhanaga , kuhlasele zisuka yona iSwallows .
Ukuhlangana kukaKamohelo Mahlatshi , Kgaokgelo Sekgota noGamildien kuzithwalise kanzima izitobha zeTTM .
UNdengane weTTM obematasa nokudlalisa kabi uMahlatshi usindele unompempe uPhilangenkosi Khumalo obekubonakala engazimisele ukukhipha amakhadi kwesokuqala .
Kwesesibili ugcine elitholeli eliphuzi uNdengane .
Bese kungathi uyabukisa uKhumalo ngokukhipha amakhadi aphuzi .
Nakuba ibhola belisezinyaweni zeSwallows esikhathini esiningi kodwa iTTM beyifika kuzwakale ebhokisini lezitha .
Ukube ubelele eVries ngabe kushintshwe iTTM isivalele amagoli amathathu kaManzini nelikaMadhanaga .
Abaqeqeshi beTTM , uMpho Maleka noDavid Mathebula kuthe uma bebona ukuthi kuyonakala , esiwombeni sesibili babeuya noCelimpilo Ngema ongene esikhundleni sikaManzini noJoseph Malongoane abangene bayishukumisa bebambisene noLerato Lamola ongawuqedanga umdlalo .
Ngoka - 50 , uNgema udedele ingizunga evinjwe uVries maqede walimala ihlombe .
Ukungena kukaTokelo Ranti noThabo Rakhale kube nezithelo , iTTM bese ihlasela ingaqedi okudale ukutatazela kwabeSwallows .
Zivele sezikhona izinkulumo ezithi insimbi seyiqalile ukushisa kubadlali nakubaqeqeshi beSwallows .
Amanye amaqembu aseyibambile indlela edlala ngayo .
ISwallows isiyoze idlale neChippa United ngoMashi 20 , eNelson Mandela Bay Stadium .
ITTM izoqhubeka nokuhlala endaweni ka - 14 ngamaphuzu awu - 16 , emidlalweni ewu - 18 .
Kolandelayo iTTM izokwamukela iLamontville Golden Arrows , e - Old Peter Mokaba Stadium ngoLwesithathu .
Imiphumela yeDStv Premiership : SuperSport United 0 - 0 TS Galaxy ; Cape Town City 1 - 2 Stellenbosch ; Chippa United 0 - 3 Orlando Pirates ; Black Leopards 1 - 3 Lamontville Golden Arrows ; Swallows 1 - 1 Tshakhuma .
Imiphumela yeGladAfrica Championship : Cape Umoya United 0 - 2 Uthongathi ; JDR 1 - 2 Cape Town All Stars ; Bizana Pondo Chiefs 0 - 0 Richards Bay FC ; Jomo Cosmos 1 - 3 TS Sporting ; Polokwane City 1 - 0 University of Pretoria ; Pretoria Callies 2 - 3 Royal AM ; Sekhukhune 1 - 0 Free State Stars ; Cape Town Spurs 1 - 1 Steenburg .
UMotsepe umelwe wukukhipha iCaf ehlazweni
" I - AFRICA idinga ukuhlanganyela ngobuhlakani , kanjalo nesiphiwo esikhethekile sabo bonke omengameli ( bezinhlangano eziphethe ibhola ) emazweni angamalungu ( eCaf ) .
" Lawa ngamanye amazwi kaPatrice Motsepe ngesikhathi emukela ukuqokwa kwakhe ukuba ngumengameli omusha weConfederation of African Football Association eRabat , eMoroco ngoLwesihlanu .
" Uma sonke sisebenza ngokubambisana , unobhutshuzwayo e - Afrika uzokuba nempumelelo nentuthuko engakaze ibonakale phambili , " kusho le njinga yezimayini ekleliswe yaba ngeyesishiyagalolunye kubantu abacebile e - Afrika .
Uthe uthokoze kakhulu ( ngokuqokelwa esikhundleni ) .
Ngakho izinto kuzodingeka zenziwe ngokukhulu ukushesha ngoba muningi kakhulu umsebenzi osadinga ukwenziwa .
Kuzodingeka senze isiqiniseko sokuthi ibhola lase - Africa aligcini nje kuphela ngokwaziwa lapha e - Africa kuphela kodwa nasemhlabeni wonke .
" I - Africa ichitha izigidi zama - dollar minyaka yonke ithenga amalungela emidlalo yebhola komabonakude ukuveza amaligi angaphandle kwe - Afrika .
Kunesidingo sokuthi sizakhele eyethu imikhiqizo , ngaleyo ndlela sizophumelela .
" Ibhola lase - Africa ngeke liphinde lifane nakuqala .
U - 95 % wezingxoxo zethu uzoba yibhola , ngiyavuma kuhle lokho , kodwa kuzofanele kube no - 5 % lapho sizoxoxa khona ngokubaluleka kwezinkampani ezizimele ( ezingafaka imali ebholeni ) .
Sidinga ukubuyisa ukuziqhenya , isithunzi nokuhlonishwa kwe - Africa , " kusho uDkt Patrice Motsepe .
UMotsepe ukhuluma kanjena nje , ubhekene nenselelo enkulu yokukhipha iCaf ehlazweni engene kulo iphethwe ngu - Ahmad Ahmad obe ngumengameli wokuqala wale nhlangano odabuka e - Afrika esemazansi .
U - Ahmad ngowaseMadagascar , umiswe iminyaka emibili engazihlanganisi nebhola emuva kokulahlwa ngamacala enkohlakalo .
" Ukubola kwesandla " sika - Ahmad kubonakale nangokuthi womahlanu amazwe abemele iCaf kwi - 2018 Fifa World Cup aphume wonke esigabeni samaqoqo , obekuqala ukwenzeka eminyakeni engu - 36 .
Kuqokwa u - Ahmad , ekhipha u - Issa Hayatou , waseCameroon obeseqhoqhobele esokuhola iCaf iminyaka engu - 29 , kwaba khona abasola umengameli weFifa , uGianni Infantino ngokuba nomthelela emiphumeleni yokhetho .
Nasekuqokweni kukaMotsepe angaphikiswa , asifihliwe isandla sika - Infantino kwazise ubephambili emihlanganweni ebiseMorocco ngaphambi kokhetho .
Kule mihlangano bebekhona bobane abebebanga , uMotsepe , u - Ahmed Yahya waseMauritania no - Augustin Senhgor waseSenegal abaphume embangweni bamukela ngaphambi kokhetho izikhundla zokuba ngamaphini , elesibili nelokuqala kaMotsepe .
Kanjalo noJacques Anouma wase - Ivory Coast , osale ekhalela " intandoyeningi " ekhonjwa kwesokuba ngumeluleki oyisipesheli kaMotsepe .
Ukukhipha iCaf ehlazweni , nazi ezinye zezinto ngokombiko we - AFP , ezimele uMotsepe ukuba aziqondise .
Ukulwa nenkohlakaloIgama leCaf lingcolisekile eminyakeni edlule lilandelwa yizinsolo zenkohlakalo , ezinye zazo eziqinisekisiwe ophenyweni lweFifa kwazise wamiswa iminyaka emihlanu u - Ahmad .
Okufanele kukhathaze uMotsepe wukuthi ngaphambi kokumiswa u - Ahmad ubesekwa yizifunda ezingu - 46 kwezingu - 54 zeCaf ukuthi abuyele ihlandla lesibili ekubeni ngumengameli .
U - Ahmad usolwa " ngokukhwabanisa imali , wukusebenzisa amandla ngendlela engeyiyo , wukwamukela nokunikezela ngezipho nokunye .
" Indlela yokuphatha Umbiko wakamuva wocwaningo lwamabhuku olunzulu wePricewaterhouse Coopers uveze ukuthi iCaf inezinto eziningi ezikhokhela ngemali eqhamuka kuye ekhukhwini lakhe , okunika isithombe sokungaphathwa ngendlela kwezimali nenhlangano uqobo .
Amabhuku ayo kuthiwe " kawakholakali " okuningi ukusebenza kwemali akunawo amaphepha akusekayo .
Emahhovisi ekomkhulu eCairo kuthiwa ashoda ngabasebenzi , okuholela ekutheni abakhona badonse kanzima futhi bangabi namdlandla .
Ukungabonwa kwiTV kwemidlaloInhlangano ehamba phambili ukusakaza ibhola lase - Afrika ngesiNgisi eseGoli , iSuperSport , igcine ngo - 2019 ukukhombisa imidlalo yamaqembu yeCaf ngenxa yengxabano ngezinkontileka .
" Ezinselelweni ezibhekene noMotsepe wukwakha ubumbano kwiCaf nokulungisa indaba yemidlalo kwiTV , " kusho uKalusha Bwalya , oke wengamela inhlangano eyengamele ibhola eZambia futhi oke wanqoba i - African Footballer of the Year .
Wukulungisa ezokuxhumanaUma ungena kwi - website yeCaf kuncane kakhulu okuthola okumayelana nezindaba zebhola lase - Afrika .
World Cup 2022 " uthola uhla lwemidlalo , izinkundla namagama onondweba emidlalo yokuhlunga edlalwe ngoSepthemba 2019 .
Ayikho kodwa imiphumela , amagama abashaye amagoli nezikhathi zamagoli .
Imidlalo ezodlala ngoMeyi iqhathwe ngoJanuwari 21 , 2020 kodwa namanje uhla lwemidlalo olukhona kalunayo imininingwane edingekayo .
Indaba yonondwebaZihlale zivela izinsolo zesandla semfene konondweba emidlalweni yeCaf .
Ayikho iVAR e - Afrika futhi no - Infantino uyayibona inkinga , useze wathi akuqokwe uhlu lonondweba beqophelo base - Afrika abazoholelwa yiFifa .
Ukulungisa udaba lwemihlomuloAmaqembu amaningi agcina engayikhuthaleli imidlalo yeCaf ngoba imali yemihlomulo iqala ukungena emuva kwemizuliswano emibili ( kwiChampions League ) , emithathu ( kwiConfederation Cup ) .
Nalawo maqembu abekezela aze ayonqoba isicoco seChampions League esihambisana noR37 million , akhala ngokuthi akuwenzeli mehluko otheni kwazise isigamu sikhokha amabhonasi abadlali .
" Kuyichilo ukuthi abanikazi bamaqembu anqoba izicoco bangena emaphaketheni abo ukuqinisa amabhuku ezimali , " kusho u - Infantino .
Uvuma eyokubanjwa kweqhinga lokunqoba OweZinyoni
UMQEQESHI weSwallows , uBrandon Truter , uvuma eyokubanjwa kwamaqhinga abekade ezigelezela ngawo esaphuma kwiGladAfrica Championship ekuqaleni kwesizini .
IZinyoni zitheleke kwiDStv Premiership zathwesa ubunzima inqwaba yamaqembu , zithela othulini athenjiwe okukhona kuwona iKaizer Chiefs .
Nokho itshe seligaya ngomunye umhlathi njengoba sezihluleka ukucosha amaphuzu agcwele .
ISwallows isidlale ngokulingana emidlalweni eyisihlanu yeligi ilandelana nakuba ingayazi induku kwengu - 17 kwiPremiership .
UTruter uveze ukuthi abaqeqeshi bamaqembu sebeyalazi " ikhubalo " lakhe .
" Iqembu libukeka liphephile ezembeni .
Manje sesiqala umjikelezo wokugcina walo mjaho .
Kufanele siqhamuke namasu amasha esizowasebenzisa eqenjini ngoba abantu sebeyibonile indlela esilihlela ngayo iqembu futhi bayakusebenzisa lokho .
Uyabona ngesibalo semidlalo esiyidlala ngokulingana .
Ngokwamaqhinga sekuqala ukuba nzima .
Kodwa kumnandi , kwenza ucabange ujule .
Awukwazi ukuthembela ekutheni unjena futhi izinto uzenza ngendlela ethize .
Kufanele kube khona esikwenzayo ezimeni ezithize emidlalweni .
Kodwa kumnandi .
Akukwenzi unethezeke , " kusho uTruter .
ISwallows izovakashela iTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ( TTM ) emdlalweni weLast 16 yeNedbank Cup ePeter Mokaba Stadium , ePolokwane , kusasa ngo - 6 ntambama .
" Wumdlalo onzima esizowudlala neTTM .
Angicabangi ukuthi iseyiqembu elifanayo nesidlale nalo ekuqaleni kwesizini .
Badlala kahle .
Ngicabanga ukuthi manje sebewine imidlalo emithathu ilandelana .
Ngakho kuzoba wumdlalo onzima .
Abadlali babukeka bezelwe kabusha ngaphansi kwabaphathi abasha .
Bafuna ukudlala .
Kunabadlali abasezingeni eliphezulu abangawushintsha umdlalo .
Kuzoba nezinguquko esikimini sethu , kodwa hhayi ngoba siwuthatha kancane lo mqhudelwano noma siwuthatha njengento engekho phambili kithina .
Sifuna ukwenza kahle kuyona yonke imidlalo kungakhathalekile ukuthi yiligi noma yindebe .
Sizobophela abadlali abangu - 11 abakhona , " kusho uTruter .
I - TTM , esinabaphathi abasha , izintambo kuyona zisabanjwe uDavid Mathebula noMpho Makola njengoba uDylan Kerr esalinde imvume yokusebenza kuleli .
I - UEFA isongela amaqembu ezimpunyela aqala iSuper League
INHLANGANO ephethe ibhola e - Europe , i - UEFA , isisongele amaqembu ezimpunyela ase - Europe asememezele ukuthi azoba yingxenye ye - European Super League ( ESL ) ngokuthi bazowakhipha kuyo yonke imincintiswano engaphansi kwe - UEFA .
NgeSonto , amaqembu ahamba phambili e - Europe athuse iziphathimandla zebhola ngokunjalo nabalandeli ememezela izinhlelo zomncintiswano omusha ozobizwa nge - ESL .
Kulawo maqembu kubalwa ayisithupha ase - England ( Manchester United , Manchester City , Liverpool , Arsenal , Chelsea , neTottenham Hotspur ) , amathathu ase - Italy ( Juventus , Inter Milan , AC Milan ) , namanye amathathu ase - Spain ( Barcelona , Real Madrid , Athletico Madrid ) .
Onke lawa maqembu ajoyina i - ESL njengabasunguli , kanti uma isiqalile ngeke agawulwe yizembe futhi ngeke adinge ukuhlungela ukudlala kuyo minyaka yonke .
Ngokwemibiko yamaphephandaba ezemidlalo e - Europe , kuvela ukuthi iBayern Munich neDortmund banqabile ukuba yingxele yale ligi , okwamanje .
NePSG yaseFrance , equkethe abadlali abaphambili emhlabeni , kuvela ukuthi isaziqhathulula , kayifuni ukumataniswa nalo mncintiswano .
I - Juventus ibe yiqembu lokuqala ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izobe idlala kwi - ESL abathemba ukuthi izoqala ngesizini ezayo .
Iphendula lezi zindaba i - UEFA nezinhlangano ezengamele amaligi emazweni ase - Europe , bathe bazokwenza konke okusemandleni ukuvimba lo mncintiswano .
" Sizobheka konke esingakwenza ngokomthetho wezinkantolo ngokunjalo nangokomthetho wezemidlalo .
Ingqikithi yebhola isekubeni khona kokuncintisana kumdlalo , akukwazi ukuba okunye , " kusho UEFA esitatimendeni .
Ithe amaqembu azoba yingxenye ye - ESL azovalelwa ngaphandle kuyo yonke imincintiswano ye - EUFA yamaqembu okubalwa kuyo i - UEFA Champions League ( UCL ) ne - Europa League .
I - UEFA isongela kanjena nje kuyimanje iManchester City , Real Madrid neChelsea bakuma - semifinal e - UCL .
Kwi - Europa League nakhona kubusa amaqembu afuna ukudlala kwi - ESL njengoba kuma - semifinal kukhona iManchester United ne - Arsenal .
Ngaphandle kokuvalelwa ngaphandle kule mncintiswano , i - UEFA ithe abadlali abagijima kuleli qembu bangase banqatshelwe ukudlalela amaqembu esizwe .
Kuphinde kwayibhimbela i - Arrows ibanjelwa ekhaya
ILAMONTVILLE Golden Arrows iphinde yahluleka ukubuyela emgqigqweni wayo eqale ngawo isizini ibanjwa yiBaroka emdlalweni weDStv Premiership eSugar Ray Xulu Stadium , eClermont , izolo ntambama .
I - Arrows , ehlulwe okwesibili kule sizini emidlalweni yeligi iqunjwa phansi yiBlack Leopards ngesonto eledlule , bekulindeleke ukuthi ibuyise umfutho wayo oholele ekutheni idlale imidlalo engu - 11 ingahlulwa kule sizini .
Umgqigqo omuhle we - Arrows unyomfwe yiCape Town City emasontweni adlule .
Izolo kuphinde kwacaca ukuthi Abafana Bes'thende badonsa kanzima ukubuyisa umfutho abaqale ngawo isizini oholele ekutheni baphenduke elinye lamaqembu esatshwayo kwiPremiership .
IBaroka iyona ezinze kuqala , yangena iphindelela ebhokisini le - Arrows .
Nokho udonga lwasemuva lwe - Arrows luphumelele ukuyichiliza yonke iminyakazo .
Unozinti waBafana Bes'thende , uSifiso Mlungwana , utakule ezakhe echithela ngaphandle i - free kick ebiyingozi kaJoslin Kamatuka ngomzuzu ka - 12 .
Emuva kwalokho , i - Arrows iyibonile ingozi eyicathamelayo , yaqala yangena emdlalweni .
Nokho awekho amathuba abephakamisa amaphaphu kwazise iminyakazo eminingi iphelele odongeni lwasemuva lweBaroka .
Esiwombeni sesibili , iBaroka ibuye nomfutho ofanayo neqale ngawo umdlalo , yafaka ingcindezi kwi - Arrows .
Nokho Abafana Bes'thende ngokuhamba kwesikhathi bakushintshile konke lokho , bangena ngawo wonke amazibuko befuna igoli .
Kodwa ke kucacile ukuthi iBaroka isebenzela ukuphuma nephuzu ngesikhathi unozinti wayo u - Oscarine Masuluke eselala phansi , enza sengathi ulimele , nobekuyimizamo yokuhambisa isikhathi .
I - Arrows ibilokhu izame njalo ukuthola igoli kodwa kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya .
Womabili amaqembu agcine ehlomule ngephuzu .
Komunye umdlalo weligi obuyizolo eSisa Dukashe Stadium , eMdantsane , iChippa United neCape Town City nabo bashayane baze babukana umdlalo uphela ngo 0 - 0 .

UMoseamedi uthemba umgqigqo wasekhaya weTeam of Choice
SITHEMBISO MKHIZELIMNIKA ithemba irekhodi lakamuva lokwenza kahle ekhaya , uJudas Moseamedi ongenye yezinsika zeMaritzburg United ephoqwa isimo ukunqoba kwiBaroka , kusasa , ngo - 5 ntambama , eHarry Gwala Stadium .
Ngenxa yokwazi isimo iqembu elibhekene naso , lo mgadli osashaye amagoli amane kule sizini yeDStv Premiership , uthe sebekudlulisile emqondweni ukushaywa kwabo i - Orlando Pirates ngo 2 - 0 kodlule .
Kuyabaphoqa ukuthi bawathole womathathu amaphuzu kwiBaroka ukuze basuke emsileni .
" Sisenalo ithuba lokusuka kule ndawo esikuyo .
Ngeke kusize ngalutho ukulahla ithemba .
Noma sidliwe kodlule kodwa kuyathokozisa ukubona ozakwethu benokuzethemba , begqugquzekile futhi kunokumamatheka ebusweni babo .
Ukudlalela ekhaya kwenza kube lula ukwehlula iBaroka .
Kumele senze isiqiniseko sokuthi siyaqhubeka nokungehlulwa ekhaya , " kubeka uMoseamedi .
Emidlalweni emithathu yakamuva , eHarry Gwala Stadium , iTeam of Choice , eqeqeshwa u - Ernst Middendorp , ishaye ngo - 1 - 0 iBlack Leopards , yabambana ngo - 1 - 1 neKaizer Chiefs , kowokugcina yabhaxabula iChippa United ngo - 5 - 1 .
Ihleli endaweni ka - 13 kwi - log ngamaphuzu awu - 20 , emidlalweni ewu - 21 .
Uma isafuna ukudlala kwiDStv Premiership ngesizini ezayo kumele kule midlalo eyisishiyagalolunye eyisalele igweme ukulahla amaphuzu .
Okungayiduduza ukuthi iphethe esandleni umdlalo kwiLeapords esekugcineni ngamaphuzu awu - 13 , nemibili kwiChippa United anamaphuzu awu - 17 .
Nokushaywa kweChippa United yiBaroka , ngoLwesibili , akubuzwa ukuthi kuzijabulisile azikaMoseamedi .
AmaChilli Boys abambe unombolo - 13 ngamaphuzu awu - 19 .
UMoseamedi uthe balindele umdlalo onzima kwiBaroka .
" Uma ubheka imiphumela yemidlalo yakamuva yeBaroka uyabona ukuthi bayiqembu elidlala kahle .
NakoweChippa , batshengisile ukuthi bayiqembu elinzima .
Okwethu okuzilungiselela ngokuphelele .
" Ukunqoba kweBaroka , ngoLwesibili kuyibeke endaweni yesishiyagalombili .
UGoodman Mosele oshaye igoli lokunqoba iChippa maqede waqokwa njengomdlali wosuku , uthe : " Iseyinde indlela , lesi yisiqalo .
NgoLwesihlanu sinomdlalo onzima neMaritzburg , uma singaphinde sithole amaphuzu amathathu kungaba lula ukubheka phambili .
" Kusasa iTeam of Choice izobe ilwela ukubuyisa izinduku kwiBaroka .
Emlenzeni wokuqala yashaywa ngo - 2 - 1 ekuhambeni .
UGcaba ubona iCosmos isenethuba embangweni wesicoco seGladAfrica
STHEMBISO NGOBESEISITOBHA seJomo Cosmos , u - Ayanda Gcaba , sibona besenalo ithuba lokufica amanye amaqembu aphezulu kwi - log yeGladAfrica Championship .
UGcaba usho kanje ngaphambi kokuba ezakhe zibhekane noThongathi FC emdlalweni ozokuba ngoMgqibelo ngo - 3 .
30 ntambama ePrincess Magogo Stadium , KwaMashu .
ICosmos eqeqeshwa ngumnikazi wayo u - Ephraim " Jomo " Sono , iyiqale ngegiya eliphezulu isizini ka - 2020 / 2021 , kepha kamuva kubukeka izinto zingayihambeli kahle njengoba ilahla amaphuzu .
Ngempelasonto edlule ikhale ngaphansi kwiTS Sporting ishaywa ngo 3 - 1 , eTsakane Stadium .
Ukwehlulwa kwayo kuyishovele kunombolo - 11 .
Inamaphuzu awu - 20 emidlalweni ewu - 16 .
Ngakolunye uhlangothi , uThongathi olucijwa nguPitso Dladla , luzoya kulo mdlalo luhambela phezulu njengoba luguqise ngo 2 - 0 iCape Umoya United , eKapa .
AmaCane Cutters asendaweni yesishiyagalolunye ngamaphuzu angu - 21 emidlalweni engu - 15 .
UGcaba uvumile ukuthi ayibajabulisi neze indawo abakuyo manje , kwi - log .
" Isimo esikuso kwi - log asisihle neze futhi akusijabulisi kodwa kuzomele sikuguqule ngokushesha ukuze sibuyele embangweni wesicoco seligi .
" Nakuba ngingafuni ukuzwakala njengomuntu obeka izaba kodwa imbangela enkulu yokungenzi kahle kwethu emidlalweni yakamuva , kube wukulimala kwabanye abadlali abamqoka beqembu kanti abanye bebesezigwebeni zamakhadi nokuyinto ephamazise umgqigqo iqembu eliqale ngawo isizini , " usho kanje uGcaba owayegijima kwiFree State Stars nakwi -
Orlando Pirates kumasizini edlule .
Lo mdlali uqhube wathi : " Ngicabanga ukuthi ukubuya kwabanye abadlali kuzokwenza iqembu lethu liqine kakhulu .
Nakuba okwamanje sihlezi endaweni engeyinhle kodwa ngokubona kwami sisenalo ithuba lokuwafica amaqembu aphezulu .
Okuzomele sikwenze nje wukuthi siqinisekise ukuthi siyayinqoba imidlalo yethu ezayo .
Ngicabanga futhi ukuthi uma singanqoba imidlalo emibili kulandelana lokhu kungenza umehluko omkhulu kakhulu kwi - log .
" Ngesikhathi iCosmos igcina ukuhlangana noThongathi kwiligi ngoDisemba , kwanqoba iCane Cutters ngo 1 - 0 .
