Umpetha ka - 400m usebheke ukungena kuma - Olympics
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUZIBONA engakwazi ukungena eqenjini elizomela elakuleli kuma - Olympic Games , uZakithi Nene , ojabulise abathandi bezokusubatha baKwaZulu - Natal enqoba indondo yegolide ku - 400m kuma - ASA Senior Track and Field + Combined Events & 20km Championships aphothulwe ePitoli ngempelasonto .
Kulo mqhudelwano obushisa phansi , uZakithi oqeqeshwa uVictor Vaz , ushaye intambo ngesikhathi esiwu - 45 . 54 .
Isibili sithathwe uLottering Darll wasesifundeni i - Eastern Province Athletics ( EPA ) noConrade Pieter we - Athletics Central Northwest ( ACN ) .
Ama - Olympics azokuba seTokyo , eJapan ngoJulayi .
Isikhathi esibekelwe ukungena kuma - Olympics ka - 2021 ku - 400m u - 44 : 90 .
UNene utshele Isolezwe ukuthi ukunqoba indondo ezingeni likazwelonke kungenye yempumelelo angasoze ayikhohlwa empilweni yakhe .
" Ngibonga kakhulu kumqeqeshi wami nasemndenini wami ngokuhlale bengeseka .
Ukunqoba emqhudelwaneni obusePitoli , ngishiya abantu abafana noLottering noPieter kuyinto enkulu kimina .
Ngicabanga ukuthi siyiKwaZulu - Natal kukhulu ebesingakwenza kodwa sizamile .
Ingijabulisile indlela esidlale ngayo .
Njengamanje isifiso sami ukumela izwe lami kuma - Olympics .
Nomqeqeshi wami nabobonke abangiphethe sisazohlala phansi sibone ukuthi lokhu sikuhlela kanjani .
Ikusasa liyakhanya kubasubathi bakithi , isifiso ukubona abasubathi baKwaZulu - Natal begcwala emaqenjini esizwe .
Ngithanda nokubongela uMathanga ( Mbuleli ) nabanye ngobungcweti abutshengisile enqoba ku - 10 000m , " kuchaza uNene .
Lo msubathi odabuka eMnambithi uhambela phezulu kulezi zinsuku kulandela ukuthi eqokelwe eqenjini lesizwe le - relay eliya kumaWorld Athletics Relay ePoland angoMeyi 1 - 2 .
" NasePoland ngithembisa ngokuqhubeka nokusebenza kahle .
Kuzoba nzima , kodwa ngizolwa , kungamane kunqamuke izinyawo .
" USteve Mkasi ongumengameli weKwaZulu - Natal Athletics ( KZNA ) uthe beyithimba bajabule kakhulu .
" Lesi yisiqalo , kukhulu kuyeza .
Sisazohlangana sibone ukuthi abasubathi bethu sibajabulisa kanjani .
Kumele sivumelane ngokuthi sibakhuthaza kanjani , siyaziqhenya ngabo .
Sifisa ukuthi babe khona abazomela elakuleli kuma - Olympics , " kubeka uMkasi . Abanye abanqobile : 100m ( M ) : Akani Simbine 100m ( W ) : Reabetse Moloi 200m ( M ) : Wayde van Niekerk 200m ( W ) : Justine Palframan 400m ( W ) : Deline Mpiti 400mh ( M ) : Le Roux Heimman 400mh ( W ) :

UMazinyo uyaziqhenya ngokutakula iMaritzburg
XOLILE MPISANEUMQEQESHI weMaritzburg United , u - Ernst Middendorp , uthi ukuvala ngqi emuva ikhona okubasizile ukuthi baphephe engozini yokudliwa yizembe .
I - Team of Choice ingene emdlalweni wokusonga isizini , ewudlale nomkhaya AmaZulu , idinga iphuzu ukuze ingazifaki engcupheni yokudlala kweyokuhlunga .
Emva kokungenisa amagoli amabili bedlala neSuperSport United , uMiddendorp uthe baqhamuke neqhinga elenze bagcine bebambene noSuthu ngo - 0 - 0 , baqeda endaweni ka - 13 ngamaphuzu awu - 30 .
" Ngiyasazi isimo ukuthi besinjani ekuqaleni kukaDisemba .
Emva kwemidlalo eyisithupha , besingenawo amaphuzu .
Emva kweyisishiyagalombili , besinamaphuzu amabili kuphela kwawu - 24 ebesesiwadlalelile .
Siqede imidlalo ewu - 15 , okunguhhafu wesizini , sinamaphuzu ayisishiyagalolunye kuphela , kodwa manje sesiphethe isizini ngawu - 30 , " kusho uMiddendorp .
" Sikhethe ukungena kulo mdlalo wokugcina nezitobha ezine emuva .
Bezingakhuphuki nakancane futhi zingavuli izikhala phakathi kwazo .
Zidlale ngokubambisana nabadlali ababili ebesiqinise ngabo isisu .
" Ngesikhathi silungiselela uSuthu besibheke kakhulu ukuthi sidlale ngokusondelana , silekelelane , singazivuli izikhala ngasebhokisini lethu .
" Besithi sizobathola kuma - free - kick namakhona noma silinde benze amaphutha bese siyabazuma ngejubane .
Siwatholile amathuba amabili noma amathathu .
Ukuba sidlale ngobuhlakani phambili besizolishaya igoli , sithole nomphumela obungalindelwe muntu .
" Kodwa - ke AmaZulu enze kahle kakhulu ngokuqeda endaweni ewafaka kwiChampions League .
Iwona abewuphethe umdlalo imizuzu yonke ewu - 95 , kodwa ekugcineni sawabamba ngo - 0 - 0 ngenxa yokuzikhandla .
" UMiddendorp uthe kumele bazishayele ihlombe ngokutakula leli qembu emva kokuthi lihlale emsileni isikhathi eside kwisizini ka - 2020 / 21 .
" Kuyamangalisa esikwenzile .
Asingenanga kwiChampions League , asisiwinanga isicoco seligi noma enye indebe .
Sahlulwa ekhaya emdlalweni wokugcina womzuliswano wokuqala , sibambe ibhuleki , kodwa manje sisindile ezembeni , asidinganga nokudlala kweyokuhlunga .
Kumele siziqhenye , sincome abadlali ngabakwenzile , nawo wonke umuntu odlale indima ekutheni sigcine siphumelele . "
UMulenga ukhalima ozakwabo ngaphambi kowe'Downs
UMGADLI waMaZulu , u - Augustine Mulenga , ugcizelela eyokugwema amaphutha kozakwabo uma sebebhekene neMamelodi Sundowns koweDStv Premiership eJonsson Kings Park Stadium namhlanje ngo - 3 ntambama .
Usuthu , oludlala ingcwenga yebhola ngaphansi komqeqeshi uBenni McCarthy , luthwele amathemba enqwaba yamaqembu kwiPremiership okuthi luvimbe iSundowns ingavuli igebe elikhulu lamaphuzu esicongweni .
Ukudlubulundela kusemanje kweSundowns kungasho ukushabalala kwamathuba okuwina isicoco kwamanye amaqembu asakholwa wukuthi awukapheli umjaho .
ISundowns enemidlalo ewu - 20 , iqhwakele ngamaphuzu awu - 46 .
Ilandelwa AmaZulu aseqoqe amaphuzu awu - 40 emidlalweni ewu - 22 .
" Engingakugcizelela kozakwethu wukuthi singawenzi amaphutha amaningi ngoba bengasihlula ngawo .
Uma singabenza ukuthi bona benze amaphutha , nginesiqiniseko sokuthi sizoqoqa amaphuzu amathathu .
Kufanele nje sigweme ukwenza amaphutha amaningi .
Sonke sisebenza kanzima futhi siwubheke ngabomvu lo mdlalo neSundowns ngoba wumdlalo omkhulu .
Amaphuzu amathathu azosisondeza kubona ngoba basesicongweni se - log , " kusho uMulenga .
ISundowns ayikaze ihlulwe emdlalweni weligi kule sizini .
Ithole isibhaxu kwiMTN 8 , CAF Champions League nakwiNedbank Cup ekhishwe kuyona yiTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ( TTM ) sekushaywa amaphenathi ngempelasonto edlule .
Imimoya iphansi ekhempini yamaBrazilians ngenxa yalokhu .
Umqeqeshi wamaBrazilians , uManqoba Mngqithi , uthe ithimba elisiza ekululameni kwabadlali lisebenza kanzima ngenxa yokuthi bafinyelele esikhathini esengeziwe neTshakhuma ekubeni bevele benemidlalo ethothene .
" Ukuba besazi ukuthi sizohlulwa , bekungaba ngcono ukuthi kwenzeke lokho emizuzwini engu - 90 .
Kodwa akusekho ongakwenza ngakho .
Abadlali bethu bayazi ukuthi banomthwalo kuyona yonke le midlalo futhi sidlala yonke le midlalo ngenxa yempumelelo yabo .
Ukuba bekungenjalo ngabe nathi sidlala imidlalo embalwa njangamanye amaqembu esidlala nawo .
Kodwa ngoba bayaqhubeka nokwenza kahle , kufanele bamelane nomphumela walokho .
Siyakwazi okusimele .
Siyakwazi okuzokwenzeka eThekwini .
Ngeke kube wumdlalo olula kodwa kufanele silwe .
Ithimba lethu elibhekele isimo sabadlali lisebenza kanzima ukwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi abadlali bethu basesimeni sokuya emdlalweni naMaZulu , benze okulindelekile kubona , " kusho uMngqithi .
Umdlalo womzuliswano wokuqala weligi wala maqembu waphela ngo - 4 - 3 kunqoba iSundowns .
Imidlalo yeDStv Premiership : Namuhla : Ngo - 3:00 PM : Chippa United v Baroka ( Nelson Mandela Bay Stadium ) .
Ngo - 5:00 PM : Bloemfontein Celtic v Swallows ( Dr Petrus Molemela Stadium ) .
Kusasa : Ngo - 3:00 PM : Black Leopards v Stellenbosch ( 3:00 PM , Thohoyandou Stadium ) ; AmaZulu v Mamelodi Sundowns ( Jonsson Kings Park ) .
Ngo - 5:00 PM : Kaizer Chiefs v Cape Town City ( FNB Stadium ) ; SuperSport United v Lamontville Golden Arrows ( Lucas Moripe Stadium ) .
OweSekhukhune ufuna ukufaka ingcindezi ngombango wesicoco
STHEMBISO NGOBESEUMQEQESHI weSekhukhune United , uMacDonald Makhubedu , uthi akukho ukwenza ngokunye ngaphandle kokuqhubeka nokuwaqoqa egcwele amaphuzu ukuze baqhubeke nokushubisa umbango wesicoco kwiGladAfrica Championship .
UMakhubedu ukhulume kanje ngemuva kokuba ezakhe ziphunyuke ngembobo yenaliti ngesikhathi ziguqisa ngo - 1 - 0 iFree State Stars emdlalweni wamaphuzu obuseMakhulong Stadium , eTembisa ngempelasonto .
Igoli leSekhukhune libekwe enethini nguThabang Sibanyoni ngomzuzu ka - 67 esiwombeni sesibili .
Ukunqoba kweSekhukhune kuqhubekile nokuyibeka endaweni yesibili kwi - log ngamaphuzu angu - 27 emidlalweni engu - 16 .
IRichards Bay FC isazihola phambili ngamaphuzu angu - 28 .
Ngempelasonto , iBay eqeqeshwa nguSimo Dladla , iyekele ithuba elihle lokuvula igebe kwi - log njengoba idlale ngokulingana ngo - 0 - 0 neBizana Pondo Chiefs , eKing Zwethini Stadium , eMlaza .
" Sijabule kakhulu ngokuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele kulo mdlalo nakuba bekunzima kwazise besidlala neqembu elikwaziyo ukuvala emuva , ngaphezu kwalokho baqeqeshwa ngu - Allan Freese ongomunye wabaqeqeshi asebenamava kakhulu ebholeni lakuleli .
" Emidlalweni yethu elandelayo kumele siqhubeke futhi nokuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele ukuze siqhubeke nokufaka ingcindezi kwiBay ( Richards ) okuyiyona ehlezi phezulu kwi - log njengamanje , " kusho uMakhubedu .
USiyabulela Shai , odlala esiswini kwiSekhukhune , yena uthe bekubafanele ukuwunqoba umdlalo wabo neStars kwazise basebenze kanzima .
" Ngemuva kokulahla amaphuzu emidlalweni yethu edlule , sizitshele ukuthi lona kumele siwunqobe kumnyama kubomvu , nangempela sikwenzile lokho .
Siyajabula ukuthi sikwazile ukunqoba lapha , " kusho uShai oqokwe njengomdlali ovelele kulo mdlalo .
NgoMgqibelo , iSekhukhune izobuyela enkundleni iyobhekana ne - University of Pretoria emdlalweni ongo - 3 .
30 ntambama e - Absa Tuks Stadium , ePitoli .
Kuzothatha isikhathi ukuhlanganisa iBafana
UMGADLI weBafana Bafana , uPercy Tau , uyibona izothatha isikhathi impumelelo ngaphansi komqeqeshi omusha , uHugo Broos , oshaye ngesithende ' amakhehla ' esikwatini sakhe .
UTau , ogijima kwiBrighton & Hove Albion kwi - English Premier League , e - England , ngomunye wabadlali abambalwa abasinde ezembeni likaBroos okubeke kwacaca ukuthi okudlisa iBafana wukuthi inabadlali abaningi abaneminyaka engaphezu kuka - 30 .
Kubadlali abamqoka abasale ngaphandle esikwatini sokuqala sikaBroos kukhona ukaputeni uThulani Hlatshwayo , Bongani Zungu , Dean Furman , Sifiso Hlanti nabanye .
IBafana izodlala ne - Uganda emdlalweni wobungani ngoJuni 10 .
Ebhentshini leBafana kuzohlala amaphini kaBroos uCedomir Janevski noHelman Mkhalele .
" Kuhlala kukhulunywa uma kufika umqeqeshi omusha noma izinto zingahambanga kahle .
Siyashintshwa isikwati .
Abadlali abadala yibona abadliwa yizembe .
Kodwa ke yisinqumo somqeqeshi .
Kuhlukile ngoba kunabadlali esengidlale nabo isikhathi eside , manje ukubakhipha nje kanjalo , ufake abasha , kuzothatha isikhathi ( ukuhlangana kweqembu ) .
Kungcono ngoba sinalo mdlalo wobungani esizowusebenzisa ukuzama ukuhlangana ngaphambi kowokuhlungela oweNdebe yoMhlaba ( ngoSepthemba ) .
Kodwa kunzima ngoba nami ngineminyaka engu - 27 okusho ukuthi nami ngiyalandela .
Sizobheka ukuthi umqeqeshi omusha ufuna senzeni nokuthi ufuna sidlale kanjani .
Kodwa ngiyathemba ukuthi kuzoba ngcono , " kusho uTau .
Emuva kokubolekiswa kwi - Union SG , Club Brugge yaseBelgium ne - Anderlecht , uTau ugcine ebuyele kwiBrighton eyamsayinisa edlala kwiMamelodi Sundowns ngo - 2018 .
KwiSea Gulls udlale imidlalo emithathu kusukela ebuyele kuyona ngoJanuwari .
Nokho uTau , oseholidini kuleli njengoba kuvalwe isizini , uthe uzohlala alwele indawo yakhe kwiBrighton wathi eyokubolekiswa ayikakhulunywa .
" Angicabangi ukuthi kukhona ofuna ukwenza lokho okwamanje .
Ngisahlale izinyanga eziyisithupha kwiBrighton .
Uma bengibolekisa kuzobe kuyini isizathu ngoba angidlalanga imidlalo eyanele .
Ngakho ngibheke ukulwela indawo yami .
Yileyo inhloso yami futhi mina neqembu sisabona kanjalo .
Iqembu lisafuna ngihlale ngidlale .
Nami ngifuna ukulwela indawo yami .
Kuhlala kuthiwa ikusasa alaziwa .
Kodwa okwamanje sobabili siyavumelana ngokuthi ngizohlala ngilwele indawo yami , " kusho uTau .
Kunconywa uNcikazi noKhenyeza ngomlando oqoshiwe
XOLILE MPISANEOWAYEGIJIMA kwiLamontville Golden Arrows , uMzuvukile Tom , uthi ubudlelwano obuhle phakathi komqeqeshi , uMandla Ncikazi , nomsizi wakhe , uMabhuti Khenyeza , yibona obenze leli qembu liqophe umlando kule sizini ephelile .
Abafana Bes'thende baqede endaweni yesine kwiDStv Premiership , nokuyindawo ephezulu kunazo zonke selokhu bangena esigabeni esikhulu .
U - Tom , owadlala imidlalo engu - 168 kwi - Arrows , uthe bekusobala ukuthi laba baqeqeshi bayimbumba , nokwenze leli qembu lidlale into ehlangene .
" Izinto ze - Arrows ngicabanga ukuthi zilunge ingakaqali nesizini .
Ngiyazi besisincane isikhathi sokucija abadlali ngaphambi kokuthi isizini iqale kodwa kuyacaca ukuthi kuningi okuhle abakwenza okube nomthelela ekutheni bayiqale kahle isizini , " kusho uTom .
" Ngingaphinde ngimncome uNcikazi nabaphathi beqembu ngokuthi babuyise uKhenyeza azolekelela umqeqeshi .
UKhenyeza uyayazi futhi uyayithanda i - Arrows .
Ungumuntu ozimiselayo futhi okuzondayo ukuhlulwa .
Kusobala ukuthi lokhu ukudlulisele kubadlali .
Ngingasho ukuthi noNcikazi unomqondo ofanayo .
" Indlela uNcikazi noKhenyeza abasebenzisane ngayo kule sizini ibiyinhle kakhulu .
Izithelo bezibonakala enkundleni ngendlela leli qembu ebelidlala ngayo .
Abadlali bebengadideki ngoba bebetshelwa izinto ezihambisanayo .
Indlela abebeshesha ngayo ukuliwina ibhola , baphinde bahlasele ngesivinini , ibikhombisa ukuthi bebezimisela ejimini .
" Lo mdlali , owayegijima emuva ohlangothini lwesinxele , uqoke unozinti , uSifiso Mlungwana , nesitobha , uNkosinathi Sibisi , njengabadlali abamchaze kakhulu .
" Ngizoqala ngoMlungwana ngoba ekuqaleni kwesizini ngangingamthembile neze .
Ngangibona sengathi wondlekile , ngithi lokho kuzomphazamisa emsebenzini wakhe .
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ngibonile ukuthi cishe yindlela adalwe ngayo ngoba akukho obekukhombisa ukuthi uyivila .
Usebenze kakhulu kule sizini , " kuqhuba uTom .
" Ngeke ngikwazi ukumshiya ngaphandle ukaputeni uSibisi ohole leli qembu ngendlela emangalisayo .
Ubengenavalo , engena shi empini noma kunzima .
Akasukile kakhulu egadeni kodwa indlela abegxuma ngayo awine amabhola ahamba phezulu ingihlabe umxhwele .
" Ngiyabancoma nabadlali abancane abafike eqenjini elikhulu bangakhombisa ukwesaba .
Ngaphambilini bekuthi uma kukhushulwe abadlali abaphuma enkulisa yeqembu kuthathe isikhathi ukuthi bajwayele kodwa laba bangene khaxa .
" Echaza ngokumele kwenziwe yi - Arrows ukuze lingehli izinga ngesizini ezayo , uTom uthe : " Ibhola liyagingqika ngakho - ke akumele uthembele kwisizini edlule .
Kuningi okuhle abangaqhubeka nakho kodwa futhi bayabadinga abadlali abathathu noma abane abazoqinisa isikwati .
" Kubalulekile ukuthi umdlali nomdlali angakhululeki kakhulu endaweni yakhe , azi ukuthi kukhona omunye olambele ukudlala .
Wonke amaqembu aphumelelayo enza kanjalo . "
Owe - TTM uyigeze ubebebe iDowns beyiwashisa ijezi
IMAMELODI Sundowns iphazamise amathuba eChippa United ikhishwa yiTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ( TTM ) kowandulela owamanqamu weNedbank Cup eLoftus Versfeld Stadium , ePitoli , izolo ntambama .
AmaBrazilians abuyiselwe kwamhlaba , nje bekulindeleke ukuthi azidlele amahlanga kwiTTM kulandela ukuziphuzela kwi - Orlando Pirates kuma - quarterfinal ngesonto eledlule .
Ukunqoba kwawo bekuzosho ukuqhubeka nethuba lezindondo ezintathu kule sizini .
Manje asesele nokulwela ukuvikela isicoco seDStv Premiership nokunqoba iCaf Champions League asengene kuyo kuma - quarterfinal .
Ukuphumelela kweTTM kusho nokuphela kwethemba leChippa ebikade ibona ithuba lokungena ingasebenzanga kwiCAF Confederation Cup ngesizini ezayo uma iNedbank Cup igcina inqotshwe iSundowns ebukeka izovikela iligi ibuyele kwiCaf Champions League .
Ngokujwayelekile iqembu elinqoba iNedbank Cup lingena kwiConfederation Cup kodwa iChippa ibingangena noma ingawunqobanga lo mqhudelwano ukube ibizodlala neSundowns .
IChippa sekufanele izilwele yona uma isibhekene neTTM kowamanqamu ngoMeyi 8 enkundleni ezomenyezelwa namuhla .
Iqembu elizowina lizojoyina elizoqeda endaweni yesithathu kwiDStv Premiership kwiConfederation Cup .
Emdlalweni wayizolo iSundowns iqale umdlalo idlala ngokukhululeka , iphatha ibhola ngendlela eyithandayo .
Nokho abadlali beTshakhuma bebezama ngayo yonke indlela ukuyincisha amathuba okungena ebhokisini .
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi iTTM ivulele injeje , eholele ekutheni kuphakame imimoya ebhentshini leSundowns .
Emuva kwalokho iTTM iqalile ukudlala , yaphatha ibhola .
Nokho ibihluleka ukwakha amathuba acacile okushaya amagoli , ngaphandle kwamafree - kick abengaphandle kwebhokisi .
Esiwombeni sesibili , iSundowns ibuye ngomfutho .
USiphelele Mkhulise ucishe wayibeka phambili edlulisa ibhola kunozinti weTTM , uWashington Arubi , kodwa walikhipha seliyongena u - Alfred Ndengane .
ISundowns iqhubekile nokungqongqoza kodwa ibingafuni lutho iTshakhuma .
Kwale noma sekuyiwa esikhathini esengeziwe , alikho iqembu elivume ukugoba uphondo , zagcina zihlukaniswe amaphenathi .
U - Arubi ubala ukhasha emapalini njengoba egeze namagoli abesefane nabaliwe , okukhona nelikaSibusiso Vilakazi .
Noma sekukhahlelwa amaphenathi la maqembu abengafuni ukwenza izinto zibe lula njengoba bonke abadlali abayisihlanu iqembu ngalinye bewavalele phakathi .
Ibhimbi kube ngukaputeni weSundowns , uHlompho Kekana iphenathi yakhe evinjwe ngu - Arubi .
Bese kusemahlombe kaThembisani Nevhulamba ukufaka iTTM kowamanqamu , nembala wangaphoxa wayivalela phakathi .
OweGalaxy ukhale ngonompempe behlulwa
STHEMBISO NGOBESEUMQEQESHI weTS Galaxy , u - Owen da Gama , ukhala ngezinqumo zonompempe njengoba iqembu lakhe lilokhu liqhubeka nokulahla amaphuzu amqoka emidlalweni yalo yakamuva kwiDStv Premiership .
Ngempelasonto , iThe Rockects ihlulwe ngo - 2 - 0 yiTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila emdlalweni wokubanga amaphuzu obuse - Emirates Airline Park Stadium , eGoli .
Amagoli eTshakhuma eqeqeshwa nguMpho Maleka ngokubambisana noDavid " DVD " Mathebula , abekwe enethini nguBrandon Theron noThabo Rakhale ngokwehlukana kweziwombe .
Ukunqoba kweTTM lapha kuyiphefumulise kancane empini yezembe njengoba isinyukele endaweni ka - 14 ngamaphuzu awu - 19 emidlalweni ewu - 21 .
Ngakolunye uhlangothi , iGalaxy yona isahlezi endaweni yesishiyagalombili ngamaphuzu awu - 26 emidlalweni ewu - 22 .
Lona besekungumdlalo wesithathu weGalaxy ihlulwa kulandelana kwazise ngaphambi komdlalo wayo neTTM , ihlulwe yiMariztburg United ngo - 2 - 0 yaphinde yaguqiswa ngo - 2 - 1 yiBloemfontein Celtic .
Ngemuva komdlalo , uDa Gama uzwakalise ukukhathazeka okukhulu ngendlela onompempe abathatha ngayo izinqumo emidlalweni yabo .
" Njengamanje sibhekene nesimo esinzima kakhulu lapha ekilabhini njengoba imiphumela ingasivumi , ngaphezu kwalokho futhi nezinqumo ezithathwa ngonompempe emidlalweni yethu ziyashaqisa kakhulu .
" Siyawakhanda amathuba futhi siwashaye namagoli kodwa ekugcineni lawo magoli agcine engabalwanga ngezizathu esingazazi .
Impela ziyethusa kakhulu izinqumo ezithathwa ngonompempe enkundleni , " usho kanje uDa Gama .
Lo mqeqeshi uqhube wathi njengoba bephinde behlulwa kuzomele babuyele emuva ukuyolungisa izinto .
" Lona bese kungumdlalo wethu wesithathu sihlulwa kulandelana nokuyinto eqalayo ukwenzeka selokhu ngithathe izintambo zokuqeqesha lapha eqenjini .
Lokhu ngikubona kufaka ingcindezi enkulu kubadlali bami njengoba abanye babo babuye benze amaphutha okungafanele ngabe ayenzeka kubadlali abadlala esigabeni esikhulu .
" Kodwa - ke kuzomele sibuyele emuva siyolungisa izinto , ngaphezu kwalokho futhi kumele siyibongele iTshakhuma ngokunqoba lapha .
" UMaleka uthe isimo abakuso njengamanje kwi - log siyabakhathaza kakhulu kodwa bajabulile ngokuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele kulo mdlalo .
Uthe izinguquko abazenzile esiwombeni sesibili zibe nomthelela omkhulu ekutheni banqobe kulo mdlalo .
Isendalini iTeam of Choice
UKUKHULA ngesivinini esethusayo kwezikweletu kushayisa ngovalo ezikhulwini zeMaritzburg United kangangokuthi sezivule izandla kunoma ngubani ofuna ukuthenga iTeam of Choice .
Lokhu kushiwo ngusihlalo waleli qembu , uFarouk Kadodia , ekhuluma neThe Witness , lapho eveze khona ukuthi ngaphandle kokwamukela ukudayisa , uma kukhona umasipala ozimisele ngokungena ezingxoxweni nabo nalapho abanankinga .
NgokukaKadodia , izikweletu ababhekene nazo zingu - R9 million ( okuyimali abebeyiboleka ukugcina iqembu lisesimeni esilindelekile kwiPSL ) .
Phakathi kwezizathu uKadodia azibekile kugqame ukuphela kukaphawini wemali engena ngokubakhona kwabalandeli enkundleni .
Lokhu kudalwe yiCovid - 19 kusukela ngoMashi 2020 kanti nesivumelwano sabo noMasipala uMsunduzi ( ebese sineminyaka eyisithupha siqhubeka ) asizange sivuselelwe ngaphambi kokuqala isizini esanda kusongwa .
" Ukuvalwa kwezwe kusiphuce imigudu eminingi yemali yize ibingenkulu kodwa bekuzameka .
Ukuvaleka kukaphawini kaMasipala uMsunduzi kusibulele kakhulu nakho .
" Njengakuwona wonke amaqembu inkinga enkulu amaholo abadlali .
Kuthe ukuba ngcono sidedela uRushine de Reuck eya kwiMamelodi Sundowns kodwa ukungabinalo uxhaso njengeChippa United , TS Galaxy , Lamontville Golden Arrows , AmaZulu neRoyal AM ( abathola okuthile komasipala babo ) kusishayile , " kubalisa yena .
U - Kadodia uthe iTeam of Choice bayibona ibiza u - R55 million .
" Kuningi esikuzamile sivula izandla kwabafuna ukuthenga amasheya kodwa iningi beligcina lishaya amakhala ngoba libona ukuthi izibalo zethu azihlangani , ngeke benze inzuzo .
Ngingakusho kugcwale umlomo ukuthi eminyakeni engu - 11 edlule izikhulu zeMaritzburg beziyithwele emahlombe , " kusho uKadodia .
Ethintwa Isolezwe , uthe lolu daba lubucayi kakhulu ukuthi angaludingida ocingweni .
OweChiefs akayizwa eyokupaka ibhasi eGuinea
UMDLALI wasemuva weKaizer Chiefs , uKearyn Baccus , uncamela ukuthi behlulwe behlasela kunokupaka ibhasi uma sebebhekene neHoroya AC koweCAF Champions League .
IChiefs izogijimisana neHoroya yaseGuinea emdlalweni wokugcina wesigaba samaqoqo kaGroup C eGeneral Lansana Conte Stadium , eConakry , ngoMgqibelo ngo - 9 ebusuku .
Kulo mdlalo kufanele kuphume iqembu elizolandela iWydad Casablanca yaseMorocco kuma - quarterfinal .
IChiefs neHoroya bayalingana ngamaphuzu ayisishiyagalombili kwi - log .
Amakhosi adinga ukudlala ngokulingana okunamagoli noma awine ukuze ezodlulela kuma - quarterfinal .
" Ngincamela ukuhlasela ngihlulwe kunokuhlala emuva ngidlale ngokulingana .
Ngakho , ngokwami uma sihlasela ngakho konke , sidlalela ukuwina , akukho okuzosilahlekela , " kusho uBaccus .
" Umoya muhle eqenjini .
Siwulungele umdlalo .
Sifuna ukwenza kahle kwiChampions League njengoba singenzi kahle kwiligi okwamanje .
Siwubheke ngabomvu umdlalo futhi sijabule .
Sibheke uMgqibelo .
" IChiefs ifulathele uMzansi izolo ekuseni nabadlali abangu - 18 .
Ihambe ngaphandle kukanozinti uDaniel Akpeyi , nomgadli uSamir Nurkovic abathole amakhadi abomvu ngesikhathi leli qembu lihlula iWydad ngesonto eledlule .
ULeonardo Castro , obekubhekwe ukuthi atakule Amakhosi , usale kuleli kulandela ukwephuka ikhala eshaya igoli emdlalweni weligi ophele ngo - 2 - 2 neStellenbosch ngoLwesibili .
Uma iChiefs iphumelela ukwehlula iHoroya ekuhambeni , izoba yiqembu lokuqala laseMzansi elenze lokho .
IHoroya isibhekene namaqembu ahlukene akuleli emiqhudelwaneni yeCAF kodwa alikho eselike layishayela ekhaya .
Ngo - 2018 , idlale ngokulingana ngo - 2 - 2 neMamelodi Sundowns esigabeni samaqoqo , kwathi ngo - 2019 , yathela isibhaxu sika - 2 - 1 kwi - Orlando Pirates .
Nyakenye iHoroya ivulele isibhaxu sika - 2 - 1 kwiBidvest Wits esigabeni samaqoqo kwiCAF Confederation Cup .
Emdlalweni wokuqala wesigaba samaqoqo , iChiefs neHoroya badlale ngokulingana ngo - 0 - 0 .
Isitobha seChiefs , uReeve Frosler , sithe umphumela wakamuva weChampions League behlula iWydad ubafaka umfutho nokuzethemba .
" Kubalulekile ukuhlala sigcwele ukuzethemba futhi sikholelwe kwesikwazi ukukwenza .
Sidlala ekuhambeni , kuzoba wumdlalo ohluke kakhulu .
Kufanele sibekezele , sikholelwe kithina ukuthi sizodlulela phambili , " kusho uFrosler .
Kuvela okubhuntshise izingxoxo zeMaritzburg neDowns ngoMabunda
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUNQABE ukubolekiswa kwiMaritzburg United , uTiyani " Shuga " Mabunda olizwa ngendaba ijezi kwiMamelodi Sundowns .
Isolezwe lithole ukuthi iSundowns bese iqede konke neTeam of Choice kodwa lo mdlali oyibamba esiswini washaya phansi ngonyawo , wathi akalibeki eMphithi .
Ngokusho kwalo mthombo osondelene nalo mdlali isizathu esidale ukuthi anqabe wukuthi kwiMaritzburg ubengeke athole imihlomulo agixabezwa yona eChloorkop .
Kuthiwa uMabunda uthe ufuna ukuyiqedela kwiSundowns inkontileka yakhe ephela ekusongweni kwesizini ka - 2020 / 21 .
" UMabunda usekwamukele ukuthi iSundonws ngeke iyivuselele inkontileka yakhe .
Osekumhlalise kuyo yimali .
UFarouk Kadodia ( umnikazi weMaritzburg ) bese eqede konke neSundowns , beyingenankinga ukuthi imdedele .
KwiMaritzburg kubukeka ebezolithola ithuba lokudlala , " kubeka umthombo .
Kuthintwa uKadodia ukuvumile ukuthi bebefuna ukumboleka uMabunda kodwa kwavimba ezinto ezithile .
" Kuliqiniso ukuthi besimgaqele uMabunda ngesikhathi kusavulwe iwindi .
Kuvimbe izinto engingeke ngikwazi ukuzidalula kwabezindaba .
Empeleni angithandi ukuphawula kakhulu ngalolu daba , kumele sikuhloniphe ukuthi uMabunda unenkontilela neSundowns , " kusho uKadodia .
Imizamo yokuthola ukuphawula kweSundowns ayiphumelelanga njengoba lowo okhulumela iqembu uShupi Nkgadima engazange ayiphendule imibuzo athunyelelwe yona .
Ngaphambi kokuqala kwale sizini , iSwallows beyifuna ukuboleka lo mdlali .
Ivinjwe ukuthi beyingeke ikwazi ukumholela imali ayithola kwiSundowns .
Selokhu kuqale isizini , uMabunda owake waba semabhukwini eBlack Leopards nakwaweFree State Stars , ulizwa ngendaba ijezi kwiSundowns .
Ubanga indawo esiswini no - Andile Jali , Hlompho Kekana , noRivaldo Coetzee osuswe emuva wafakwa esiswini .
UMabunda izinto ziqale ukumbhedela ngesizini edlule edlala imidlalo eyisishiyagalolunye kuphela yeDStv Premiership neyisithupha yemiqhudelwano .
Wagcina ukuba nesizini enhle kweka - 2018 / 19 , edlala imidlalo ewu - 22 .
Eminyakeni edlule uke waba ngelinye lamasosha ayeyizithenjwa zikaPitso " Jingles " Mosimane oseqeqesha i - Al Ahly yase - Egypt .
UMabunda usenqobe neSundowns isicoco seCaf Champions League ngo - 2016 , isicoco seDStv Premiership kahlanu , kabili iTelkom Knockout neNedbank Cup ngokuhlukana kwemiqhudelwano .
Ulandwe phesheya ' ozofaka ' iBafana kweyomhlaba
ULANDWE phesheya umqeqeshi ozothwala ijoka elisindayo , lokufaka iBafana Bafana kwi - 2022 Fifa World Cup .
Lokhu bese kunesikhathi kuhlongozwa ngegama lika - Carlos Queiroz , odabuka ePortugal , kodwa kuqale ukuqina sekuhoxa isithangami sabezindaba ebesizoba izolo ngo - 10 ekuseni .
Kulesi sithangami ibigcwele incwadi ukuthi kuzokwethulwa umqeqeshi kwabezindaba nasesizweni kodwa kuvele ukuthi " ngenxa yemigudu yokuhambelana kwamazwe omhlaba ehlukene , ngokwemigomo yeCovid - 19 , umcimbi uhlehlile .
" Isigungu esiphezulu kuzwelonke seSouth African Football Association ( Safa ) sihlanganile izolo emhlanganweni ongabikwangwa kwabezindaba .
Kulo mhlangano Isolezwe ngeSonto litshelwe ngaphambi kwawo yisikhulu esiphelu kwiSafa , uTebogo Motlanthe , ukuthi uzoba khona kodwa kasibange sisatholakala emuva kwawo ukuveza ukuthi kuvunyelwane ngani .
Nokho imithombo yeSolezwe ngeSonto ivezile ukuthi eqinisweni , zikhale kuye uMotlanthe ukuthi akaqikelele ukuthi isonto elisombulukayo lingapheli engathuliwe umqeqeshi .
Kufanele ngoba ngoMeyi 12 iBafana ihlangana neZimbabwe , iqala imidlalo yokuhlungela iWorld Cup eseQatar .
" Ihlanganile iNEC ( isigungu esiphezulu seSafa kuzwelonke ) kwaphuma isinqumo esithi lingapheli isonto ingaphothuliwe indaba yomqeqeshi , " kusho umthombo ongaphakathi kwiSafa .
Umthombo uxinwa ngegama likaQueiroz , okuvele ukuthi umengameli weSafa , uDanny Jordaan ubese zamazamise zonke izinhlaka ukuthi abuyiswe .
" Bahlanu abaqeqeshi obese kudingidwa ngabo , nguHugo Broos , Harve Renard , Benni McCarthy kodwa umgwamanda uvumelane ngoCarlos Quieroz , kwathi uPitso Mosimane walala isibili esivumelwaneni , " kusho umthombo uqinisekisa ukuthi uzokwethulwa kwelisombulukayo umqeqeshi .
Isolezwe ngeSonto lingakuveza ukuthi babalelwa ku - 200 abaqeqeshi abavela kuwo wonke amagumbi omhlaba , abafake izicelo zalo msebenzi onzima .
Kusuke ku - 100 kwayiwa ku - 60 ngokusho komthombo , kwase kuyiwa kwabahlanu .
Obekuseqhulwini kobekufunwa ngamava omqeqeshi , wukuthi uke walifaka yini izwe emiqhudelwaneni emikhulu , abe negama elimisa ithemba lokuthi uzofika angene emjahweni , angalokhu ekhala ngesikhathi futhi abe namava emidlalweni yamazwe ngamazwe .
Ebuzwa ngakho konke lokhu uDominic Chimhavi okhulumela iSafa , uthe : " Mnewethu mina angihlali kwiNEC , ngizifanela nawe .
Kanginalo ulwaizi kuze kube nginikwa isitatimende okufanele ngisithumele kwabezindaba .
Ngeke ngikuphikise kukho konke okushoyo kodwa asethembe ukuthi ubuholi sebuyikhombile insizwa ethenjiwe , " kusho uChimhavi .
Lize lashona elayizolo engasalubambi ucingo uMotlanthe , kanjalo nezinye izikhulu ezisesigungwini esiphezulu .
Enye into ekhomba uQuieroz ngokuthi kubukeka kuzobekwa phambi abadlali be - Under 23 abaya kuma - Olympics eJapan kwazise baphethe isithunzi seVision 2022 kanti sebejwayelene .
IBaroka isibheke ukuqeda kwiTop 8
INTATHELI YESOLEZWEIBAROKA FC seyizolwela ukuqeda emaqenjini ayisishiyagalombili aphezulu kwiDStv Premiership .
Lokhu kuzethemba komqeqeshi weBaroka , uThoka Matsemela , kugqame ngemuva kokuqeda umgqigqo waMaZulu FC abeseqhube imidlalo ewu - 16 engayazi induku kwiligi .
IBakgaga ibuyisele Usuthu kwamhlaba ilwehlula ngo - 1 - 0 wegoli likaRichard Mbulu ngoLwesibili eKing Zwelithini Stadium , eMlaza .
" Bekuwumdlalo onzima kodwa ngincoma abafana , basebenze ngokuzikhandla .
Ngicabanga ukuthi siwahlelele kahle AmaZulu .
Iqhinga lethu lokubavimba bangakwazi ukudlala ibhola emuva lisebenze kahle .
Ngiyabajabulela abadlali ngendlela abadlale ngayo .
Ngibonga nethimba labaqeqeshi .
Siwajabulela kakhulu la maphuzu amathathu , " kusho uMatsemela .
Amaphuzu amathathu anyusele ezikaMatsemela endaweni yesishiyagalolunye kwi - log ( ngaphambi kwemidlalo yayizolo ) .
IBaroka isiqoqe amaphuzu awu - 32 emidlalweni ewu - 27 .
Emdlalweni wabo olandelayo bazobhekana nomkhaya , iTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila , ngoLwesibili ePeter Mokaba Stadium ngo - 3 ntambama .
" ITshakhuma ngomunye umdlalo onzima .
Kumele siqinisekise ukuthi kukhona esikutholayo , ikakhulukazi amaphuzu amathathu ukuze sizosondela kwiTop 8 .
Ukushaya iqembu elisefomini njengaMaZulu , ebeseliqhube imidlalo ewu - 16 lingashaywa kodwa sakwazi ukulibamba , kuyasikhuthaza .
" Eminye imidlalo esele yeBaroka kukhona owe - Orlando Pirates ekhaya bese ivala isizini neSwallows ekuhambeni ngoJuni 5 .
Amanye amaqembu aselwela ukuqeda kwiTop 8 ehambisana nokudlala kwiMTN 8 ngesizini ezayo kukhona iKaizer Chiefs , TS Galaxy , Cape Town City neBloemfontein Celtic .
UMcCarthy upiklela abebemngabaza eqashwa wuSuthu
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUMQEQESHI waMaZulu , uBenni McCarthy , upiklela ababethi uzohluleka ukufeza iphupho likamengameli woSuthu , uSandile Zungu lokusonga iDStv Premiership lusemaqenjini amane aphezulu .
Usuku lwangoLwesithathu balusonge begcwele ukumamatheka abalandeli boSuthu olumabheshu ankone nezakhamuzi zaKwaZulu - Natal .
Luqinisekise ukuthi ngesizini ka - 2021 / 22 luzobe lubhukuda nezingwenya kwiCaf Champions League .
Le ngqophamlando yenzeke ngokucoboshisa iSwallows ngo - 1 - 0 , wephenathi eshaywe nguTapelo Xoki , osohlwini lwabadlali abagaqele umklomelo wokuba yisitobha esiye savelela kwisizini ka - 2020 / 21 .
Ngala maphuzu amathathu , luqinisekise ukuthi akekho osazolususa kweyesibili .
Lunamaphuzu awu - 53 , emidlalweni ewu - 29 .
I - Orlando Pirates elele isithathu , noma ingawunqoba owokugcina , ezowudlala neTshakhuma kusasa , izogcina iphelela emaphuzwini angu - 52 .
" Ngiyazi ukuthi sisalelwe wumdlalo wokugcina kodwa sikufezile ebesiphupha ngakho .
Sizuze obekungalindelwe muntu .
Ngesikhathi umengameli waMaZulu ethi ufuna iqembu liqede iligi likwiTop 4 , abantu bathi uyahlanya .
Ngesifanayo nakimi , ngifika , abantu bathi uZungu udlala ngemali yakhe , uthenga igama nje .
Ngixoshiwe kwiCape Town City , kangiyena umqeqeshi wezinga eliphezulu .
Ngaleyo ndlela ngizohluleka ukufeza phupho lakhe .
Esengifuna ukukwazi wukuthi njengamanje wubani ohleka yedwa , " kusho uMcCarthy esonga izandla , waqhiyama .
AMaZulu kawagcinanga ngokuqopha umlando wokuzibekela indawo kwiChampions League , abe yiqembu lesibili ukushaya iSwallows kwiligi .
UMcCarthy uqhube wathi akazi ukuthi angakuchaza kanjani ukujabula anakho .
Uthe uyazi ukuthi kukhona abese bebangabaza ngenxa yokuhlulwa yiBaroka nePirates emidlalweni edlule .
" Uma sekuphele imidlalo ewu - 16 ungahlulwa , ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uzoqhuzuka .
Izimbangi zizokwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi zikwenzela umsebenzi ube lukhuni .
Ingqwele ihlulelwa ngokuthi ivuke izithintithe .
Lokho sikwenzile ngokushaya iSwallows engenye yamaqembu anzima .
Ukudlala kwayo ngokulingana kwengu - 19 , sifike sakuqeda .
Besinalo ithuba lokushaya amanye amagoli , kodwa siyalimukela leli esinqobe ngalo , lisifake kwiChampions League .
" Kusasa uSuthu luzovala nomkhaya balo , iMaritzburg United abazobe belwela ukuvika ukuya emidlalweni yokuhlunga .
I - United isendaweni ka - 13 ngamaphuzu awu - 29 .
Ngesizini ka - 2014 / 15 , la maqembu abhekana kowokugcina .
Sekuyindaba endala ukuthi iTeam of Choice yashovela ehlathini omkhaya bayo , ibashaya ngo - 2 - 1 , kowawuseMoses Mabhida Stadium .
UMngqithi ufuna abadlali bakhe bafunde ngephutha lezitha
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEOMUNYE wabaqeqeshi beMamelodi Sundowns , uManqoba " TV " Mngqithi , uthi abadlali bakhe kumele bathole isifundo esenzweni sesitobha seCR Belouizdad esibe nesandla ekuhlulweni kwaleli qembu ngembudlu yamagoli .
Ngempelasonto iSundowns inqobe umdlalo wesibili weCaf Champions League , ibhaxabula ngo - 5 - 1 , iBelouizdad yase - Algeria , emdlalweni obuseBenjamin Mkapa National Stadium , eTanzania .
EzaseChloorkop zinqobe ngamagoli amabili kaThemba " Mshishi " Zwane , Peter Shalulile , Lebohang Maboe noKermit Erasmus .
Kowokuqala zashaya i - Al Hilal ngo - 2 - 0 .
KowangeSonto , igoli lokuqala kube iphenathi eshaywe uZwane .
Idaleke ngokuthi isitobha seBelouizdad , uChouhaib Keddad , sibambe ibhola ngesandla , engasabonwa ezintini unozinti uGaya Merbali .
Unompempe , uBoubou Traore , akacucuzanga , uyibeke emlotheni wabe esekhipha uKeddad ngekhadi elibomvu .
UMgqithi obambisene noRhulani Mokwena noSteve Komphela ekucijeni iSundowns , uthe ukholelwa ukuthi ukube uKeddad ulivumelile igoli , wangalivimba ngesandla , ngabe ezakhe zibuyile emdlalweni .
Uthe bebeze emdlalweni inhloso wukuhlasela ngamandla , bacindezele izitha okuyokhona abakwenzile .
" Kumele ngikusho nokuthi sisizwe nawukuthi bathole ikhadi elibomvu umdlalo usaphansi .
Engifisa ukuthi abadlali bami bafunde kukho ngoba ngikholwa wukuthi ukube lo mdlali wabo wasemuva ulivumelile igoli bebezoqhubeka nesibalo esifanele ( sabadlali ) , babe nethuba lokulwa , babuye emdlalweni , " kusho uMngqithi .
Ngokwamazwi alo mqeqeshi kubukeka konke kubavunile eTanzania .
Lo mdlalo kwakumele ube emasontweni amabili edlule e - Algeria , izikhulu zakuleliya lizwe zavimba iSundowns ukuya khona , kubekwa isizathu " sezempilo .
" " Siye kulo mdlalo sazi ukuthi sizobhekana neqembu elinzima .
Okusijabulisile ukuthi kwenzeke konke ebesikuhlelile , sibafake ingcindezi zisuka bagcina sebenza amaphutha .
" Siphinde salekelelwa iphutha lokuphuma zisuka kwesitobha ngekhadi elibomvu .
Kodwa esiwombeni sokuqala kusingene ekhanda lokho sangalwela ukubagqobhoza kodwa silibele wukugcina ibhola .
Sikulungisile lokho nethimba lami labaqeqeshi esikhathini sekhefu .
Ngibonga kakhulu kubona nakubacwaningi bethu abasisize kakhulu siya esiwombeni sesibili .
Kusithokozisile ukunqoba ngalesi sibalo samagoli .
" ISundowns ibambe indawo yokuqala kuGroup B weChampions League ngamaphuzu ayisithupha .
Umdlalo olandelayo ungoMgqibelo lapho izobe ibhekene neTP Mazembe yaseCongo ngo - 3 ntambama ekuhambeni .
IDowns yenze okwehlule iBafana eSudan
UKUBE kuyashintshwana ngemiphumela , iMamelodi Sundowns ibingawudlulisela kwiBafana Bafana umphumela ewuthole idlala ngokulingana ngo 0 - 0 ne - Al - Hilal Omdurman , eSudan nokusho ukulahla amaphuzu okokuqala ngqa kweyamaqoqo eCaf Champions League ka - 2020 / 2021 .
IBafana ingene ehlazweni ngesonto eledlule ihluleka wukungena kweyamanqamu e - 2022 Africa Cup of Nations eseCameroon ngoJanuwari , emuva kokuvumela ukunenebulwa yiSudan ngo 2 - 0 kuleliya lizwe .
Iqembu lakuleli liye emdlalweni lidinga iphuzu kuphela kanti abekhona amathemba emuva kokunqoba ngo 2 - 0 emlenzeni wokuqala lapha ekhaya .
ISundowns yanqoba ngo 2 - 0 emlenzeni wokuqala eTshwane , kanti isayinqobe yonke imidlalo yayo kwiGroup B nokuyibeka emaphuzwini angu - 13 , okusho ukuthi ibisivele izifakile esigabeni sama - quarterfinal .
I - Omdurman isendaweni yesithathu ngemuva kweBelouizdad yase - Algeria , ekweyesibili ngamaphuzu ayisithupha .
Yize kungasho lutho ukulahla amaphuzu eSudan kweSundowns , kwazise isivele iqedile ngeyamaqoqo kodwa izimbangi zayo kwiDStv Premiership zizomincela ukuthi kutolike njengokubohla kwefomu , eziye ekhefini lemidlalo yeFederation of International Football Association zishaya ngayo .
ISundowns evikela isicoco , yiyo yodwa engakehlulwa emidlalweni yeDStv Premiership kule sizini .
Ukungadlali kweyeligi kule mpelasonto kusho ukuthi izobuya ngoLwesibili neTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ePeter Mokaba Stadium , ePolokwane , isele ngemidlalo emithathu ezimbangini zayo .
ISundowns iqhwakelele esicongweni selog ngamaphuzu angu - 40 kanti kwabayijaha eduze kubalwa izimbangi ezingajwayelekile ngasesicongweni , iLamontville Golden Arrows naMaZulu FC .
Kukhona ne - Orlando Pirates , ebuyela enkundleni neMaritzburg United ngoLwesithathu .
Endaweni yesithathu ngemuva kweSundowns , ikhona neSuperSport United ubuholi bayo obulokhu buyiphike njalo imibiko ethi leli qembu liyadayisa .
Ukungathembeli kubadlali beSundowns yize yenza kahle kwiligi nasemidlalwemi yeligi , ngenye yezinto ezilethele obengumqeqeshi weBafana , uMolefi Ntseki , ukugxekwa ngokubhacaza kweqembu lakhe .
ISundowns isesethubeni lezicoco ezintathu kule sizini kwazise ngaphezu kweligi neChampions League , kusekhona neNedbank Cup ezohlangana kuma - quarterfinal ayo nePirates ngo - Ephreli 15 eLoftus .
Kushubile kowesicoco seGladAfrica Championship
STHEMBISO NGOBESEKULINDELEKE ukuba nangale mpelasonto uqhubeke nokushuba umbango wokunqoba isicoco seGladAfrica Championship nowokuvika izembe emaqenjini agijima kulesi sigaba esiphakela eseDStv Premiership .
Njengoba imidlalo yeGladAfrica isiya ngasemaphethelweni kwazise sekusele imidlalo engaphansi kweyishumi , wonke amaqembu asedlalela ukufa nokuphila njengoba enezinhloso ezingafani .
Phezulu kwi - log ugingqigongqo kumaqembu asembangweni weqhulu , iRichards Bay FC neSekhukhune United abalokhu beshintshana ngokuhlula kule ndawo .
Kuzoyiwa emidlalweni yangempelasonto iBay iqhwakele ngamaphuzu awu - 38 emidlalweni ewu - 22 .
I - United iyalandela kweyesibili ngawu - 36 emidlalweni ewu - 23 .
Phakathi nesonto womabili la maqembu ahlulekile ukuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele .
INatal Rich Boyz iguqiswe ngo - 2 - 1 yiFree State Stars kungalindele muntu eMhlathuze Sports Complex .
ISekhukhune sona sihlulekile ukubuya namaphuzu agcwele sibambana ngo - 1 - 1 neTS Sporting , Kabokweni Stadium , eMpumalanga .
Kulawo alandela ngemuva embangweni , i - JDR Stars neRoyal AM nabo abangazibekile phansi embangweni wesicoco njengoba bekwazile ukuthola amaphuzu amathathu kweyabo imidlalo .
IJDR neRoyal AM sebeyalingana ngamaphuzu awu - 36 ne - United , sebehlukaniswe amagoli endaweni yesithathu neyesine .
Amaqembu aphezulu kuleli sigaba abanga ukudla ubhedu bese ethola ithikithi eliya ngqo esigabeni esikhulu iDStv Premiership .
Abazohlulwa yilokhu bazokhalela kwindawo yesibili neyesithathu ukuze badlale emidlalweni yokuhlungela ukukhuphukela phezulu .
Nasemsileni we - log izinto zishubile njengoba kubalekelwa ukwehlela kwi - ABC Motsepe League .
IBizana Pondo Chiefs eqeqeshwa nguClinton Larsen yiyona esabambe ibhuleki emsileni ngamaphuzu angu - 16 , iCape Town Spurs isendaweni ka - 15 ngamaphuzu angu - 23 .
Kusasa , la maqembu azongqubuzana ngo - 3 ntambama eParow Park Stadium , eKapa .
ICape Town All Stars esendaweni ka - 13 neSteenberg United esendaweni ka - 14 bobabili basabambene ngamaphuzu angu - 24 .
Ngale mpelasonto , umdlalo ozokube ubhekwe kakhulu kwiGladAfrica ophakathi kwabakhaya iBay noThongathi FC .
Umdlalo ukusasa ngo - 3 ntambama ePrincess Magogo Stadium , KwaMashu .
Kuzokube kungowamagqubu njengoba ngesikhathi egcina ukuhlangana la maqembu emzuliswaneni wokuqala , iBay ecijwa nguSimo " Govuza " Dladla yanqoba ngo - 2 - 1 kumaCane Cutters aphekwa nguPitso Dladla , emdlalweni owawuseMhlathuze .
Akungabazeki ukuthi iBay izofuna ukuvuka ngomkhaya bayo lapha ukuze iqhubeke nokuhlala esicongweni .
UThongathi lona luzokuya kulo mdlalo luhambela phezulu njengoba lusanda kubuya namaphuzu agcwele kulandela ukuqumba phansi kwalo ngo - 3 - 2 i - All Stars emdlalweni obuseKapa .
Imidlalo yeGladAfrica Championship ngempelasonto : Namuhla : Ngo - 3:00 PM : Cape United v Royal AM ( Parow Park ) .
Kusasa : Ngo - 3:00 PM : Cape Town Spurs v Pondo Chiefs ( Parow Park ) ; Uthongathi FC v Richards Bay ( Princess Magogo ) ; Free State Stars v JDR Stars ( Goble Park ) ; TS Sporting v University of Pretoria ( Kabokweni Stadium ) .
NgeSonto : Ngo - 3:00 PM : Polokwane City v Cape Town All Stars ( Old Peter Mokaba ) ; Sekhukhune United v Jomo Cosmos ( Makhulong Stadium ) .
USeema uzimisele ngokufunda kuPapic oqashwe iLeopards
LIPHUMILE iqhina embizeni ngenhloso yeBlack Leopards ngomqeqeshi uKosta Papic obekuphikwa ukuthi uzothatha isikhundla sikaLehlohonolo Seema .
UPapic ujoyine iLeopards ngesonto eledlule , kwathiwa uzoba yinhloko yabaqeqeshi , engamele umsebenzi kaSeema , Morgan Shivhambu noMongezi Bobe .
Nokho emuva komdlalo neLamontville Golden Arrows eThekwini , iLidoda Duvha ewuwinile , uSeema udalule ukuthi uPapic ulinde ukuthola imvume yokusebenza kuleli ukuze abajoyine ebhentshini njengomqeqeshi .
" Umqeqeshi uPapic ufikile , sisebenza kamnandi naye .
Ngiyazi njalo ukuthi uma siqeqesha iqembu ngiba seduze kwakhe , sikhulume .
Uma ubheka namuhla ( ngoLwesibili ) , akashintshanga lutho .
Kodwa uma esethole amaphepha akhe , uzoshintsha ezindaweni ezithize .
Ngiyajabula ukuba naye lapha .
Akukho ukudideka ( ngemisebenzi yethu ) .
Uzoba ngumqeqeshi , uzosihola sinoMorgan futhi kufanele sifunde kuyena .
Asibhekile ukuba ngabaqeqeshi okwamanje .
Sidinga ukufunda , senze isiqiniseko sokuthi iBlack Leopards ithola amaphuzu ukuze sisuke lapho esikhona , " kusho uSeema .
Indaba yokuthi uPapic uzogudluza uSeema iphikwe nayisikhulu uChief Thidiela , sathi siyazi ukuthi eMzansi uma kuqashwa inhloko yabaqeqeshi bonke abantu bacabanga ukuthi kukhona ozosuswa esikhundleni kodwa kubona akunjalo .
UPapic ukhuza ibuya kwiLeopards ayiqeqesha ngesizini ka - 2014 / 2015 .
Emuva kokumenyezelwa kuleli qembu , ubuziwe ukuthi uzozibambela yini ejimini .
Uphendule wathi : " Hhayi okwamanje .
Kodwa ngesikhathi esizayo lokho kuzokwenzeka uma konke kuhamba kahle .
" UPapic nethimba lakhe kufanele baqhamuke neqhinga lokuhlula AmaZulu abazobhekana nawo emdlalweni we - Last 16 yeNedbank Cup eThohoyandou Stadium , ngoMgqibelo ngo - 3 ntambama .
" Sizobhekana nomdlalo ngamunye .
Sesiside isikhathi ( sagcina ukuwina ) .
Indlela esizizwa ngayo , umoya esinawo ( kuhle ) .
Nginesiqiniseko sokuthi akudingi sibatshele abadlali ukuthi sesidlulile ebunzimeni .
Bayazizwela bona .
Sebeyazi ukuthi kunjani ukuwina imidlalo , " kusho uSeema .
Mayelana nomdlalo naMaZulu uthe : " Sizodlala neqembu elinzima futhi .
Iqembu elihle .
Anginaso isiqiniseko sokuthi ukhona lapha obekholwa ukuthi sizophuma namaphuzu agcwele ngaphandle kwethu .
Sisenako lokho kukholwa njengoba sibheke kulo mdlalo wangoMgqibelo .
Kufanele siqhubeke sidlale ngoba asikho isikhathi sokuziqeqesha kwazise imidlalo isondelene .
Ngebhadi umqeqeshi kufanele ababone emdlalweni abanye abadlali .
Ngakho kufanele sizame ukudlulela emzuliswaneni olandelayo wale ndebe ukuze sidlale imidlalo eminingi ezosisiza ukulungisa lapho kudingeka khona . "
IChiefs isakuthola kunzima ukungena kwiTop 8
Intatheli yeSolezweIKAIZER Chiefs ihlulekile wukungena kwiTop 8 yeDStv Premiership ngemuva kokubanjwa yiBaroka FC emdlalweni weDStv Premiership ogcine uphele ngo 1 - 1 ngoLwesine ntambama ePeter Mokaba Stadium , eLimpopo .
Amakhosi abedinga ukunqoba ukuze akwazi ukungena kumaqembu ayisishiyagalombili aphezulu kwi - log kodwa ngenxa yalo mphumela asahleli endaweni yesishiyagalolunye ngamaphuzu awu - 25 .
Lona bekuwumdlalo wesibili kulandelana ehluleka wukuthola amaphuzu agcwele .
Kodlule ashayana aze abukana neStellenbosch FC umdlalo uphela ngo 2 - 2 .
Agcina ukunqoba ngo 1 - 0 kwiligi ehlula i - Orlando Pirates .
Nakuwona lo mdlalo iChiefs bekungathi izogcina inqobe ngalo igoli elilodwa njengoba ibibekwe phambili uLebo Manyama esiwombeni sesibili .
Nokho ngemuva kokucindezela kweBaroka , leli qembu lasekhaya ligcine lilitholile igoli lokulinganisa elibekwe enethini u - Evidence Makgopa .
IChiefs ayizange ibe nesizini enhle kwiPremier Soccer League njengoba ihlulekile wukuthatha iMTN 8 neNedbank Cup , idonsa ngodizili nakwiligi .
Isilwela ukuthi okungenani ukuqeda kwiTop 8 nokuzoyinika indawo kwiMTN 8 ngesizini ezayo .
Kulo mdlalo iBaroka iyona eqale yathi ukuphatha umdlalo kodwa kungekho okutheni okuthusa u - Itumeleng Khune emapalini eChiefs .
Kunalokho ngemuva kwemizuzu ewu - 10 kuqale umdlalo umgadli weChiefs uSamir Nurkovic udlaliswe kabi ebhokisini kodwa unompempe uVelaphi Sicelo wangakubona lokho njengephenathi .
EzikaHunt ziqhubekile nokuhlasela kodwa kwangalunga kwaze kwayiwa ekhefini .
. Esiwombeni sesibili , iChiefs ithole igoli ngomzuzu - 58 ngemuva kwebhola elihle alifakelwe uKhama Billiat ngesithende .
IBaroka iqhubekile nokuhlasela iphindelela .
Ngomzuzu ka - 81 uMakgopa ushayele iBaroka igoli lokulinganisa emuva kwebhola eligotshwe kwesokudla .
Libuyile ithemba kumaProteas ezenzela kwiWest Indies
XOLILE MPISANEUmshwibi wamaProteas , uKagiso Rabada , ubona lizokhuphuka izinga lokuzethemba kumaProteas emva kokuhlula iWest Indies kalula emdlalweni wokuqala wochungechunge lwama - test .
AmaProteas anqobe lo mdlalo , obuseDarren Sammy Cricket Ground , nge - innings eyodwa nama - run awu - 63 ngempelasonto .
I - West Indies ikhishwe isashaye ama - run awu - 97 kwi - innings yokuqala , yashaya awu - 162 kweyesibili .
AmaProteas abhethe kanye ahlanganisa ama - run awu - 322 .
URabada uthathe iwikhethi eyodwa kwi - innings yokuqala , wabuya esevutha kweyesibili , ethatha amahlanu .
Ubeqala ukwenza lokhu kusukela ngo - 2018 Mashi .
" Kulo mdlalo uyaye ukale imisebenzi yakho ngokushaya ama - run awu - 100 uma ubhetha noma ukuthatha amawikhethi amahlanu noma awu - 10 uma uwumshwibi , " kusho uRabada .
" Yikona osuke uzimisele ngako njalo uma ungena enkundleni .
Ngiyazi besekudlule isikhathi eside ngihluleka ukukwenza kodwa ngiyajabula ukuthi sekwenzekile .
" Iyona ndlela oqhathanisa ngayo ukuthi udlale kanjani nokuthi uzilungiselele ngendlela efanele yini .
Ubani ongeke ajabule uma enze into encomekayo ?
Ngiyaziqhenya kakhulu ngendlela engisebenze ngayo , " kusho yena .
AmaProteas abeqala ukuwina umdlalo we - test ekuhambeni kusukela ngo - 2017 .
Adinga ukungahlulwa kwi - test yesibili ukuze alunqobe lolu chungechunge .
" Siseyiqembu elisha futhi sisakha .
Uma ubheka abadlali abanamava okuthenjelwe kubona , abakhulile kangako ngokweminyaka , " kuchaza uRabada .
" Ngingazibala mina noma uQuinny ( De Kock ) .
U - Dean ( Elgar ) nguyena osemnkantshubovu , mina ngineminyaka ewu - 26 kodwa kusho lukhulu ukuthi ngibalwa nomakadebona kuleli qembu .
" Ukunqoba lo mdlalo wokuqala kuzosinika umdlandla esizowusebenzisa kolandelayo neminye esizoyidlala kule minyaka ezayo .
Ngeke sizikhukhumeze kodwa sizothatha konke okuhle esikwenzile , siqhubeke nokusebenza ngokuzikhandla .
" Kweminye imidlalo esihlulwe kuyona besizigwaza ngowethu ngokuthi sibuye silehlise izinga , umdlalo ugcine usiphunyukile .
Kulo mdlalo ( esiwudlale neWest Indies ) besilokhu sihamba ngegiya eliphezulu .
Siyazi ngeke kube lula kolandelayo kodwa okubalulekile ukuthi siqhubeke nezinga eliphezulu .
" Umdlalo wesibili uzoqala ngoLwesihlanu ntambama ngo - 4 , nawo uzodlalelwa eDarren Sammy Cricket Ground .
Kubuye ukuzethemba kwabeChiefs iqhubeka nokunqoba
IKAIZER Chiefs ibheke ukuqhubeka nomgqigqo wokucosha amaphuzu uma isibhekene neStellenbosch emdlalweni weDStv Premiership eFNB Stadium , eNasrec , namuhla ngo - 5 ntambama .
Ngempelasonto edlule , iChiefs ihlule iWydad Casablanca yaseMorocco ngo 1 - 0 emdlalweni wamaqoqo weCaf Champions League ingasaphelele enkundleni emuva kokuthola amakhadi abomvu kukaDaniel Akpeyi noSamir Nurkovic .
Ngaphambi kwalokho yayihlule i - Orlando Pirates koweDStv Premiership .
Kuyona yomibili le midlalo , Amakhosi awangenelwanga yigoli .
Lokhu akubuzwa ukuthi kubuyisa ithemba kubalandeli bayo abafisa okungenani iqede kwi - Top 8 ekupheleni kwesizini ukuze idlale kwiMTN 8 ngezayo .
Umgadli uLazalous Kambole ubona ukuhlangana kwezinto kwenyusa ukuzethemba eqenjini .
" Bekuwumdlalo onzima ( neWydad ) ngoba sidlale singasaphelele okwenze sashintsha indlela esidlala ngayo .
Kudingeke simise izinto ngenye indlela ngokomdlalo .
Kodwa okubalulekile ukuthi siwinile .
Iqembu lidlale kahle kakhulu , " kusho uKambole .
" Kuzoba wumdlalo ohluke kakhulu neStellenbosch kodwa sizowenza umsebenzi wokuyicubungula siyiKaizer Chiefs .
Okufanele sikwenze nje wukuzinikela ngokuphelele , senze isiqiniseko sokuthi siqoqa amaphuzu agcwele .
Indlela esiyiyona , singehlula noma yiliphi iqembu uma sigxilisa imiqondo yethu .
Njengoba sidlalela ekhaya neStellenbosch , sinethuba elikhulu lokuwina .
Bayiqembu elihle elihlala lizimisela ikakhulukazi uma lidlala neChiefs .
" Amakhosi asethubeni lokuzibekisela indawo kuma - quarterfinal eChampions League okokuqala emlandweni wawo .
Kudingeka ngoMgqibelo ekuhambeni ahlule iHoroya AC yaseGuinea emdlalweni wokugcina wamaqoqo ukuze ajoyine iWydad kwi - Last 8 .
Nokho kungayifaka engozini iChiefs ukudlala neStellies isicabanga ngoweChampions League .
Umqeqeshi weStellenbosch , uSteve Barker , ukholwa wukuthi beangawacosha amaphuzu agcwele kwiChiefs .
" Sizodlala neChiefs ekuhambeni isaphuma ekutholeni imiphumela emihle .
Isidlale imidlalo emibili ingangenelwa yigoli .
Ihlule iPirates neCasablanca .
Kodwa ngibona ukuthi siyiqembu sesikhule kakhulu futhi sinyukelwe wukuzethemba .
Singehlula noma yiliphi iqembu noma yinini inqobo nje uma sizinikela futhi siqhubeka nokukholwa ukuthi singayiwina yonke imidlalo esiyidlalayo .
Siyethemba ukuthi sizodlala kahle , sizibeke ethubeni lokuwaqoqa womathathu amaphuzu , " kusho uBarker .
Ngempelasonto , iChiefs izomela iNingizimu Afrika kwiChampions League ihambisana neMamelodi Sundowns ebambane ngo 0 - 0 ne - Al Hilal yaseSudan .
ISundowns , esivele idlulele kuma - quarterfinal , izovala neCR Belouizdad yase - Algeria ngoLwesihlanu ePitoli .
IPirates , edlale ngokulingana ngo 0 - 0 ne - Al Ahly Benghazi kweyamaqoqo eCaf Confederation Cup , izophinda nayo ngeSonto ngo - 6 ntambama e - Orlando Stadium .
Imidlalo yeDStv Premiership NamuhlaNgo - 3:00 PM - Tshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila v Mamelodi Sundowns ( Peter Mokaba Stadium ) .
Ngo - 5:00 PM - Kaizer Chiefs v Stellenbosch ( FNB Stadium ) .
USuthu selubheke ukubambelela kweyesibili kwi - log
STHEMBISO NGOBESEUKAPUTENI waMaZulu FC , uMbongeni " Shoes " Gumede , uthi bazimisele ukubambelela endaweni yesibili kwi - log yeDStv Premiership kuze kusongwe isizini .
Ngaphansi kukaBenni McCarthy , ongumqeqeshi , Usuthu ludlala ingcwenga yebhola njengoba luvulela isibhaxu kwamanye amaqembu .
Lokhu kufakazelwa wukuhlala kwalo endaweni yesibili ngamaphuzu angu - 50 emidlalweni engu - 27 .
Ngaphambi kokuba ezikaMandlakazi zibuyiselwe kwamhlaba ngempelasonto edlule yiBaroka FC , eziguqise ngo - 1 - 0 eKing Zwelithini Stadium , eMlaza , bese zidlale imidlalo yeligi engu - 16 zingayazi induku .
Ekhuluma neSolezwe uGumede , oyisiqongqwane sasemuva oSuthwini , uthe ukuhlulwa kwabo yiBaroka akwehlanga kahle kubona kodwa wathembisa ukuthi bazovuka bazithathe .
" Angifuni ukuqamba amanga , akwehlanga kahle ukuhlulwa kwethu yiBaroka ngemuva kwesikhathi eside singehlulwa , ngaphezu kwalokho besidlalela ekhaya .
" Kodwa - ke ukwehlulwa yiBaroka sesikudlulisile sesibheke imidlalo yethu yokugcina elandelayo .
Nakuba kungeke kube yinto elula ukuyenza kodwa kuzomele nakanjani siyinqobe ukuze sizoqeda isizini sihlezi endaweni yesibili kwi - log , " usho kanje uGumede owafika oSuthwini ngo - 2015 esuka kwi - Orlando Pirates .
Lo mdlali , odabuka eMlaza , uthe kungabajabulisa kakhulu ukuyodlala kwiCaf Champions League .
Amaqembu aqeda endaweni yokuqala neyesibili kwi - log adlala kulo mqhudelwano .
" Nakuba singafuni ukuzifakela ingcindezi ngemidlalo yeCaf kodwa nathi singaMaZulu siyafisa ukuzibona sikulo mqhudelwano .
Lokhu kungalinyusa kakhulu igama leqembu futhi kusize nabadlali beqembu ekutheni bathole isipiliyoni sokuyodlala emidlalweni yeCaf .
" Umdlalo olandelayo weligi waMaZulu uzokuba ngonzima kakhulu njengoba ezobhekana ne - Orlando Pirates ngoMeyi 27 e - Orlando Stadium , eSoweto .
" Kuhlale kunzima ngaso sonke isikhathi ukubhekana namaqembu amakhulu ngakho - ke nakulo mdlalo wethu nePirates sibheke ukuthi ube ngonzima kakhulu .
Kodwa sizokwenza ngakho konke okusemandleni ethu ukuthi sibuya nomphumela osivunayo , " kusho uGumede .
Egcina ukuhlangana la maqembu emzuliswaneni wokuqala weligi , abambana ngo 1 - 1 eJonsson Kings Park Stadium , eThekwini .
IDowns ivule igebe kwi - log ishaya iStellies , iBay yawasha ijezi
IMAMELODI Sundowns iqhubekile nokuvula igebe esicongweni se - log yeDStv Premiership ishaya iStellenbosch FC ngo 2 - 1 emdlalweni obuseDanie Craven Stadium , eStellenbosch , izolo ntambama .
IStellenbosch yiso esibone inethi kuqala inethi ngonyawo lukaStanley Dimgba ngesiwombe sokuqala ngomzuzu ka - 33 , kwathi elokulinganisa leSundowns lashaywa wuGaston Sirino ngesiwombe sesibili , ngomzuzu ka - 51 .
Kanti elokunqoba leDowns lavalelwa phakathi wuPeter Shalulile ngomzuzu ka - 90 .
Ukunqoba kweSundowns umdlalo kusho ukuqhubeka kwayo nokuvula igebe esicongweni se - log yePremiership .
Njengamanje isinamaphuzu angu - 39 emidlalweni engu - 17 , ilandelwa yiGolden Arrows ngawu - 35 emidlalweni engu - 19 .
AmaSandawane asasele emuva ngemidlalo emibili , ngenxa yokuxinwa kwawo yimidlalo yeCaf Champions League .
NgoLwesibili leli qembu lasePitoli lizobuyela kweyeChampions League ngokududulana neTP Mazembe eLoftus Versfeld , ePitoli , ngo - 6 kusihlwa .
Khonamanjalo iChippa United izibekisele indawo kuma - semifinal eNedbank Cup okwesithathu , emlandweni wayo emuva kokuhlula iRichards Bay FC ngo 2 - 1emdlalweni we - quarterfinal obuseSisa Dukashe Stadium , eMdantsane izolo ntambama .
Amagoli eChippa ashaywe ngo - Anthony Laffor noRamasimong Maloisane .
EleBay elishaywe nguSiyabonga Vilane obekungelesithathu lakhe kulo qhudelwano ka - 2021 .
ULaffor ubeshaya igoli lokuqala kusukela ewelele kwiChippa ngoJanuwari .
IChippa ifinyelele kuma - semifinal ngo - 2017 nango - 2019 .
Kuyiwa emdlalweni wayizolo uSimo Dladla , ocija iBay , akakufihlanga ukuthi yize sebekuma - quarterfinal kodwa into emqoka kubo wukwenyukela kwiDStv Premiership .
Nangempela uphumuze ezinye izethenjwa , okubalwa kuzo nokaputeni wezakhe , uSiphamandla Mtolo .
IBay ibuyela enkundleni ngoLwesithathu nePretoria Callies kanti iChippa ithembe umphumela wayizolo ukuthi uyivuse uma isibuyela neSwallows ngoMgqibelo .
Imidlalo namuhla : Cape Town All Stars v Pretoria Callies , eDanie Craven ngo - 3 ; Black Leopards v Tshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila , eThohoyandou ngo - 6 .
Umqeqeshi ucacisa ngezilomo kuRante noLebese
UMQEQESHI weTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila , uMpho Maleka , ucacisa ngezilomo zakhe uTokelo Ranite ozakhele ugazi kwi - Orlando Pirates noGeorge Lebese odume kwiKaizer Chiefs .
URantie ufike kwiTshakhuma ekuqaleni kwesizini ngemuva kwesikhathi eside izinto zingamhambeli kahle echithwa amaqembu okubalwa kuwo iCape Town City neMamelodi Sundowns .
Lokho kwenze akangashesha ukungena egiyeni kodwa uMaleka uthi useyaqala ukuba wumshini .
NgoTokelo kufanele sibonge umlolongi wemiziba ( fitness trainer ) ngokuthi kade elokhu emuphusha , emkhuthaza ukuthi akhiphe amangwevu akhe , " kusho uMaleka .
" Nguye obemfuna ukuthi enze okungaphezu kwabezicabangela khona .
Nokumdlalisa kwethu imizuzu ethe xaxa ( engaphezu kuka - 80 behlula iTS Galaxy koweligi ngo - Ephreli 10 ) yize bekuhambisana nezinhlelo zethu kodwa bekuncike nasekuzinikeleni .
Siyakubonga ukunikela akukhombisile .
Sethemba ukuthi uzoqhubeka asinikeze okungaphezulu .
" Okumqoka wukuthi ube ngaseqenjini elinqobile ngokwakha igoli .
Njengomgadli siyazi ukuthi uma ungayibonswanga inethi uke uhalele ukuthi noma - ke usungakhela ozakwenu .
Ngilangazelele ukuthi lokho kumkhuthaze enze okuthe xaxa emdlalweni olandelayo .
KwiTshakhuma uRantie kulindelwe abuyise ithalente lakhe ebeselicwila kungaqondakali ukuthi kubangwa yini .
Empeleni ngemuva kokuganwa eminyakeni edlule uRantie uvele wacwila waphenduka neqaqa emaqenjini aphesheya kwazise uqale ukugqama khona .
Uficwa yisinyama nje uke waba semabhukwini eFC Bournemouth inyukela kwi - English Premier League .
Nokho ugcine esethutheleka naseTurkey kwaya walahlekelwa nayindawo yakhe kwiBafana Bafana abebukeka enekusasa eliqhakazile kuyo .
Esinye isilomo okulindelwe lukhulu kuso kwiTshakhuma nguLebese yena izinto eziqale ukumbhedela esekwiChiefs esolwa ngokuvilapha .
Bekulindelwe ukuthi afike avuke ngaphansi kukaPitso Mosimane kwiSundowns kodwa kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya wabolekiswa kwiSuperSport United .
Ugcine evumbuka e - USA kodwa kuthe izinto zisamhambela kahle , kwafika iCovid - 19 yavala imingcele nokuholele ekutheni aze afike kwiTTM .
" UGeorge silindele ukuthi abekhona emidlalweni esemthethweni esontweni noma amabili ezayo , " kusho uMaleka .
" Naye njengoba ngike ngasho ngoTK ( Tokelo ) usebenza kakhulu nomlolongi womzimba ukuze abuyele egiyeni lokudlala .
Ngokomqondo kodwa uyambambona ukuthi usekulungele . "
Injabulo iligi yabesifazane ithola abaxhasi
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEINKAKHA yeBanyana Banyana , uPortia Modise , ithi kufana nokuphenduleka kwemithandazo yeminyaka ukuthola uxhaso kwebhola labesifazane .
Izolo inhlangano eyengamele ibhola kuleli , iSouth African Football Association ( Safa ) , yethule iHollywoodbets njengabaxhasi beligi kazwelonke yabesifazane esizokwaziwa ngeHollywoodbets Super League .
Empeleni lezi zindaba zizwakale ngempelasonto edlule kodwa iSafa yanquma ukuzethulela abezindaba izolo .
Umengameli wale nhlangano , uDanny Jordaan , umemezele ukuthi iHollywoodbets ixhase le ligi ngo - R17 million esivumelwaneni sesizini eyodwa .
Iqembu elizoba ngompetha lizoklonyeliswa u - R2 million , isibili sithole isigidi samarandi .
Kuvele nokuthi wonke amaqembu ayingxenye yale ligi azothola u - R150 000 .
Ezinye izindaba ezijabulisile ngezithi umdlali ozoqokwa njengovelele ekupheleleni kwesizini uzokhala emuke no - R50 0 .
UModise , owaqokwa ngo - 2006 njengomdlali ovelele kwiWomen's African Football Championship , uthe wethemba ukuthi ukungena kweHollywoodbets kuzoheha nabanye abaxhasi .
Le nsephe , eyayingalibheki ipali , kade yayikusho ukuthi ibhola labesifazane kuleli lizokhula kuphela uma izinkampani zifaka imali .
" Sekuphele isikhathi eside sizama ukuthi elakuleli libe neligi kazwelonke yabesifazane , yezinga eliphezulu .
Ukuqala kokungena kwabaxhasi kusho ukuthuthuka kwebhola labesifazane .
Ngesikhathi iqalwa le ligi ngesizini edlule , bekunzima kakhulu kubanikazi bamaqembu ngenxa yokuswela imali yokuhambela imidlalo .
Bazoke baphumule abanikazi bamaqembu .
" Okwenza ngicele nezinye izinkampani ukuthi zixhase ukuthi ekugcineni lezi zingane kumele zondle imindeni yazo ngokudlala ibhola .
Kakungafani nezikhathi zethu lapho esasiphuma kwesinye isikhathi singaphethe lutho , " kubeka uModise owaba ngowokuqala kuleli zwekazi ukushaya amagoli awu - 100 eqenjini lesizwe .
Uveze nokuthi unethemba lokuthi iHollywoodbets akhona amalungelo ezowathenga okusakazwa kwale ligi eziteshini ezinkulu zikamabonakude kuleli .
" Ngithanda ukubonga iSABC ngokusakaza ibhola labesifazane ngezimpelasonto .
Nokho kakwanele , ngesikhathi iba miningi imidlalo esakazwayo , bazosondela nabanye abaxhasi .
Lokhu kuzophinde kudayise abadlali bethu emaqenjini ase - Europe .
Ngicela nokuthi iHollywoodbets neSafa babambisane ekumaketheni le ligi ezinkundleni zokuxhumana , " kusho uModise .
U - Jordaan uthe lolu xhaso luzolekelela abanikazi bamaqembu ekuthuthukiseni ibhola labesifazane kuleli .
" Sijabule kakhulu ngalolu xhaso , luzoshintsha okuningi .
Lokhu kusho ukuthi iSafa iyaqhubeka nokubeka ibhola labesifazane ezingeni lomhlaba .
Ngikhuluma nje sinabadlali abawu - 32 abenza kahle kumaligi ase - Europe , " kusho uJordaan .
Umqeqeshi weBanyana , uDesiree Ellis , uthe lolu xhaso luzokwenza ube lula umsebenzi wokuqoka abadlali bamaqembu esizwe .
UZuma uzimisele ngokulwela indawo kwiChiefs
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUMDLALI weKaizer Chiefs uDumisani Zuma okungacaci kahle ngekusasa lakhe kuleli qembu , uthandazela ukuthi aqhubeke nebhola alidlale koweCaf Champions League uma sebebhekene neCape Town City .
IChiefs izokwamukela iCity emdlalweni weDStv Premiership namuhla ngo - 5 ntambama .
Emidlalweni ewu - 21 yeDStv Premiership esadlalwe iChiefs , uZuma oyibamba ohlangothini lwesokudla , usafakwe kweyisishiyagalombili kuphela .
Wagcina ukudlala kwiligi ngoJanuwari , ezakhe zishaywa i - Orlando Pirates ngo - 2 - 1 .
Kawukho nowodwa umdlalo awuqedile , nowePirates akawudlalanga wonke .
Ngesikhathi iChiefs idlala neHoroya AC koweChampions League wangena sekusele imizuzu ewu - 25 .
Wafika wawushintsha umdlalo , Amakhosi akwazi ukubuya umdlalo wagcina uphela ngo 2 - 2 .
Mhlawumbe uma engaqhubeka nokwenza kahle uma enikwe ithuba lokho kungamakhela ugazi kumqeqeshi uGavin Hunt okubhekwe ayakhe kabusha iChiefs ngesizini ezayo .
" Kangilimele nakancane , engilwa nako ukulwela ukuba sesimeni esihle sokudlala .
Okuhle ukuthi manje ngihlale ngineqembu , ngiziqeqesha nalo .
Konke kuzolunga ngokushesha .
Ukuzethemba kwami kubuye kakhulu , ukungena ngisize iqembu ukudlulela kuma - quarterfinal eChampions League kwenze omkhulu umehluko .
Isifiso sami ukuqhubeka nendlela engigcine ukudlala ngayo , " kubeka uZuma .
IChiefs iya emdlalweni weCity iphuma ekudlaleni ngokulingana neBaroka ngo 1 - 1 .
Kwi - log isendaweni yesishiyagalolunye , ngamaphuzu awu - 25 , emidlalweni ewu - 21 .
Yagcina ukunqoba kwilog ngenyanga edlule ishaya iPirates ngo 1 - 0 .
AmaCitizens acijwa uJan Olde Riekerink , akweyesikhombisa , ngamaphuzu awu - 30 , emuva kwemidlalo ewu - 22 .
Kumaqembu akwi - Top 8 , iwona asangenelwe amagoli amaningi , awu - 29 .
Asevalele enethini awu - 33 .
Kufanele ukuthi ezikaRiekerink zizoya kowaMakhosi zethemba ukuqhubeka nezikwenze kwiSuperSport United eziyibhaxabule ngo - 3 - 0 .
" Umdlalo wethu neCity uzoba nzima kakhulu .
Emidlalweni edlule yenze kahle kakhulu .
Nangesikhakhi siyishaya emlenzeni wokuqala yayinzima ngendlela eyisimanga .
Empeleni njengoba sezibheke ngasekupheleni kweligi , yonke imidlalo izoba nzima .
Singabadlali siyazi ukuthi iqembu likwesiphi isimo , kusiphoqa ukunqoba emdlalweni ngamunye , " kuqhuba uZuma .
URiekerink uthe ufisa sengathi bangaqhubeka nomgqigqo abawutshengisile bedlala neSuperSport .
" Uma singaqhubeka naleli phupho esinalo , neChiefs singayishaya .
Siyazi ukuthi izitha zethu ziyiqembu elikhulu , elinomlando , elinesikwati esiqinile futhi elidlala kwiChampions League .
Lifuna nokungena kwi - Top 8 , kuzoba umdlalo wamaqembu anentshisekelo yokunqoba .
Nathi sinesikwati esihle , wonke amasosha ami azobe ephelele , " kusho uRiekerink .
Ukhonjwa kuMaZulu oweMaritzburg United
SIBUSISO MDLALOSEISIKHWISHIKHWISHI somdlali wasophondweni lwesokunxele kwiMarizburg United , uMxolisi " Jomo " Kunene , sesingumdlali waMaZulu FC ngemuva kokusayiniswa yileli qembu elisembhidlangweni wokuqinisa isikwati salo ukulungisela isizini ka - 2021 / 2022 .
Ngokusho komthombo weSolezwe ngeSonto osondelene nomdlali , AmaZulu aseqede konke noKunene , osekusele wukuthi ethulwe ngokusemthethweni ekuqaleni kukaJulayi nabanye abadlali abasha abasayiniswe yaye eqenjini " UKunene usesayinile kuMaZulu .
Lokho ngingakuqinisekisa .
Osekusele nje manje wukuthi kuphele le nyanga kaJuni bese emenyezelwa ngokusemthethweni nabanye abadlali asebesayiniswe ngaMaZulu nalabo okulindeleke basayine ingakapheli le nyanga .
Yize esevele esayinile uKunene , kodwa okwenza kungabi lula ukuthi kumenyezelwe wukuthi inkontileka yakhe neMaritzburg iphela ekupheleni kukaJuni .
Empeleni uKunene akayedwa osuka kwiMaritzburg United , kodwa bakhona nabanye abadlali abambalwa abasuka kwiMaritzburg abazobonakala kuMaZulu okusaxoxwa nabo , " kusho umthombo .
UKunene ukhonjwa kuMaZulu nabanye ozakwabo nje , vele itshe limi ngothi kwiMaritzburg United okubikwa ukuthi iyadayiswa .
Usihlalo weTeam of Choice , uphumele obala kuleli sonto ngezinhloso zakhe zokufaka iqembu endalini ekhala ngezindleko nezikweleti abhekene nazo ekuliphatheni iqembu .
Ngaphandle kukaKunene , ngokuthola kwaleli phephandaba abanye abadlali beqembu laseMgungundlovu , abangase bavumbuke oSuthwini maduze kubalwa uKwanda Mngonyama noThabiso Kutumela , oke wayamaniswa neMamelodi Sundowns neKaizer Chiefs .
Imenenja yakhe , uVasili Barbis , weGlobal Finest Athletes , ivumile ukuthi lo mdlali usesayine inkontileka nelinye iqembu kodwa wala waphetha ukudalula iqembu asayine kulo .
" Ngeke ngikwazi ukusho okwamanje ukuthi iliphi iqembu ayakulona uKunene , kodwa ngingakuqinisekisa ukuthi sesiyisayinile inkontileka .
Ngicela uphinde ungithinte ngoJulayi 1 , ngizobe sengikwazi ukukutshela igama leqembu , " kusho uBarbis .
UKunene ( 29 ) , odabuka eNyanyadu , eDannhauser , wubengomunye wabadlali abamqoka beMaritzburg abesemabhukwini ayo amasizini amane .
Ukuya kwakhe kuMaZulu kufaniswa nokubuyela ekhaya kwendodana yolahleko , kwazise leli nxele likhuliswe ezinhlakeni zoSuthu ngaphambi kokujoyina iSwallows FC ebisadlala kwiNational First Division ( GladAfrica Championship ) , asuke kuyo waya kwiBaroka FC isizini eyodwa ngaphambi kokuya eMphithi .
UBrilliant Mkhathini , obhekene nezokuxhumana kuMaZulu uthe : " Njengamanje asikakhulumi ngabadlali kuze kube yisikhathi esifanele kanti nabaphathi abakasho lutho ngezindaba zabadlali .
UNcikazi uzolwa nenkinga yokugeja kwi - Arrows
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEUFUNA kulungiswe inkinga yokugeja kwiLamontville Golden Arrows umqeqeshi waleli qembu uMandla Ncikazi .
UNcikazi ukusho lokhu ngemuva kokudedela amaphuzu agcwele bebanjelwa ekhaya yiBloemfontein Celtic emdlalweni weDStv Premiership ophele ngo - 1 - 1 eSugar Ray Xulu Stadium , ngempelasonto edlule .
Ukungawini kwaBafana Bes'thende kubalahlekisele ngethuba lokubuyela endaweni yesibili kwi - log njengoba sebehleli kweyesithathu .
Indawo yesibili ithathwe AmaZulu FC anqobe iStellenbosch bese kuqhwakela iMamelodi Sundowns .
UNcikazi obebonakala ephoxekile ngemuva komdlalo , uthe akajabhisiwe indlela abafana bakhe abadlale ngayo , uphoxwe ukuyeka kwabo inqwaba yamathuba .
" Siyeke inqwaba yamathuba , kumele ukube lo mdlalo siwunqobile .
Sizolwa nayo le nto yokuba buthuntu phambi kwamapali .
Kangisoli muntu , kumele sizigxeke sonke .
Mayelana nokudlala , abadlali bami badlale kahle uma kuqhathaniswa nomdlalo odlule ( weSwallows ) .
Akusenani , leli phuzu lizokwengeza kokufunwa ukuzuzwa iqembu , lingcono iphuzu kunokwehlulwa , " kubeka uNcikazi .
Ngomdlalo weSiwelele bekungowesithathu i - Arrows idlala ngokulingana kulandelana .
Ibambane neCape Town City neSwallows .
Yagcina ukunqoba ekuqaleni kukaMashi ishaya iTshakhuma ngo - 2 - 1 .
Ngo - Ephreli 21 , ezikaNcikazi zizovakashela iSuperSport United , eMasterpieces Moripe Stadium koqala u - 5 ntambama .
Amatsatsantsa a Pitori aphuma esibhaxwini esivuthayo sika - 3 - 0 asithole kumaCitizens ngeledlule .
Kwi - log yeDStv Premiership aya ngokwehla njengoba esesendaweni yesithupha ngamaphuzu awu - 35 , emidlalweni ewu - 22 .
Ake abalwa namaqembu amathathu phezulu .
NoJohn Maduka ocija iCeltic ukhale ngamathuba ayekwe abafana bakhe .
" Lo mdlalo kumele ukube siwunqobe ngenqwaba yamagoli .
Ukungasebenzisi amathuba kusiphuce amaphuzu amabili wonke .
Siye kulo mdlalo sazi ukuthi i - Arrows idlala ibhola elifana nelethu .
Besiyivumela ize kithina bese siyayizuma .
Yingakho sithole amathuba amaningi .
Sizoqhubeka nokusebenza kanzima kuze kube iyalunga indaba yokushaya amagoli , " kusho uMaduka .
ICeltic izodlala neSwallows ngo - Ephreli 20 eSeisa Ramabodu Stadium ngo - 5 ntambama .
EzikaMaduka zisendaweni yeshumi ngamaphuzu awu - 24 , emidlalweni ewu - 22 .
Umdlali weGalaxy ubona bengena kwiTop 8
STHEMBISO NGOBESEISIKHWISHIKHWISHI somdlali weTS Galaxy , uLindokuhle Mbatha , sibona besethubeni elihle lokubalwa namanye amaqembu eDStv Premiership azoqeda isizini ka - 2020 / 2021 ekwiTop 8 nokuhambisana nokudlala emqhudelwaneni weMTN 8 ngesizini ezayo .
UMbatha odabuka Osizweni , eNewcastle , ukhuluma kanje , kamuva nje iGalaxy eqeqeshwa ngu - Owen Da Gama , ikhombisa ukuba sefomini enhle kakhulu njengoba ilokhu iqhubekile nokuvulela isibhaxu kwamanye amaqembu agijima kwiligi .
Emidlalweni emihlanu yakamuva , amaRockets awakahlulwa .
Anqobe iBloemfontein Celtic ngo 1 - 0 , iBlack Leopards ngo 3 - 1 , abuye ephula irekhodi leSwallows FC lokungahlulwa eyicoboshisa ngo 2 - 1 .
Emidlalweni emibili leli qembu likaTim Sukazi lidlale ngokulingana ngo 0 - 0 neSupersport United nango 1 - 1 neChippa United .
Njengamanje iGalaxy ihlezi endaweni yesikhombisa kwi - log ngamaphuzu angu - 26 emidlalweni engu - 19 .
UMbatha uthe lokhu kungenxa yokuzikhandla kwabo bengabadlali kanti nokufika kukaDa Gama othathe izintambo kuDan " Dance " Malesela osekwiChilli Boyz , kwenze umehluko omkhulu .
" Isizini asiyiqalanga neze kahle kwazise imiphumela emihle ibigqoza , kodwa - ke siyajabula ukuthi manje sesiqalile ukuwina imidlalo ilandelana nokuyinto ebingenzeki phambilini .
Nakuba ngingathandi ukuqhathanisa abaqeqeshi kodwa ngingasho ukuthi ukufika kukaDa Gama kwenze kwaba nomehluko omkhulu eqenjini .
Ngaphezu kwalokho ufikele kubadlali iningi labo alaziyo njengoba kade esiqeqesha kwiHighlands Park ngesizini edlule , nokuyinto eyenza ukuba umsebenzi wakhe nowethu singabadlali ube lula kakhulu uma sesisenkundleni , " kusho uMbatha owayegijima kwiPlatinum Stars nakwiMamelodi Sundowns .
Lo mdlali ogijimisa okwenyamazane ezinhlangothini uqhube wathi : " Njengoba sesiqalile ukunqoba imidlalo ngibona lokhu kusibeka ethubeni elihle kakhulu lokuthi siqede isizini sikwi - Top 8 , kodwa - ke uma sifuna ukwenza lokho kumele siqhubeke nokusebenza kanzima ukuze sifeze leli phupho .
" NgoMgqibelo iGalaxy izobuyela enkundleni izobhekana neMariztburg United emdlalweni weligi ngo - 5 ntambama eMbombela Stadium , eNelspruit .
Akungabazeki nakancane ukuthi lo mdlalo uzobe ungowamagqubu kwazise ngesikhathi egcina ukuhlangana la maqembu emzuliswaneni wokuqala , iGalaxy yabukisa ngeTeam of Choice iyibhudluza ngo 3 - 0 eHarry Gwala Stadium , eMgungundlovu .
I - United nayo iwadinga egcwele amaphuzu kwazise ibalekela izembe .
Ibambe indawo ka - 14 kwi - log ngamaphuzu awu - 14 emidlalweni ewu - 18 .
UJele uyayethemba iPirates kweyeCaf
UKAPUTENI we - Orlando Pirates , uHappy Jele , ubona isikwati abanaso singakuphinda okweminyaka edlule emqhudelwaneni weCAF Confederation Cup .
IPirates izokwamukela i - Enyimba FC yaseNigeria emdlalweni wesibili wesigaba samaqoqo kaGroup A ozoba se - Orlando Stadium namuhla ngo - 6 ntambama .
Emdlalweni wokuvula esigabeni samaqoqo , iPirates idlale ngokulingana ngo 1 - 1 ne - ES Setif yase - Algeria .
UJele , okunguyena kuphela osele eqenjini elafinyelela kowamanqamu weConfederation Cup ngo - 2015 beqeqeshwa ngu - Eric Tinkler , uthe isikwati abanaso kulokhu singakuphinda lokho .
Abafana bakaTinkler bahlulwa yi - Etoile du Sahel yaseTunisia kowamanqamu .
" Kuningi okufanayo phakathi kwaleli qembu nelango - 2015 elafinyelela kowamanqamu .
Indlela esidlala ngayo nabadlali esinabo .
Siyasizana , siyalekelelana .
Kungenzeka sithubeleze sifinyelele kowamanqamu , siyiwine indebe .
Sinesikwati esihle .
Esikudingayo manje yimiphumela , " kusho uJele .
Isikwati sikaTinkler sasithakwe ngabadlali okukhona kubona uLucky Lekgwathi , Sifiso Myeni , Thandani Ntshumayelo , Ayanda Gcaba , Kermit Erasmus nabanye .
IPirates isendaweni yesibili kuGroup A ngephuzu kanye neSetif .
Emsileni kuhlezi i - Al Ahly Benghazi yaseLibya .
Eqhulwini kuhlezi i - Enyimba ehlule iBenghazi kowokuvula .
" Amalungiselelo ahambe kahle .
Sithole iphuzu ekuhambeni .
Siyazi ukuthi kubalulekile ukuwina ekhaya .
Siyicwaningile i - Enyimba .
Siyazi ukuthi iyiqembu eliyingozi .
Siyazi futhi lapho ibuthaka khona .
Kufanele sisebenze kanzima ukuze siwine kusasa ( namuhla ) .
Njengoba sengike ngadlala kwiCaf , kuwumsebenzi wami ukuthi ngibacathulise nabanye .
Lo mqhudelwano ubalulekile kimina , ubalulekile naseqenjini .
IPirates iyiqembu elikhulu .
Ulwazi oluncane enginalo kufanele ngiludlulisele kwabanye ozakwethu , " kusho uJele .
Endleleni ebheke esigabeni samaqoqo , i - Enyimba igudluze iBloemfontein Celtic yaseNingizimu Afrika .
Asikapholi isilonda seBaroka kumdlali weChiefs
SITHEMBISO MKHIZEKALIVUMI ukuphela igqubu kumdlali weKaizer Chiefs , uNjabulo Blom lokubanjwa yiBaroka FC bagcina bephunyukwe isicoco seligi ngomdlalo wokugcina wesizini eyedlule .
La maqembu okuhlala kusiphuka isidindi uma etholene phezulu , namuhla azobhekana emzuliswaneni wesibili weDStv Premiership oqala ngo - 3 ntambama , ePeter Mokaba Stadium .
IChiefs eqeqeshwa uGavin Hunt , ihambela phezulu ngenxa yokungena okokuqala kuma - qaurterfinal eCaf Champions League .
Lokhu ikwenze ngokubambana ngo - 2 - 2 neHoroya yaseGuinea ekuhambeni ngempelasonto edlule .
Izoya kwiBaroka sekudlule imidlalo eyisikhombisa yagcina ukwehlulwa .
UBlom oyibamba esiswini kuMakhosi , uthe bayilindele iBaroka .
" Ngijatshuliswa yizinga eliphezulu lokuzethemba eqenjini .
Lokhu kudalwe imiphumela yakamuva .
Kuhlale kunzima ukudlala neBaroka , uma ngicabanga ngayo inhliziyo iba buhlungu .
Wonke umuntu wayibona ngesizini edlule isiphuca isicoco seligi .
Yebo , iSundowns ( Mamelodi ) eyagcina isithathile kodwa yiBaroka eyama endleleni yethu .
Siyakwazi esikulindele kuyo , akumele siyeye .
Siyazi ukuthi iyiqembu eligijima ngendlela eyisimanga futhi elisebenza ngokuzikhandla .
Sizokhipha konke esinako , " kusho uBlom .
Kuwafa wafa womdlalo wokugcina wesizini ka - 2019 / 20 , uManual Kambala washayela iBaroka igoli lokulinganisa kungasalindele muntu .
EleChiefs okwase kubhekwe ukuthi iChiefs izonqoba ngalo lashaywa nguKhama Billiat .
Bekungokwesibili iBakgaga ima endleleni yeChiefs .
Ngo - 2011 , isadlala kwi - ABC Motsepe League , yashaya Amakhosi ngo - 1 - 0 wegoli likaThobani Mncwango kuma - quarterfinal yeNedbank Cup .
Kule sizini , emlenzeni wokuqala , iChiefs yabambana neBaroka ngo - 1 - 1 koweligi .
EzikaHunt zasizwa umkhonto owagwaza ekhaya kaGoodman Mosele sewuyophela umdlalo .
Yize kulokhu iChiefs ingalweli isicoco seligi kodwa kusemqoba ukuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele njengoba ilwela ukungena kwiTop 8 .
Isaqoqe amaphuzu awu - 24 emidlalweni ewu - 20 okuyibeka endaweni yesishiyagalolunye .
Uma iBaroka inqoba izoyigudluza iChiefs endaweni ekuyo .
Njengamanje , ezikaThoka Matsemela zikweyeshumi nambili , ngamaphuzu awu - 23 , emidlalweni ewu - 21 .
UBlom onemidlalo ewu - 19 yeDStv Premiership , ubengekho kodlule weligi bebambana ngo - 2 - 2 neStellenbosch , ngenxa yamakhadi .
Uthe uyajabula ukubuyela kweyeligi .
" Kwangiphatha kabuhlungu ukungabibikho sidlala neStellenbosch .
Ayikho into engangizoyenza , ngase ngithole amakhadi amane .
Ukunqoba kwethu koweChampions League , eGuinea , emdlalweni obunzima ngendlela eyisimanga , ngikholelwa ukuthi nakho kuzosisiza koweBaroka .
IChampions League ihlukile , uma sidlala kuyo sisuke simele izwe , " kusho uBlom .
Liyayishonela iChiefs elwela ukuqeda kwiTop 8
ZAKHELE XABATshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ( 1 ) 2Kaizer Chiefs ( 0 ) 1LIYAYISHONELA iKaizer Chiefs ezabalazela ukungena kwiTop 8 njengoba iphinde yalahla amaphuzu ihlulwa yiTshakhuma Tsha Madzivhandila ( TTM ) emdlalweni weDStv Premiership ePeter Mokaba Stadium , ePolokwane , izolo ebusuku .
Igoli leChiefs lishaywe nguLebogang Manyama esiwombeni sesibili .
Awe - TTM abekwe enethini nguThabo Rakhale noThabo Mnyamana esiwombeni ngasinye .
Amakhosi angene enkundleni ebheke ukuqoqa amaphuzu agcwele kulandela ukubanjwa yiBloemfontein Celtic ngempelasonto edlule .
Kule sizini iChiefs ingena , iyaphuma kwi - Top 8 ngenxa yokuhluleka wukugcina umgqigqo .
Ukuhamba kwemidlalo iChiefs ihluleka ukucosha amaphuzu kusho ukungena engcupheni yokungayidlali iMTN 8 ekuqaleni kwesizini ezayo .
Amakhosi asalelwe yimidlalo emine ukuthi azame ukuzibekisela indawo kulo mqhudelwano .
Umdlalo weTTM neChiefs , bekungowokuqala womqeqeshi uDylan Kerr esebhentshini kulandela ukulunga kwemvume yakhe yokusebenza eMzansi emahoreni ambalwa ngaphambi kokuqala komdlalo .
Izolo , iChiefs ikhombise ukuwuphatha umdlalo usaqala kodwa ihluleka uma isifike phambili .
Emuva kwesikhathi eside onozinti bezipholele , uBruce Bvuma , obesemapalini eChiefs , uchilizele ngaphandle ishodi likaMnyamana ngomzuzu ka - 22 .
Ngoka - 38 iChiefs ingene obishini uNjabulo Blom ethola ikhadi eliphuzi lesibili emuva kokudonsa uNdabayithethwa Ndlondlo ngaphandle kwebhokisi .
Leyo free - kick ishaywe nguMnyamana , yashaya ipali , yashayisa kuBvuma wayicosha .
Sekusele imizuzu emithathu , uRakhale ulibeke esifubeni , waqobela phakathi ibhola eligotshwe nguMnyamana kwesokudla .
Esiwombeni sesibili , iChiefs ibuye yazama ukucindezela kodwa iTTM ibikhombisa ukuba yingozi uma ithola ibhola .
Unozinti weTTM , uWashington Arubi , ugcine ekutholile azokwenza echithela phezu kwepali ibhola elingqofwe nguSamir Nurkovic ngomzuzu ka - 51 .
Ngomzuzu ka - 65 unompempe uVictor Hlungwane unikeze iChiefs iphenathi emuva kokuthi u - Ayanda Nkili edlalise kabi uNurkovic ebhokisini .
Ishaywe nguManyama kodwa wayibamba u - Arubi .
UManyama uyilandelile , wamjika , wayiqobela phakathi .
Sekubalwa imizuzwana kuphele umdlalo , uHlungwane uyikhombe emlotheni emuva kokuthi uSiyabonga Ngezana ebambe ibhola ngesandla ebhokisini .
Ishaywe phakathi nguMnyamanaEmdlalweni olandelayo , iTTM ebalekela izembe izobhekana neChippa United kowamanqamu weNedbank Cup eFree State Stadium ngoMgqibelo ngo - 6 ntambama .
Ngokunqoba lapha inyukele endaweni ka - 14 ngamaphuzu awu - 25 .
IChiefs sekuzomele iyozama ukulwela amaphuzu agcwele uma isidlala neSwallows ngoLwesithathu oluzayo .
Ngalolu suku iTTM izobe idlala neSuperSport United .
UMotsepe ukhuculula insila eqaqele kwiCaf
INDLALA yemidlalo yeBafana Bafana kuthelevishini emidlalweni yasekuhambeni sekuzoba into endala uma kungukuthi imizamo kamengameli weConfederation of African Football ( Caf ) , uPatrice Motsepe , iyaphumelela .
UMotsepe owayevele ethembise izinguquko ezinqala ngesikhathi esakhankasela ukhetho , ukhiphe isitatimende ngeSonto lapho enaba khona ngemihlangano eyahlukahlukene nezinhlaka ezahlukene kunobhutshuzwayo wase - Afrika abelokhu ehlangana nazo .
Uqale ukwenza lokhu kusukela eqokiwe ngenhloso yokwenza ibhola lase - Afrika lihehe kwabakwamanye amazwekazi , liphinde lizakhele lona inzuzo ukuze kuzokwanda abaxhasi .
Kuningi okungenzeki ngendlela okuqashelwe wuMotsepe nethimba lakhe njengoba bebelokhu bengena bephuma emihlanganweni nabaxhasi ( bakhona nalaba abafisa ukufaka isandla ) , izikhulu zohulumeni kanjalo nomengameli .
NgokukaMotsepe , ubuholi obudlule bebuphethe ngendlela engagculisi okufakazelwa yindlela umhlaba wonke oyibuka ngayo iCaf .
Ukungaphathwa ngendlela ethembekile kwemali okuhambisana nokungabi - nabo abaphathi abaqotho , ngezinye zezizathu uMotsepe nethimba lakhe , bebone kungcono balande i - Price Waterhouse Coopers ( PWC ) ukuba izobasiza ngokuphenyisisa zonke izinkinga ebezibikwa phambilini ngeCaf .
Umbiko wesikhashana wePWC uveze ubugebengu obusabekayo obebenzeka ngaphambilini .
